paśya śaineya sainyāni dravamāṇāni saṃyuge
mahāntaṃ ca raṇe śabdaṃ dīryamāṇāṃ ca bhāratīm
dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ tāta vikṣiptaṃ savyasācinā
atyantāpacitaiḥ śūraiḥ phalgunaḥ paravīrahā
paśyaitad dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām anīkaṃ sudurāsadam
śṛṇu dundubhinirghoṣaṃ śaṅkhaśabdāṃś ca puṣkalān
siṃhanādaravāṃś caiva rathanemisvanāṃs tathā
nāgānāṃ śṛṇu śabdaṃ ca pattīnāṃ ca sahasraśaḥ
sādināṃ dravatāṃ caiva śṛṇu kampayatāṃ mahīm
purastāt saindhavānīkaṃ droṇānīkasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
tasmiṃś ca nihate yuddhe kathaṃ jīveta mādṛśaḥ
śyāmo yuvā guḍākeśo darśanīyaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
laghvastraś citrayodhī ca praviṣṭas tāta bhāratīm
tanna jānāmi vārṣṇeya yadi jīvati vā na vā
kurūṇāṃ cāpi tat sainyaṃ sāgarapratimaṃ mahat
eka eva ca bībhatsuḥ praviṣṭas tāta bhāratīm
aviṣahyāṃ mahābāhuḥ surair api mahāmṛdhe
pratyakṣaṃ te mahābāho yathāsau carati dvijaḥ
yugapac ca sametānāṃ kāryāṇāṃ tvaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ
nāhaṃ śocāmi dāśārhaṃ goptāraṃ jagataḥ prabhum
sa hi śakto raṇe tāta trīṃl lokān api saṃgatān
prajahyāt samare prāṇāṃs tasmād vindāmi kaśmalam
tasya tvaṃ padavīṃ gaccha gaccheyus tvādṛśā yathā
tādṛśasyedṛśe kāle mādṛśenābhicoditaḥ
raṇe vṛṣṇipravīrāṇāṃ dvāv evātirathau smṛtau
pradyumnaś ca mahābāhus tvaṃ ca sātvata viśrutaḥ
astre nārāyaṇasamaḥ saṃkarṣaṇasamo bale
vīratāyāṃ naravyāghra dhanaṃjayasamo hy asi
tat tvāṃ yad abhivakṣyāmi tat kuruṣva mahābala
nānyathā tāṃ mahābāho saṃprakartum ihārhasi
parityajya priyān prāṇān raṇe vicara vīravat
na hi śaineya dāśārhā raṇe rakṣanti jīvitam
bhīrūṇām asatāṃ mārgo naiṣa dāśārhasevitaḥ
tavārjuno gurus tāta dharmātmā śinipuṃgava
vāsudevo guruś cāpi tava pārthasya dhīmataḥ
praviśaitad balaṃ tāta dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥ
praviśya ca yathānyāyaṃ saṃgamya ca mahārathaiḥ
yathārham ātmanaḥ karma raṇe sātvata darśaya
saṃjaya uvāca
prītiyuktaṃ ca hṛdyaṃ ca madhurākṣaram eva ca
kālayuktaṃ ca citraṃ ca svatayā cābhibhāṣitam
dharmarājasya tad vākyaṃ niśamya śinipuṃgavaḥ
sātyakir bharataśreṣṭha pratyuvāca yudhiṣṭhiram
evaṃvidhe tathā kāle madṛśaṃ prekṣya saṃmatam
na me dhanaṃjayasyārthe prāṇā rakṣyāḥ kathaṃ cana
kuśaly ahaṃ kuśalinaṃ samāsādya dhanaṃjayam
avaśyaṃ tu mayā sarvaṃ vijñāpyas tvaṃ narādhipa
dṛḍhaṃ tv abhiparīto 'ham arjunena punaḥ punaḥ
āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā yāvad dhanmi jayadratham
tvayi vāhaṃ mahābāho pradyumne vā mahārathe
jānīṣe hi raṇe droṇaṃ rabhasaṃ śreṣṭhasaṃmatam
pratijñā cāpi te nityaṃ śrutā droṇasya mādhava
śaktaś cāpi raṇe droṇo nigṛhītuṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
dharmarājaṃ yathā droṇo nigṛhṇīyād raṇe balāt
nigṛhīte naraśreṣṭhe bhāradvājena mādhava
evaṃ gate naraśreṣṭha pāṇḍave satyavādini
yadi droṇo raṇe kruddho nigṛhṇīyād yudhiṣṭhiram
jayārthaṃ ca yaśorthaṃ ca rakṣa rājānam āhave
sa bhavān mayi nikṣepo nikṣiptaḥ savyasācinā
bhāradvājād bhayaṃ nityaṃ paśyamānena te prabho
tasyāpi ca mahābāho nityaṃ paśyati saṃyuge
nānyaṃ hi pratiyoddhāraṃ raukmiṇeyād ṛte prabho
māṃ vāpi manyate yuddhe bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ
so 'haṃ saṃbhāvanāṃ caitām ācāryavacanaṃ ca tat
pṛṣṭhato notsahe kartuṃ tvāṃ vā tyaktuṃ mahīpate
ācāryo laghuhastatvād abhedyakavacāvṛtaḥ
upalabhya raṇe krīḍed yathā śakuninā śiśuḥ
yadi kārṣṇir dhanuṣpāṇir iha syān makaradhvajaḥ
tasmai tvāṃ visṛjeyaṃ vai sa tvāṃ rakṣed yathārjunaḥ
yaḥ pratīyād raṇe droṇaṃ yāvad gacchāmi pāṇḍavam
udīcyā dākṣiṇātyāś ca ye cānye 'pi mahārathāḥ
ye ca karṇamukhā rājan rathodārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
ete 'rjunasya kruddhasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
udyuktā pṛthivī sarvā sasurāsuramānuṣā
sarākṣasagaṇā rājan sakiṃnaramahoragā
jaṅgamāḥ sthāvaraiḥ sārdhaṃ nālaṃ pārthasya saṃyuge
evaṃ jñātvā mahārāja vyetu te bhīr dhanaṃjaye
yatra vīrau maheṣvāsau kṛṣṇau satyaparākramau
daivaṃ kṛtāstratāṃ yogam amarṣam api cāhave
kṛtajñatāṃ dayāṃ caiva bhrātus tvam anucintaya
droṇe citrāstratāṃ saṃkhye rājaṃs tvam anucintaya
ācāryo hi bhṛśaṃ rājan nigrahe tava gṛdhyati
pratijñām ātmano rakṣan satyāṃ kartuṃ ca bhārata
na hy ahaṃ tvā mahārāja anikṣipya mahāhave
dṛṣṭvā śreyaḥ paraṃ buddhyā tato rājan praśādhi mām
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
na tu me śudhyate bhāvaḥ śvetāśvaṃ prati māriṣa
kariṣye paramaṃ yatnam ātmano rakṣaṇaṃ prati
ātmasaṃrakṣaṇaṃ saṃkhye gamanaṃ cārjunaṃ prati
sa tvam ātiṣṭha yānāya yatra yāto dhanaṃjayaḥ
mamāpi rakṣaṇaṃ bhīmaḥ kariṣyati mahābalaḥ
pārṣataś ca sasodaryaḥ pārthivāś ca mahābalāḥ
draupadeyāś ca māṃ tāta rakṣiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
virāṭo drupadaś caiva śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
dhṛṣṭaketuś ca balavān kuntibhojaś ca māriṣa
nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayās tathā
ete samāhitās tāta rakṣiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
samāsādayituṃ śakto na ca māṃ dharṣayiṣyati
dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca samare droṇaṃ kruddhaṃ paraṃtapaḥ
yatra sthāsyati saṃgrāme pārṣataḥ paravīrahā
eṣa droṇavināśāya samutpanno hutāśanāt
kavacī sa śarī khaḍgī dhanvī ca varabhūṣaṇaḥ
viśrabdho gaccha śaineya mā kārṣīr mayi saṃbhramam
dhṛṣṭadyumno raṇe kruddho droṇam āvārayiṣyati
saṃjaya uvāca
dharmarājasya tad vākyaṃ niśamya śinipuṃgavaḥ
pārthāc ca bhayam āśaṅkan parityāgān mahīpateḥ
apavādaṃ hy ātmanaś ca lokād rakṣan viśeṣataḥ
na māṃ bhīta iti brūyur āyāntaṃ phalgunaṃ prati
dharmarājam idaṃ vākyam abravīt puruṣarṣabha
kṛtāṃ cen manyase rakṣāṃ svasti te 'stu viśāṃ pate
anuyāsyāmi bībhatsuṃ kariṣye vacanaṃ tava
na hi me pāṇḍavāt kaś cit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate
tasyāhaṃ padavīṃ yāsye saṃdeśāt tava mānada
yathā hi me guror vākyaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ dvipadāṃ vara
tathā tavāpi vacanaṃ viśiṣṭataram eva me
priye hi tava vartete bhrātarau kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
tavājñāṃ śirasā gṛhya pāṇḍavārtham ahaṃ prabho
droṇānīkaṃ viśāmy eṣa kruddho jhaṣa ivārṇavam
tatra yāsyāmi yatrāsau rājan rājā jayadrathaḥ
yatra senāṃ samāśritya bhītas tiṣṭhati pāṇḍavāt
gupto rathavaraśreṣṭhair drauṇikarṇakṛpādibhiḥ
itas triyojanaṃ manye tam adhvānaṃ viśāṃ pate
āsaindhavavadhād rājan sudṛḍhenāntarātmanā
anādiṣṭas tu guruṇā ko nu yudhyeta mānavaḥ
ādiṣṭas tu tvayā rājan ko na yudhyeta mādṛśaḥ
abhijānāmi taṃ deśaṃ yatra yāsyāmy ahaṃ prabho
huḍaśaktigadāprāsakhaḍgacarmarṣṭitomaram
iṣvastravarasaṃbādhaṃ kṣobhayiṣye balārṇavam
yad etat kuñjarānīkaṃ sāhasram anupaśyasi
kulam añjanakaṃ nāma yatraite vīryaśālinaḥ
āsthitā bahubhir mlecchair yuddhaśauṇḍaiḥ prahāribhiḥ
nāgā meghanibhā rājan kṣaranta iva toyadāḥ
anyatra hi vadhād eṣāṃ nāsti rājan parājayaḥ
ete rukmarathā nāma rājaputrā mahārathāḥ
ratheṣv astreṣu nipuṇā nāgeṣu ca viśāṃ pate
dhanurvede gatāḥ pāraṃ muṣṭiyuddhe ca kovidāḥ
gadāyuddhaviśeṣajñā niyuddhakuśalās tathā
khaḍgapraharaṇe yuktāḥ saṃpāte cāsicarmaṇoḥ
śūrāś ca kṛtavidyāś ca spardhante ca parasparam
nityaṃ ca samare rājan vijigīṣanti mānavān
karṇena vijitā rājan duḥśāsanam anuvratāḥ
etāṃs tu vāsudevo 'pi rathodārān praśaṃsati
satataṃ priyakāmāś ca karṇasyaite vaśe sthitāḥ
tasyaiva vacanād rājan nivṛttāḥ śvetavāhanāt
te na kṣatā na ca śrāntā dṛḍhāvaraṇakārmukāḥ
madarthaṃ viṣṭhitā nūnaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt
prayāsyāmi tataḥ paścāt padavīṃ savyasācinaḥ
yāṃs tv etān aparān rājan nāgān saptaśatāni ca
prekṣase varmasaṃchannān kirātaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitān
kirātarājo yān prādād gṛhītaḥ savyasācinā
svalaṃkṛtāṃs tathā preṣyān icchañ jīvitam ātmanaḥ
āsann ete purā rājaṃs tava karmakarā dṛḍham
teṣām ete mahāmātrāḥ kirātā yuddhadurmadāḥ
hastiśikṣāvidaś caiva sarve caivāgniyonayaḥ
ete vinirjitāḥ sarve saṃgrāme savyasācinā
madartham adya saṃyattā duryodhanavaśānugāḥ
etān bhittvā śarai rājan kirātān yuddhadurmadān
ye tv ete sumahānāgā añjanasya kulodbhavāḥ
karkaśāś ca vinītāś ca prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥ
jāmbūnadamayaiḥ sarvair varmabhiḥ suvibhūṣitāḥ
labdhalakṣyā raṇe rājann airāvaṇasamā yudhi
uttarāt parvatād ete tīkṣṇair dasyubhir āsthitāḥ
karkaśaiḥ pravarair yodhaiḥ kārṣṇāyasatanucchadaiḥ
anekayonayaś cānye tathā mānuṣayonayaḥ
mlecchānāṃ pāpakartṝṇāṃ himavaddurgavāsinām
kṛpaṃ ca saumadattiṃ ca droṇaṃ ca rathināṃ varam
sindhurājaṃ tathā karṇam avamanyata pāṇḍavān
kṛtārtham atha cātmānaṃ manyate kālacoditaḥ
tena saṃbhāvitā nityaṃ paravīryopajīvinā
vināśam upayāsyanti maccharaughanipīḍitāḥ
ye tv ete rathino rājan dṛśyante kāñcanadhvajāḥ
ete durvāraṇā nāma kāmbojā yadi te śrutāḥ
śūrāś ca kṛtavidyāś ca dhanurvede ca niṣṭhitāḥ
saṃhatāś ca bhṛśaṃ hy ete anyonyasya hitaiṣiṇaḥ
akṣauhiṇyaś ca saṃrabdhā dhārtarāṣṭrasya bhārata
yattā madarthaṃ tiṣṭhanti kuruvīrābhirakṣitāḥ
apramattā mahārāja mām eva pratyupasthitāḥ
tāṃs tv ahaṃ pramathiṣyāmi tṛṇānīva hutāśanaḥ
tasmāt sarvān upāsaṅgān sarvopakaraṇāni ca
yathopadiṣṭam ācāryaiḥ kāryaḥ pañcaguṇo rathaḥ
kāmbojair hi sameṣyāmi kruddhair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
nānāśastrasamāvāpair vividhāyudhayodhibhiḥ
kirātaiś ca sameṣyāmi viṣakalpaiḥ prahāribhiḥ
lālitaiḥ satataṃ rājñā duryodhanahitaiṣibhiḥ
śakaiś cāpi sameṣyāmi śakratulyaparākramaiḥ
tasmād vai vājino mukhyā viśrāntāḥ śubhalakṣaṇāḥ
upāvṛttāś ca pītāś ca punar yujyantu me rathe
tasya sarvān upāsaṅgān sarvopakaraṇāni ca
rathe prāsthāpayad rājā śastrāṇi vividhāni ca
tatas tān sarvato muktvā sadaśvāṃś caturo janāḥ
rasavat pāyayām āsuḥ pānaṃ madasamīriṇam
pītopavṛttān snātāṃś ca jagdhānnān samalaṃkṛtān
vinītaśalyāṃs turagāṃś caturo hemamālinaḥ
tān yattān rukmavarṇābhān vinītāñ śīghragāminaḥ
pāṇḍurābhraprakāśābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛte
yojayām āsa vidhivad dhemabhāṇḍavibhūṣitān
dārukasyānujo bhrātā sūtas tasya priyaḥ sakhā
tataḥ snātaḥ śucir bhūtvā kṛtakautukamaṅgalaḥ
snātakānāṃ sahasrasya svarṇaniṣkān adāpayat
āśīrvādaiḥ pariṣvaktaḥ sātyakiḥ śrīmatāṃ varaḥ
tataḥ sa madhuparkārhaḥ pītvā kailāvataṃ madhu
ālabhya vīrakāṃsyaṃ ca harṣeṇa mahatānvitaḥ
dviguṇīkṛtatejā hi prajvalann iva pāvakaḥ
utsaṅge dhanur ādāya saśaraṃ rathināṃ varaḥ
kṛtasvastyayano vipraiḥ kavacī samalaṃkṛtaḥ
lājair gandhais tathā mālyaiḥ kanyābhiś cābhinanditaḥ
yudhiṣṭhirasya caraṇāv abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ
tatas te vājino hṛṣṭāḥ supuṣṭā vātaraṃhasaḥ
atha harṣaparītāṅgaḥ sātyakir bhīmam abravīt
tvaṃ bhīma rakṣa rājānam etat kāryatamaṃ hi te
āyatyāṃ ca tadātve ca śreyo rājño 'bhirakṣaṇam
jānīṣe mama vīryaṃ tvaṃ tava cāham ariṃdama
ahaṃ rājñaḥ kariṣyāmi rakṣāṃ puruṣasattama
evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca bhīmasenaṃ sa mādhavaḥ
nihate saindhave pāpe pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
pariṣvajiṣye rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
etāvad uktvā bhīmaṃ tu visṛjya ca mahāmanāḥ
saṃpraikṣat tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vyāghro mṛgagaṇān iva
taṃ dṛṣṭvā pravivikṣantaṃ sainyaṃ tava janādhipa
bhūya evābhavan mūḍhaṃ subhṛśaṃ cāpy akampata
tataḥ prayātaḥ sahasā sainyaṃ tava sa sātyakiḥ
didṛkṣur arjunaṃ rājan dharmarājasya śāsanāt
saṃjaya uvāca
dharmarājo mahārāja svenānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
prāyād droṇarathaprepsur yuyudhānasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
tataḥ pāñcālarājasya putraḥ samaradurmadaḥ
prākrośat pāṇḍavānīke vasudānaś ca pārthivaḥ
tataḥ śabdo mahān āsīd yuyudhānarathaṃ prati
sātvatena mahārāja śatadhābhivyadīryata
tasyāṃ vidīryamāṇāyāṃ śineḥ pautro mahārathaḥ
sapta vīrān maheṣvāsān agrānīke vyapothayat
te bhītā mṛdyamānāś ca pramṛṣṭā dīrghabāhunā
āyodhanaṃ jahur vīrā dṛṣṭvā tam atimānuṣam
rathair vimathitākṣaiś ca bhagnanīḍaiś ca māriṣa
anukarṣaiḥ patākābhiḥ śirastrāṇaiḥ sakāñcanaiḥ
bāhubhiś candanādigdhaiḥ sāṅgadaiś ca viśāṃ pate
ūrubhiḥ pṛthivī channā manujānāṃ narottama
śaśāṅkasaṃnikāśaiś ca vadanaiś cārukuṇḍalaiḥ
patitair vṛṣabhākṣāṇāṃ babhau bhārata medinī
gajaiś ca bahudhā chinnaiḥ śayānaiḥ parvatopamaiḥ
rarājātibhṛśaṃ bhūmir vikīrṇair iva parvataiḥ
gatasattvā mahīṃ prāpya pramṛṣṭā dīrghabāhunā
nānāvidhāni sainyāni tava hatvā tu sātvataḥ
praviṣṭas tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ drāvayitvā camūṃ bhṛśam
iyeṣa sātyakir gantuṃ tato droṇena vāritaḥ
bharadvājaṃ samāsādya yuyudhānas tu māriṣa
nābhyavartata saṃkruddho velām iva jalāśayaḥ
nivārya tu raṇe droṇo yuyudhānaṃ mahāratham
vivyādha niśitair bāṇaiḥ pañcabhir marmabhedibhiḥ
sātyakis tu raṇe droṇaṃ rājan vivyādha saptabhiḥ
hemapuṅkhaiḥ śilādhautaiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥ
taṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ sāyakair droṇaḥ sāśvayantāram ārdayat
sa taṃ na mamṛṣe droṇaṃ yuyudhāno mahārathaḥ
siṃhanādaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā droṇaṃ vivyādha sātyakiḥ
daśabhiḥ sāyakaiś cānyaiḥ ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhir eva ca
yuyudhānaḥ punar droṇaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
taṃ droṇaḥ sāśvayantāraṃ sarathadhvajam āśugaiḥ
tvaran prācchādayad bāṇaiḥ śalabhānām iva vrajaiḥ
tathaiva yuyudhāno 'pi droṇaṃ bahubhir āśugaiḥ
prācchādayad asaṃbhrāntas tato droṇa uvāca ha
tavācāryo raṇaṃ hitvā gataḥ kāpuruṣo yathā
yudhyamānaṃ hi māṃ hitvā pradakṣiṇam avartata
yadi māṃ tvaṃ raṇe hitvā na yāsy ācāryavad drutam
sātyakir uvāca
dhanaṃjayasya padavīṃ dharmarājasya śāsanāt
saṃjaya uvāca
etāvad uktvā śaineya ācāryaṃ parivarjayan
prayātaḥ sahasā rājan sārathiṃ cedam abravīt
droṇaḥ kariṣyate yatnaṃ sarvathā mama vāraṇe
yatto yāhi raṇe sūta śṛṇu cedaṃ vacaḥ param
etad ālokyate sainyam āvantyānāṃ mahāprabham
asyānantaratas tv etad dākṣiṇātyaṃ mahābalam
bāhlikābhyāśato yuktaṃ karṇasyāpi mahad balam
etad antaram āsādya codayāśvān prahṛṣṭavat
bāhlikā yatra dṛśyante nānāpraharaṇodyatāḥ
dākṣiṇātyāś ca bahavaḥ sūtaputrapurogamāḥ
hastyaśvarathasaṃbādhaṃ yac cānīkaṃ vilokyate
nānādeśasamutthaiś ca padātibhir adhiṣṭhitam
etāvad uktvā yantāraṃ brahmāṇaṃ parivarjayan
prāviśad bhāratīṃ senām aparyantāṃ sa sātyakiḥ
amarṣī kṛtavarmā tu sātyakiṃ paryavārayat
tam āpatantaṃ viśikhaiḥ ṣaḍbhir āhatya sātyakiḥ
caturbhiś caturo 'syāśvān ājaghānāśu vīryavān
tataḥ punaḥ ṣoḍaśabhir nataparvabhir āśugaiḥ
sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ pratyavidhyat stanāntare
sātvatena mahārāja kṛtavarmā na cakṣame
ākṛṣya rājann ākarṇād vivyādhorasi sātyakim
sa tasya dehāvaraṇaṃ bhittvā dehaṃ ca sāyakaḥ
sapatrapuṅkhaḥ pṛthivīṃ viveśa rudhirokṣitaḥ
samārgaṇaguṇaṃ rājan kṛtavarmā śarāsanam
tataḥ praśīrṇe dhanuṣi śaktyā śaktimatāṃ varaḥ
abhyahan dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
tato 'nyat sudṛḍhaṃ vīro dhanur ādāya sātyakiḥ
vyasṛjad viśikhāṃs tūrṇaṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
sarathaṃ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ samantāt paryavākirat
chādayitvā raṇe 'tyarthaṃ hārdikyaṃ tu sa sātyakiḥ
athāsya bhallena śiraḥ sāratheḥ samakṛntata
sa papāta hataḥ sūto hārdikyasya mahārathāt
sātyakiś cābhyagāt tasmāt sa tu bhīmam upādravat
yuyudhāno 'pi rājendra droṇānīkād viniḥsṛtaḥ
prayayau tvaritas tūrṇaṃ kāmbojānāṃ mahācamūm
sa tatra bahubhiḥ śūraiḥ saṃniruddho mahārathaiḥ
na cacāla tadā rājan sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
saṃdhāya ca camūṃ droṇo bhoje bhāraṃ niveśya ca
tathā tam anudhāvantaṃ yuyudhānasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
nyavārayanta saṃkruddhāḥ pāṇḍusainye bṛhattamāḥ
samāsādya tu hārdikyaṃ rathānāṃ pravaraṃ ratham
pāñcālā vigatotsāhā bhīmasenapurogamāḥ
vikramya vāritā rājan vīreṇa kṛtavarmaṇā
yatamānāṃs tu tān sarvān īṣad vigatacetasaḥ
abhitas tāñ śaraugheṇa klāntavāhān avārayat
nigṛhītās tu bhojena bhojānīkepsavo raṇe
atiṣṭhann āryavad vīrāḥ prārthayanto mahad yaśaḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
vyūḍham evaṃ yathānyāyam evaṃ bahu ca saṃjaya
nityaṃ pūjitam asmābhir abhikāmaṃ ca naḥ sadā
prauḍham atyadbhutākāraṃ purastād dṛḍhavikramam
nātivṛddham abālaṃ ca na kṛśaṃ nātipīvaram
laghuvṛttāyataprāṇaṃ sāragātram anāmayam
śastragrahaṇavidyāsu bahvīṣu pariniṣṭhitam
nāgeṣv aśveṣu bahuśo ratheṣu ca parīkṣitam
parīkṣya ca yathānyāyaṃ vetanenopapāditam
na goṣṭhyā nopacāreṇa na saṃbandhanimittataḥ
kulīnāryajanopetaṃ tuṣṭapuṣṭam anuddhatam
asmān abhisṛtaiḥ kāmāt sabalaiḥ sapadānugaiḥ
mahodadhim ivāpūrṇam āpagābhiḥ samantataḥ
apakṣaiḥ pakṣisaṃkāśai rathair aśvaiś ca saṃvṛtam
yodhākṣayyajalaṃ bhīmaṃ vāhanormitaraṅgiṇam
kṣepaṇyasigadāśaktiśaraprāsajhaṣākulam
dhvajabhūṣaṇasaṃbādhaṃ ratnapaṭṭena saṃcitam
droṇagambhīrapātālaṃ kṛtavarmamahāhradam
gate sainyārṇavaṃ bhittvā tarasā pāṇḍavarṣabhe
tatra śeṣaṃ na paśyāmi praviṣṭe savyasācini
sindhurājaṃ ca saṃprekṣya gāṇḍīvasyeṣugocare
kiṃ tadā kuravaḥ kṛtyaṃ vidadhuḥ kālacoditāḥ
dāruṇaikāyane kāle kathaṃ vā pratipedire
grastān hi kauravān manye mṛtyunā tāta saṃgatān
vikramo hi raṇe teṣāṃ na tathā dṛśyate 'dya vai
akṣatau saṃyuge tatra praviṣṭau kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
bhṛtāś ca bahavo yodhāḥ parīkṣyaiva mahārathāḥ
pūjitā hi yathāśaktyā dānamānāsanair mayā
tathā putraiś ca me tāta jñātibhiś ca sabāndhavaiḥ
te ca prāpyaiva saṃgrāme nirjitāḥ savyasācinā
śaineyena parāmṛṣṭāḥ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ
rakṣyate yaś ca saṃgrāme ye ca saṃjaya rakṣiṇaḥ
ekaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ panthā rakṣyasya saha rakṣibhiḥ
arjunaṃ samare dṛṣṭvā saindhavasyāgrataḥ sthitam
putro mama bhṛśaṃ mūḍhaḥ kiṃ kāryaṃ pratyapadyata
sātyakiṃ ca raṇe dṛṣṭvā praviśantam abhītavat
dṛṣṭvā kāṃ vai dhṛtiṃ yuddhe pratyapadyanta māmakāḥ
dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ tu dāśārham arjunārthe vyavasthitam
śinīnām ṛṣabhaṃ caiva manye śocanti putrakāḥ
dṛṣṭvā senāṃ vyatikrāntāṃ sātvatenārjunena ca
palāyamānāṃś ca kurūn manye śocanti putrakāḥ
vidrutān rathino dṛṣṭvā nirutsāhān dviṣajjaye
palāyane kṛtotsāhān manye śocanti putrakāḥ
śūnyān kṛtān rathopasthān sātvatenārjunena ca
hatāṃś ca yodhān saṃdṛśya manye śocanti putrakāḥ
vyaśvanāgarathān dṛṣṭvā tatra vīrān sahasraśaḥ
dhāvamānān raṇe vyagrān manye śocanti putrakāḥ
vivīrāṃś ca kṛtān aśvān virathāṃś ca kṛtān narān
tatra sātyakipārthābhyāṃ manye śocanti putrakāḥ
pattisaṃghān raṇe dṛṣṭvā dhāvamānāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
nirāśā vijaye sarve manye śocanti putrakāḥ
kṣaṇena dṛṣṭvā tau vīrau manye śocanti putrakāḥ
saṃmūḍho 'smi bhṛśaṃ tāta śrutvā kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
praviṣṭau māmakaṃ sainyaṃ sātvatena sahācyutau
tasmin praviṣṭe pṛtanāṃ śinīnāṃ pravare rathe
bhojānīkaṃ vyatikrānte katham āsan hi kauravāḥ
tathā droṇena samare nigṛhīteṣu pāṇḍuṣu
droṇo hi balavāñ śūraḥ kṛtāstro dṛḍhavikramaḥ
pāñcālās taṃ maheṣvāsaṃ pratyayudhyan kathaṃ raṇe
baddhavairās tathā droṇe dharmarājajayaiṣiṇaḥ
bhāradvājas tathā teṣu kṛtavairo mahārathaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
ātmāparādhāt saṃbhūtaṃ vyasanaṃ bharatarṣabha
prāpya prākṛtavad vīra na tvaṃ śocitum arhasi
tava nirguṇatāṃ jñātvā pakṣapātaṃ suteṣu ca
dvaidhībhāvaṃ tathā dharme pāṇḍaveṣu ca matsaram
ārtapralāpāṃś ca bahūn manujādhipasattama
ātmāparādhāt sumahān prāptas te vipulaḥ kṣayaḥ
dṛśyate pṛṣṭhataś caiva tvanmūlo hi parājayaḥ
tasmād adya sthiro bhūtvā jñātvā lokasya nirṇayam
śṛṇu yuddhaṃ yathā vṛttaṃ ghoraṃ devāsuropamam
bhīmasenamukhāḥ pārthāḥ pratīyur vāhinīṃ tava
āgacchatas tān sahasā kruddharūpān sahānugān
dadhāraiko raṇe pāṇḍūn kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
yathodvṛttaṃ dhārayate velā vai salilārṇavam
pāṇḍusainyaṃ tathā saṃkhye hārdikyaḥ samavārayat
yad enaṃ sahitāḥ pārthā nāticakramur āhave
tato bhīmas tribhir viddhvā kṛtavarmāṇam āyasaiḥ
śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau mahābāhur harṣayan sarvapāṇḍavān
sahadevas tu viṃśatyā dharmarājaś ca pañcabhiḥ
dhṛṣṭadyumnas tribhiś cāpi kṛtavarmāṇam ārdayat
virāṭo drupadaś caiva yājñaseniś ca pañcabhiḥ
śikhaṇḍī cāpi hārdikyaṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āśugaiḥ
punar vivyādha viṃśatyā sāyakānāṃ hasann iva
kṛtavarmā tato rājan sarvatas tān mahārathān
ekaikaṃ pañcabhir viddhvā bhīmaṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥ
athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
ājaghānorasi kruddhaḥ saptatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
bhīmasenaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā dharmarājapurogamāḥ
visṛjantaḥ śarān ghorān kṛtavarmāṇam ārdayan
taṃ tathā koṣṭhakīkṛtya rathavaṃśena māriṣa
vivyadhuḥ sāyakair hṛṣṭā rakṣārthaṃ māruter mṛdhe
pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
śaktiṃ jagrāha samare hemadaṇḍām ayasmayīm
cikṣepa ca rathāt tūrṇaṃ kṛtavarmarathaṃ prati
kṛtavarmāṇam abhitaḥ prajajvāla sudāruṇā
tām āpatantīṃ sahasā yugāntāgnisamaprabhām
dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ hārdikyo nicakarta dvidhā tadā
sā chinnā patitā bhūmau śaktiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇā
śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmaś cukrodha vai bhṛśam
athainaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntare
bhojas tu kṣatasarvāṅgo bhīmasenena māriṣa
śikhaṇḍinas tataḥ kruddhaḥ kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥ
śikhaṇḍī tu tataḥ kruddhaś chinne dhanuṣi satvaram
bhrāmayitvā mahācarma cāmīkaravibhūṣitam
tam asiṃ preṣayām āsa kṛtavarmarathaṃ prati
sa tasya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ chittvā saṃkhye mahān asiḥ
abhyagād dharaṇīṃ rājaṃś cyutaṃ jyotir ivāmbarāt
etasminn eva kāle tu tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥ
vivyadhuḥ sāyakair gāḍhaṃ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave
viśīrṇaṃ bharataśreṣṭha hārdikyaḥ paravīrahā
śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca vivyādha tribhiḥ pañcabhir eva ca
dhanur anyat samādāya śikhaṇḍī tu mahāyaśāḥ
avārayat kūrmanakhair āśugair hṛdikātmajam
tataḥ kruddho raṇe rājan hṛdikasyātmasaṃbhavaḥ
bhīṣmasya samare rājan mṛtyor hetuṃ mahātmanaḥ
vidarśayan balaṃ śūraḥ śārdūla iva kuñjaram
tau diśāgajasaṃkāśau jvalitāv iva pāvakau
vidhunvānau dhanuḥśreṣṭhe saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān
tāpayantau śarais tīkṣṇair anyonyaṃ tau mahārathau
kṛtavarmā tu rabhasaṃ yājñaseniṃ mahāratham
viddhveṣūṇāṃ trisaptatyā punar vivyādha saptabhiḥ
visṛjan saśaraṃ cāpaṃ mūrchayābhipariplutaḥ
taṃ viṣaṇṇaṃ rathe dṛṣṭvā tāvakā bharatarṣabha
hārdikyaṃ pūjayām āsur vāsāṃsy ādudhuvuś ca ha
śikhaṇḍinaṃ tathā jñātvā hārdikyaśarapīḍitam
apovāha raṇād yantā tvaramāṇo mahāratham
sāditaṃ tu rathopasthe dṛṣṭvā pārthāḥ śikhaṇḍinam
parivavrū rathais tūrṇaṃ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave
tatrādbhutaṃ paraṃ cakre kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
yad ekaḥ samare pārthān vārayām āsa sānugān
pārthāñ jitvājayac cedīn pāñcālān sṛñjayān api
kekayāṃś ca mahāvīryān kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
te vadhyamānāḥ samare hārdikyena sma pāṇḍavāḥ
itaś cetaś ca dhāvanto naiva cakrur dhṛtiṃ raṇe
jitvā pāṇḍusutān yuddhe bhīmasenapurogamān
hārdikyaḥ samare 'tiṣṭhad vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
te drāvyamāṇāḥ samare hārdikyena mahārathāḥ
vimukhāḥ samapadyanta śaravṛṣṭibhir arditāḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
śṛṇuṣvaikamanā rājan yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
drāvyamāṇe bale tasmin hārdikyena mahātmanā
lajjayāvanate cāpi prahṛṣṭaiś caiva tāvakaiḥ
dvīpo ya āsīt pāṇḍūnām agādhe gādham icchatām
śrutvā tu ninadaṃ bhīmaṃ tāvakānāṃ mahāhave
śaineyas tvarito rājan kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāt
kṛtavarmā tu hārdikyaḥ śaineyaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
tataḥ suniśitaṃ bhallaṃ śaineyaḥ kṛtavarmaṇe
preṣayām āsa samare śarāṃś ca caturo 'parān
pṛṣṭharakṣaṃ tathā sūtam avidhyan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
tatas taṃ virathaṃ kṛtvā sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
senām asyārdayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
sābhajyatātha pṛtanā śaineyaśarapīḍitā
tataḥ prāyād vai tvaritaḥ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
śṛṇu rājan yad akarot tava sainyeṣu vīryavān
atītya sa mahārāja droṇānīkamahārṇavam
parājitya ca saṃhṛṣṭaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave
yantāram abravīc chūraḥ śanair yāhīty asaṃbhramam
dṛṣṭvā tu tava tat sainyaṃ rathāśvadvipasaṃkulam
padātijanasaṃpūrṇam abravīt sārathiṃ punaḥ
yad etan meghasaṃkāśaṃ droṇānīkasya savyataḥ
ete hi bahavaḥ sūta durnivāryāś ca saṃyuge
duryodhanasamādiṣṭā madarthe tyaktajīvitāḥ
rājaputrā maheṣvāsāḥ sarve vikrāntayodhinaḥ
trigartānāṃ rathodārāḥ suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥ
mām evābhimukhā vīrā yotsyamānā vyavasthitāḥ
atra māṃ prāpaya kṣipram aśvāṃś codaya sārathe
tataḥ prāyāc chanaiḥ sūtaḥ sātvatasya mate sthitaḥ
rathenādityavarṇena bhāsvareṇa patākinā
tam ūhuḥ sārather vaśyā valgamānā hayottamāḥ
āpatantaṃ rathaṃ taṃ tu śaṅkhavarṇair hayottamaiḥ
parivavrus tataḥ śūrā gajānīkena sarvataḥ
kiranto vividhāṃs tīkṣṇān sāyakāṃl laghuvedhinaḥ
sātvato 'pi śitair bāṇair gajānīkam ayodhayat
vajrāśanisamasparśair vadhyamānāḥ śarair gajāḥ
prādravan raṇam utsṛjya śinivīryasamīritaiḥ
śīrṇadantā virudhirā bhinnamastakapiṇḍakāḥ
viśīrṇakarṇāsyakarā viniyantṛpatākinaḥ
saṃbhinnavarmaghaṇṭāś ca saṃnikṛttamahādhvajāḥ
hatārohā diśo rājan bhejire bhraṣṭakambalāḥ
ruvanto vividhān rāvāñ jaladopamanisvanāḥ
nārācair vatsadantaiś ca sātvatena vidāritāḥ
yattaḥ saṃprāpayan nāgaṃ rajatāśvarathaṃ prati
rukmavarṇakaraḥ śūras tapanīyāṅgadaḥ śuciḥ
kuṇḍalī mukuṭī śaṅkhī raktacandanarūṣitaḥ
śirasā dhārayan dīptāṃ tapanīyamayīṃ srajam
urasā dhārayan niṣkaṃ kaṇṭhasūtraṃ ca bhāsvaram
sātyakir vārayām āsa velevodvṛttam arṇavam
nāgaṃ nivāritaṃ dṛṣṭvā śaineyasya śarottamaiḥ
akrudhyata raṇe rājañ jalasaṃdho mahābalaḥ
tataḥ kruddho maheṣvāso mārgaṇair bhārasādhanaiḥ
asyato vṛṣṇivīrasya nicakarta śarāsanam
avidhyan māgadho vīraḥ pañcabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
acintayan vai sa śarān nātyarthaṃ saṃbhramād balī
dhanur anyat samādāya tiṣṭha tiṣṭhety uvāca ha
vivyādha ṣaṣṭyā subhṛśaṃ śarāṇāṃ prahasann iva
kṣurapreṇa ca pītena muṣṭideśe mahad dhanuḥ
tomaraṃ vyasṛjat tūrṇaṃ sātyakiṃ prati māriṣa
abhyagād dharaṇīṃ ghoraḥ śvasann iva mahoragaḥ
triṃśadbhir viśikhais tīkṣṇair jalasaṃdham atāḍayat
pragṛhya tu tataḥ khaḍgaṃ jalasaṃdho mahābalaḥ
tata āvidhya taṃ khaḍgaṃ sātvatāyotsasarja ha
athānyad dhanur ādāya sarvakāyāvadāraṇam
śālaskandhapratīkāśam indrāśanisamasvanam
tataḥ sābharaṇau bāhū kṣurābhyāṃ mādhavottamaḥ
vasuṃdharadharād bhraṣṭau pañcaśīrṣāv ivoragau
tataḥ sudaṃṣṭraṃ suhanu cārukuṇḍalam unnasam
kṣureṇāsya tṛtīyena śiraś ciccheda sātyakiḥ
tat pātitaśirobāhukabandhaṃ bhīmadarśanam
jalasaṃdhaṃ nihatyājau tvaramāṇas tu sātvataḥ
naiṣādiṃ pātayām āsa gajaskandhād viśāṃ pate
rudhireṇāvasiktāṅgo jalasaṃdhasya kuñjaraḥ
vilambamānam avahat saṃśliṣṭaṃ param āsanam
śarārditaḥ sātvatena mardamānaḥ svavāhinīm
ghoram ārtasvaraṃ kṛtvā vidudrāva mahāgajaḥ
hāhākāro mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣa
jalasaṃdhaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā vṛṣṇīnām ṛṣabheṇa ha
vimukhāś cābhyadhāvanta tava yodhāḥ samantataḥ
palāyane kṛtotsāhā nirutsāhā dviṣajjaye
etasminn antare rājan droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
tam udīrṇaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā śaineyaṃ kurupuṃgavāḥ
tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ sātvatasya ca
saṃjaya uvāca
te kirantaḥ śaravrātān sarve yattāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
tvaramāṇā mahārāja yuyudhānam ayodhayan
taṃ droṇaḥ saptasaptatyā jaghāna niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
durmarṣaṇo dvādaśabhir duḥsaho daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
vikarṇaś cāpi niśitais triṃśadbhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
durmukho daśabhir bāṇais tathā duḥśāsano 'ṣṭabhiḥ
citrasenaś ca śaineyaṃ dvābhyāṃ vivyādha māriṣa
duryodhanaś ca mahatā śaravarṣeṇa mādhavam
apīḍayad raṇe rājañ śūrāś cānye mahārathāḥ
bhāradvājaṃ tribhir bāṇair duḥsahaṃ navabhis tathā
vikarṇaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā citrasenaṃ ca saptabhiḥ
durmarṣaṇaṃ dvādaśabhiś caturbhiś ca viviṃśatim
tato rukmāṅgadaṃ cāpaṃ vidhunvāno mahārathaḥ
abhyayāt sātyakis tūrṇaṃ putraṃ tava mahāratham
rājānaṃ sarvalokasya sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
śarair abhyāhanad gāḍhaṃ tato yuddham abhūt tayoḥ
vimuñcantau śarāṃs tīkṣṇān saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān
śātakumbhamayāpīḍo babhau yūpa ivocchritaḥ
nirbhinnaś ca śarais tena dviṣatā kṣiprakāriṇā
nāmṛṣyata raṇe rājā śatror vijayalakṣaṇam
athānyad dhanur ādāya hemapṛṣṭhaṃ durāsadam
vivyādha sātyakiṃ tūrṇaṃ sāyakānāṃ śatena ha
pīḍitaṃ nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā tava putrā mahārathāḥ
sātvataṃ śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsur añjasā
duryodhanaṃ ca tvarito vivyādhāṣṭabhir āśugaiḥ
prahasaṃś cāsya ciccheda kārmukaṃ ripubhīṣaṇam
nāgaṃ maṇimayaṃ caiva śarair dhvajam apātayat
hatvā tu caturo vāhāṃś caturbhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
sārathiṃ pātayām āsa kṣurapreṇa mahāyaśāḥ
hāhābhūtaṃ jagac cāsīd dṛṣṭvā rājānam āhave
grasyamānaṃ sātyakinā khe somam iva rāhuṇā
taṃ tu śabdaṃ mahac chrutvā kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
vidhunvāno dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ codayaṃś caiva vājinaḥ
bhartsayan sārathiṃ cograṃ yāhi yāhīti satvaraḥ
tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
kṛtavarmā rathenaiṣa drutam āpatate śarī
āsasāda raṇe bhojaṃ pratimānaṃ dhanuṣmatām
kṛtavarmā tu śaineyaṃ ṣaḍviṃśatyā samārpayat
niśitaiḥ sāyakais tīkṣṇair yantāraṃ cāsya saptabhiḥ
caturaś ca hayodārāṃś caturbhiḥ parameṣubhiḥ
rukmāṅgadī rukmavarmā rukmapuṅkhān avākirat
tato 'śītiṃ śineḥ pautraḥ sāyakān kṛtavarmaṇe
prāhiṇot tvarayā yukto draṣṭukāmo dhanaṃjayam
so 'tividdho balavatā śatruṇā śatrutāpanaḥ
triṣaṣṭyā caturo 'syāśvān saptabhiḥ sārathiṃ śaraiḥ
vivyādha niśitais tūrṇaṃ sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ
suvarṇapuṅkhaṃ viśikhaṃ samādhāya sa sātyakiḥ
so 'viśat kṛtavarmāṇaṃ yamadaṇḍopamaḥ śaraḥ
abhyagād dharaṇīm ugro rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ
saṃjātarudhiraś cājau sātvateṣubhir arditaḥ
sa siṃhadaṃṣṭro jānubhyām āpanno 'mitavikramaḥ
śarārditaḥ sātyakinā rathopasthe nararṣabhaḥ
sahasrabāhoḥ sadṛśam akṣobhyam iva sāgaram
nivārya kṛtavarmāṇaṃ sātyakiḥ prayayau tataḥ
khaḍgaśaktidhanuḥkīrṇāṃ gajāśvarathasaṃkulām
pravartitograrudhirāṃ śataśaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhaiḥ
prekṣatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ madhyena śinipuṃgavaḥ
abhyagād vāhinīṃ bhittvā vṛtrahevāsurīṃ camūm
samāśvāsya ca hārdikyo gṛhya cānyan mahad dhanuḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
kālyamāneṣu sainyeṣu śaineyena tatas tataḥ
bhāradvājaḥ śaravrātair mahadbhiḥ samavākirat
paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ balivāsavayor iva
tato droṇaḥ śineḥ pautraṃ citraiḥ sarvāyasaiḥ śaraiḥ
tribhir āśīviṣākārair lalāṭe samavidhyata
tair lalāṭārpitair bāṇair yuyudhānas tv ajihmagaiḥ
vyarocata mahārāja triśṛṅga iva parvataḥ
tato 'sya bāṇān aparān indrāśanisamasvanān
bhāradvājo 'ntaraprekṣī preṣayām āsa saṃyuge
tān droṇacāpanirmuktān dāśārhaḥ patataḥ śarān
dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ supuṅkhābhyāṃ ciccheda paramāstravit
tām asya laghutāṃ droṇaḥ samavekṣya viśāṃ pate
punaḥ pañcāśateṣūṇāṃ śatena ca samārpayat
laghutāṃ yuyudhānasya lāghavena viśeṣayan
tathaiva yuyudhānena sṛṣṭāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
avākiran droṇarathaṃ śarā rudhirabhojanāḥ
viśeṣaṃ nādhyagacchāma samāvāstāṃ nararṣabhau
ājaghāna bhṛśaṃ kruddho dhvajaṃ ca niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
sārathiṃ ca śatenaiva bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ
lāghavaṃ yuyudhānasya dṛṣṭvā droṇo mahārathaḥ
saptatyā sātyakiṃ viddhvā turagāṃś ca tribhis tribhiḥ
gadāṃ jagrāha mahatīṃ bhāradvājāya cākṣipat
tām āpatantīṃ sahasā paṭṭabaddhām ayasmayīm
athānyad dhanur ādāya sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
vivyādha bahubhir vīraṃ bhāradvājaṃ śilāśitaiḥ
sa viddhvā samare droṇaṃ siṃhanādam amuñcata
taṃ vai na mamṛṣe droṇaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
tathaḥ śaktiṃ gṛhītvā tu rukmadaṇḍām ayasmayīm
tarasā preṣayām āsa mādhavasya rathaṃ prati
anāsādya tu śaineyaṃ sā śaktiḥ kālasaṃnibhā
bhittvā rathaṃ jagāmogrā dharaṇīṃ dāruṇasvanā
tato droṇaṃ śineḥ pautro rājan vivyādha patriṇā
dakṣiṇaṃ bhujam āsādya pīḍayan bharatarṣabha
sa rathopastham āsādya muhūrtaṃ saṃnyaṣīdata
cakāra sātyakī rājaṃs tatra karmātimānuṣam
tataḥ śaraśatenaiva yuyudhāno mahārathaḥ
avidhyad brāhmaṇaṃ saṃkhye hṛṣṭarūpo viśāṃ pate
tasya droṇaḥ śarān pañca preṣayām āsa bhārata
te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave
sāyakān vyasṛjac cāpi vīro rukmarathaṃ prati
tato droṇasya yantāraṃ nipātyaikeṣuṇā bhuvi
aśvān vyadrāvayad bāṇair hatasūtān mahātmanaḥ
sa rathaḥ pradrutaḥ saṃkhye maṇḍalāni sahasraśaḥ
cakāra rājato rājan bhrājamāna ivāṃśumān
abhidravata gṛhṇīta hayān droṇasya dhāvata
iti sma cukruśuḥ sarve rājaputrāḥ sarājakāḥ
te sātyakim apāsyāśu rājan yudhi mahārathāḥ
tān dṛṣṭvā pradrutān sarvān sātvatena śarārditān
vātāyamānais tair aśvair hṛto vṛṣṇiśarārditaiḥ
pāṇḍupāñcālasaṃbhagnaṃ vyūham ālokya vīryavān
śaineye nākarod yatnaṃ vyūhasyaivābhirakṣaṇe
nivārya pāṇḍupāñcālān droṇāgniḥ pradahann iva
tasthau krodhāgnisaṃdīptaḥ kālasūrya ivoditaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
droṇaṃ sa jitvā puruṣapravīras tathaiva hārdikyamukhāṃs tvadīyān
prahasya sūtaṃ vacanaṃ babhāṣe śinipravīraḥ kurupuṃgavāgrya
kiran samantāt sahasā śarān balī samāpatac chyena ivāmiṣaṃ yathā
taṃ yāntam aśvaiḥ śaśiśaṅkhavarṇair vigāhya sainyaṃ puruṣapravīram
nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ samantād ādityaraśmipratimaṃ narāgryam
amarṣapūrṇas tv aticitrayodhī śarāsanī kāñcanavarmadhārī
tayor abhūd bharata saṃprahāraḥ sudāruṇas taṃ samabhipraśaṃsan
yodhās tvadīyāś ca hi somakāś ca vṛtrendrayor yuddham ivāmaraughāḥ
śaraiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ śataśo 'bhyavidhyat sudarśanaḥ sātvatamukhyam ājau
anāgatān eva tu tān pṛṣatkāṃś ciccheda bāṇaiḥ śinipuṃgavo 'pi
saṃprekṣya bāṇān nihatāṃs tadānīṃ sudarśanaḥ sātyakibāṇavegaiḥ
krodhād didhakṣann iva tigmatejāḥ śarān amuñcat tapanīyacitrān
punaḥ sa bāṇais tribhir agnikalpair ākarṇapūrṇair niśitaiḥ supuṅkhaiḥ
vivyādha dehāvaraṇaṃ vibhidya te sātyaker āviviśuḥ śarīram
ājaghnivāṃs tān rajataprakāśāṃś caturbhir aśvāṃś caturaḥ prasahya
tathā tu tenābhihatas tarasvī naptā śiner indrasamānavīryaḥ
sudarśanasyeṣugaṇaiḥ sutīkṣṇair hayān nihatyāśu nanāda nādam
sudarśanasyāpi śinipravīraḥ kṣureṇa ciccheda śiraḥ prasahya
sakuṇḍalaṃ pūrṇaśaśiprakāśaṃ bhrājiṣṇu vaktraṃ nicakarta dehāt
nihatya taṃ pārthivaputrapautraṃ raṇe yadūnām ṛṣabhas tarasvī
mudā sametaḥ parayā mahātmā rarāja rājan surarājakalpaḥ
sadaśvayuktena rathena niryāl lokān visismāpayiṣur nṛvīraḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
tataḥ sa sātyakir dhīmān mahātmā vṛṣṇipuṃgavaḥ
rathāśvanāgakalilaṃ śaraśaktyūrmimālinam
khaḍgamatsyaṃ gadāgrāhaṃ śūrāyudhamahāsvanam
prāṇāpahāriṇaṃ raudraṃ vāditrotkruṣṭanāditam
yodhānām asukhasparśaṃ durdharṣam ajayaiṣiṇām
tīrṇāḥ sma dustaraṃ tāta droṇānīkamahārṇavam
jalasaṃdhabalenājau puruṣādair ivāvṛtam
ato 'nyaṃ pṛtanāśeṣaṃ manye kunadikām iva
tartavyām alpasalilāṃ codayāśvān asaṃbhramam
na hi me jāyate trāso dṛṣṭvā sainyāny anekaśaḥ
vahner iva pradīptasya grīṣme śuṣkaṃ tṛṇolapam
paśya pāṇḍavamukhyena yātāṃ bhūmiṃ kirīṭinā
pattyaśvarathanāgaughaiḥ patitair viṣamīkṛtām
abhyāśastham ahaṃ manye śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathim
sa eṣa śrūyate śabdo gāṇḍīvasyāmitaujasaḥ
yādṛśāni nimittāni mama prādurbhavanti vai
śanair viśrambhayann aśvān yāhi yatto 'rivāhinīm
yatraite satanutrāṇāḥ suyodhanapurogamāḥ
daṃśitāḥ krūrakarmāṇaḥ kāmbojā yuddhadurmadāḥ
śarabāṇāsanadharā yavanāś ca prahāriṇaḥ
śakāḥ kirātā daradā barbarās tāmraliptakāḥ
mām evābhimukhāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti samarārthinaḥ
etān sarathanāgāśvān nihatyājau sapattinaḥ
idaṃ durgaṃ mahāghoraṃ tīrṇam evopadhāraya
sūta uvāca
droṇo vā rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpo madreśvaro 'pi vā
tathāpi saṃbhramo na syāt tvām āśritya mahābhuja
na ca me saṃbhramaḥ kaś cid bhūtapūrvaḥ kadā cana
āyuṣman katareṇa tvā prāpayāmi dhanaṃjayam
keṣāṃ kruddho 'si vārṣṇeya keṣāṃ mṛtyur upasthitaḥ
keṣāṃ saṃyamanīm adya gantum utsahate manaḥ
ke tvāṃ yudhi parākrāntaṃ kālāntakayamopamam
dṛṣṭvā vikramasaṃpannaṃ vidraviṣyanti saṃyuge
keṣāṃ vaivasvato rājā smarate 'dya mahābhuja
sātyakir uvāca
muṇḍān etān haniṣyāmi dānavān iva vāsavaḥ
pratijñāṃ pārayiṣyāmi kāmbojān eva mā vaha
adyaiṣāṃ kadanaṃ kṛtvā kṣipraṃ yāsyāmi pāṇḍavam
adya drakṣyanti me vīryaṃ kauravāḥ sasuyodhanāḥ
muṇḍānīke hate sūta sarvasainyeṣu cāsakṛt
śrutvā virāvaṃ bahudhā saṃtapsyati suyodhanaḥ
adya pāṇḍavamukhyasya śvetāśvasya mahātmanaḥ
ācāryakakṛtaṃ mārgaṃ darśayiṣyāmi saṃyuge
adya madbāṇanihatān yodhamukhyān sahasraśaḥ
dṛṣṭvā duryodhano rājā paścāttāpaṃ gamiṣyati
matsāyakacitāṅgānāṃ rudhiraṃ sravatāṃ bahu
sainikānāṃ vadhaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃtapsyati suyodhanaḥ
adya rājasahasrāṇi nihatāni mayā raṇe
dṛṣṭvā duryodhano rājā saṃtapsyati mahāmṛdhe
adya snehaṃ ca bhaktiṃ ca pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
hatvā rājasahasrāṇi darśayiṣyāmi rājasu
saṃjaya uvāca
evam uktas tadā sūtaḥ śikṣitān sādhuvāhinaḥ
śaśāṅkasaṃnikāśān vai vājino 'cūcudad bhṛśam
te pibanta ivākāśaṃ yuyudhānaṃ hayottamāḥ
prāpayan yavanāñ śīghraṃ manaḥpavanaraṃhasaḥ
sātyakiṃ te samāsādya pṛtanāsv anivartinam
teṣām iṣūn athāstrāṇi vegavan nataparvabhiḥ
acchinat sātyakī rājan nainaṃ te prāpnuvañ śarāḥ
uccakarta śirāṃsy ugro yavanānāṃ bhujān api
śaikyāyasāni varmāṇi kāṃsyāni ca samantataḥ
bhittvā dehāṃs tathā teṣāṃ śarā jagmur mahītalam
te hanyamānā vīreṇa mlecchāḥ sātyakinā raṇe
supūrṇāyatamuktais tān avyavacchinnapiṇḍitaiḥ
pañca ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭau ca bibheda yavanāñ śaraiḥ
kāmbojānāṃ sahasrais tu śakānāṃ ca viśāṃ pate
śabarāṇāṃ kirātānāṃ barbarāṇāṃ tathaiva ca
agamyarūpāṃ pṛthivīṃ māṃsaśoṇitakardamām
kṛtavāṃs tatra śaineyaḥ kṣapayaṃs tāvakaṃ balam
dasyūnāṃ saśirastrāṇaiḥ śirobhir lūnamūrdhajaiḥ
tatra tatra mahī kīrṇā vibarhair aṇḍajair iva
kabandhaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ sarvaṃ tāmrābhraiḥ kham ivāvṛtam
te sāśvayānā nihatāḥ samāvavrur vasuṃdharām
alpāvaśiṣṭāḥ saṃbhagnāḥ kṛcchraprāṇā vicetasaḥ
jitāḥ saṃkhye mahārāja yuyudhānena daṃśitāḥ
pārṣṇibhiś ca kaśābhiś ca tāḍayantas turaṃgamān
yavanānāṃ ca tat sainyaṃ śakānāṃ ca mahad balam
sa tataḥ puruṣavyāghraḥ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
prahṛṣṭas tāvakāñ jitvā sūtaṃ yāhīty acodayat
taṃ yāntaṃ pṛṣṭhagoptāram arjunasya viśāṃ pate
cāraṇāḥ prekṣya saṃhṛṣṭās tvadīyāś cāpy apūjayan
saṃjaya uvāca
mṛgān vyāghra ivājighraṃs tava sainyam abhīṣayat
rukmapṛṣṭhaṃ mahāvegaṃ rukmacandrakasaṃkulam
rukmāṅgadaśirastrāṇo rukmavarmasamāvṛtaḥ
rukmadhvajavaraḥ śūro meruśṛṅga ivābabhau
sadhanurmaṇḍalaḥ saṃkhye tejobhāsvararaśmivān
śaradīvoditaḥ sūryo nṛsūryo virarāja ha
vṛṣabhaskandhavikrānto vṛṣabhākṣo nararṣabhaḥ
tāvakānāṃ babhau madhye gavāṃ madhye yathā vṛṣaḥ
vyāghrā iva jighāṃsantas tvadīyābhyadravan raṇe
droṇānīkam atikrāntaṃ bhojānīkaṃ ca dustaram
jalasaṃdhārṇavaṃ tīrtvā kāmbojānāṃ ca vāhinīm
hārdikyamakarān muktaṃ tīrṇaṃ vai sainyasāgaram
parivavruḥ susaṃkruddhās tvadīyāḥ sātyakiṃ rathāḥ
duryodhanaś citraseno duḥśāsanaviviṃśatī
śakunir duḥsahaś caiva yuvā durmarṣaṇaḥ krathaḥ
anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śastravanto durāsadāḥ
pṛṣṭhataḥ sātyakiṃ yāntam anvadhāvann amarṣitāḥ
atha śabdo mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣa
tān abhidravataḥ sarvān samīkṣya śinipuṃgavaḥ
mām evābhimukhaṃ tūrṇaṃ gajāśvarathapattimat
nādayan vai diśaḥ sarvā rathaghoṣeṇa sārathe
pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca kampayan sāgarān api
etad balārṇavaṃ tāta vārayiṣye mahāraṇe
paurṇamāsyām ivoddhūtaṃ veleva salilāśayam
eṣa sainyāni śatrūṇāṃ vidhamāmi śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
nihatān āhave paśya padātyaśvarathadvipān
maccharair agnisaṃkāśair videhāsūn sahasraśaḥ
samīpaṃ sainikās te tu śīghram īyur yuyutsavaḥ
jahy ādravasva tiṣṭheti paśya paśyeti vādinaḥ
tān evaṃ bruvato vīrān sātyakir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
jaghāna triśatān aśvān kuñjarāṃś ca catuḥśatān
devāsuraraṇaprakhyaḥ prāvartata janakṣayaḥ
pratyagṛhṇāc chineḥ pautraḥ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
pracchādyamānaḥ samare śarajālaiḥ sa vīryavān
asaṃbhramaṃ mahārāja tāvakān avadhīd bahūn
āścaryaṃ tatra rājendra sumahad dṛṣṭavān aham
rathanāgāśvakalilaḥ padātyūrmisamākulaḥ
śaineyavelām āsādya sthitaḥ sainyamahārṇavaḥ
saṃbhrāntanaranāgāśvam āvartata muhur muhuḥ
babhrāma tatra tatraiva gāvaḥ śītārditā iva
padātinaṃ rathaṃ nāgaṃ sādinaṃ turagaṃ tathā
aviddhaṃ tatra nādrākṣaṃ yuyudhānasya sāyakaiḥ
na tādṛk kadanaṃ rājan kṛtavāṃs tatra phalgunaḥ
yādṛk kṣayam anīkānām akarot sātyakir nṛpa
vivyādha sūtaṃ niśitaiś caturbhiś caturo hayān
sātyakiṃ ca tribhir viddhvā punar vivyādha so 'ṣṭabhiḥ
duḥśāsanaḥ ṣoḍaśabhir vivyādha śinipuṃgavam
śakuniḥ pañcaviṃśatyā citrasenaś ca pañcabhiḥ
utsmayan vṛṣṇiśārdūlas tathā bāṇaiḥ samāhataḥ
gāḍhaviddhān arīn kṛtvā mārgaṇaiḥ so 'titejanaiḥ
citrasenaṃ śatenaiva daśabhir duḥsahaṃ tathā
duḥśāsanaṃ ca viṃśatyā vivyādha śinipuṃgavaḥ
athānyad dhanur ādāya syālas tava viśāṃ pate
aṣṭabhiḥ sātyakiṃ viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
duḥśāsanaś ca daśabhir duḥsahaś ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
durmukhaś ca dvādaśabhī rājan vivyādha sātyakim
tān sarvān sahitāñ śūrān yatamānān mahārathān
pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir bāṇaiḥ punar vivyādha sātyakiḥ
tataḥ sa rathināṃ śreṣṭhas tava putrasya sārathim
vātāyamānais tair aśvair apānīyata saṃgarāt
tatas tava sutā rājan sainikāś ca viśāṃ pate
rājño ratham abhiprekṣya vidrutāḥ śataśo 'bhavan
vidrutaṃ tatra tat sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhārata sātyakiḥ
avākirac charais tīkṣṇai rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
prayayau sātyakī rājañ śvetāśvasya rathaṃ prati
taṃ śarān ādadānaṃ ca rakṣamāṇaṃ ca sārathim
ātmānaṃ mocayantaṃ ca tāvakāḥ samapūjayan
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
kathaṃ caiṣāṃ tathā yuddhe dhṛtir āsīn mumūrṣatām
śaineyacaritaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadṛśaṃ savyasācinaḥ
kiṃ nu vakṣyanti te kṣātraṃ sainyamadhye parājitāḥ
kathaṃ ca sātyakir yuddhe vyatikrānto mahāyaśāḥ
kathaṃ ca mama putrāṇāṃ jīvatāṃ tatra saṃjaya
atyadbhutam idaṃ tāta tvatsakāśāc chṛṇomy aham
kruddhasya yuyudhānasya sarve tiṣṭhantu pāṇḍavāḥ
yathā paśugaṇān siṃhas tadvad dhantā sutān mama
yuyudhāno na śakito hantuṃ yaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
naitad īdṛśakaṃ yuddhaṃ kṛtavāṃs tatra phalgunaḥ
yādṛśaṃ kṛtavān yuddhaṃ śiner naptā mahāyaśāḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhūtvā yat te vakṣyāmi bhārata
te punaḥ saṃnyavartanta kṛtvā saṃśaptakān mithaḥ
parāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā putrasya tava śāsanāt
trīṇi sādisahasrāṇi duryodhanapurogamāḥ
śakāḥ kāmbojabāhlīkā yavanāḥ pāradās tathā
kuṇindās taṅgaṇāmbaṣṭhāḥ paiśācāś ca samandarāḥ
abhyadravanta śaineyaṃ śalabhāḥ pāvakaṃ yathā
yuktāś ca pārvatīyānāṃ rathāḥ pāṣāṇayodhinām
śūrāḥ pañcaśatā rājañ śaineyaṃ samupādravan
dviradānāṃ sahasreṇa dvisāhasraiś ca vājibhiḥ
śaravarṣāṇi muñcanto vividhāni mahārathāḥ
duḥśāsano mahārāja sātyaktiṃ paryavārayat
avadhīc ca rathānīkaṃ dviradānāṃ ca tad balam
sādinaś caiva tān sarvān dasyūn api ca sarvaśaḥ
akṣaiś ca bahudhā bhagnair īṣādaṇḍakabandhuraiḥ
kūbarair mathitaiś cāpi dhvajaiś cāpi nipātitaiḥ
varmabhiś cāmaraiś caiva vyavakīrṇā vasuṃdharā
girirūpadharāś cāpi patitāḥ kuñjarottamāḥ
jātā dantivarā rājañ śerate bahavo hatāḥ
vanāyujān pārvatīyān kāmbojāraṭṭabāhlikān
nānādeśasamutthāṃś ca nānājātyāṃś ca pattinaḥ
nijaghne tatra śaineyaḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
teṣu prakālyamāneṣu dasyūn duḥśāsano 'bravīt
tāṃś cāpi sarvān saṃprekṣya putro duḥśāsanas tava
pāṣāṇayodhinaḥ śūrān pārvatīyān acodayat
aśmayuddheṣu kuśalā naitaj jānāti sātyakiḥ
tathaiva kuravaḥ sarve nāśmayuddhaviśāradāḥ
abhidravata mā bhaiṣṭa na vaḥ prāpsyati sātyakiḥ
tato gajaśiśuprakhyair upalaiḥ śailavāsinaḥ
udyatair yuyudhānasya sthitā maraṇakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
kṣepaṇīyais tathāpy anye sātvatasya vadhaiṣiṇaḥ
teṣām āpatatām eva śilāyuddhaṃ cikīrṣatām
sātyakiḥ pratisaṃdhāya triṃśataṃ prāhiṇoc charān
tām aśmavṛṣṭiṃ tumulāṃ pārvatīyaiḥ samīritām
bibhedoragasaṃkāśair nārācaiḥ śinipuṃgavaḥ
tair aśmacūrṇair dīpyadbhiḥ khadyotānām iva vrajaiḥ
prāyaḥ sainyāny avadhyanta hāhābhūtāni māriṣa
tataḥ pañcaśatāḥ śūrāḥ samudyatamahāśilāḥ
pāṣāṇayodhinaḥ śūrān yatamānān avasthitān
tataḥ punar bastamukhair aśmavṛṣṭiṃ samantataḥ
ayohastaiḥ śūlahastair daradaiḥ khaśataṅgaṇaiḥ
ambaṣṭhaiś ca kuṇindaiś ca kṣiptāṃ kṣiptāṃ sa sātyakiḥ
nārācaiḥ prativivyādha prekṣamāṇo mahābalaḥ
adrīṇāṃ bhidyamānānām antarikṣe śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
aśmacūrṇaiḥ samākīrṇā manuṣyāś ca vayāṃsi ca
nāśaknuvann avasthātuṃ bhramarair iva daṃśitāḥ
hataśiṣṭā virudhirā bhinnamastakapiṇḍikāḥ
mādhavenārdyamānasya sāgarasyeva dāruṇaḥ
taṃ śabdaṃ tumulaṃ śrutvā droṇo yantāram abravīt
eṣa sūta raṇe kruddhaḥ sātvatānāṃ mahārathaḥ
pāṣāṇayodhibhir nūnaṃ yuyudhānaḥ samāgataḥ
na śaknuvanti yantāraḥ saṃyantuṃ tumule hayān
ity evaṃ bruvato rājan bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ
pratyuvāca tato yantā droṇaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ varam
paśya yodhān raṇe bhinnān dhāvamānāṃs tatas tataḥ
ete ca sahitāḥ śūrāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
atra kāryaṃ samādhatsva prāptakālam ariṃdama
sthāne vā gamane vāpi dūraṃ yātaś ca sātyakiḥ
te vadhyamānāḥ samare yuyudhānena tāvakāḥ
yuyudhānarathaṃ tyaktvā droṇānīkāya dudruvuḥ
yais tu duḥśāsanaḥ sārdhaṃ rathaiḥ pūrvaṃ nyavartata
saṃjaya uvāca
duḥśāsanarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā samīpe paryavasthitam
bhāradvājas tato vākyaṃ duḥśāsanam athābravīt
duḥśāsana rathāḥ sarve kasmād ete pravidrutāḥ
rājaputro bhavān atra rājabhrātā mahārathaḥ
svayaṃ vairaṃ mahat kṛtvā pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
ekaṃ sātyakim āsādya kathaṃ bhīto 'si saṃyuge
na jānīṣe purā tvaṃ tu gṛhṇann akṣān durodare
śarā hy ete bhaviṣyanti dāruṇāśīviṣopamāḥ
apriyāṇāṃ ca vacanaṃ pāṇḍaveṣu viśeṣataḥ
āśīviṣasamān pārthān kopayitvā kva yāsyasi
śocyeyaṃ bhāratī senā rājā caiva suyodhanaḥ
yasya tvaṃ karkaśo bhrātā palāyanaparāyaṇaḥ
nanu nāma tvayā vīra dīryamāṇā bhayārditā
svabāhubalam āsthāya rakṣitavyā hy anīkinī
ko 'nyaḥ sthāsyati saṃgrāme bhīto bhīte vyapāśraye
yadā gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca kaurava
yamau ca yudhi draṣṭāsi tadā tvaṃ kiṃ kariṣyasi
yudhi phalgunabāṇānāṃ sūryāgnisamatejasām
na tulyāḥ sātyakiśarā yeṣāṃ bhītaḥ palāyase
yadi tāvat kṛtā buddhiḥ palāyanaparāyaṇā
pṛthivī dharmarājasya śamenaiva pradīyatām
yāvat phalgunanārācā nirmuktoragasaṃnibhāḥ
nāviśanti śarīraṃ te tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
yāvat te pṛthivīṃ pārthā hatvā bhrātṛśataṃ raṇe
nākṣipanti mahātmānas tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
kṛṣṇaś ca samaraślāghī tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
yāvad bhīmo mahābāhur vigāhya mahatīṃ camūm
sodarāṃs te na mṛdnāti tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
pūrvam uktaś ca te bhrātā bhīṣmeṇa sa suyodhanaḥ
ajeyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ saṃkhye saumya saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
sa yuddhe dhṛtim āsthāya yatto yudhyasva pāṇḍavaiḥ
gaccha tūrṇaṃ rathenaiva tatra tiṣṭhati sātyakiḥ
tvayā hīnaṃ balaṃ hy etad vidraviṣyati bhārata
śrutaṃ cāśrutavat kṛtvā prāyād yena sa sātyakiḥ
droṇo 'pi rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pāñcālān pāṇḍavāṃs tathā
praviśya ca raṇe droṇaḥ pāñcālānāṃ varūthinīm
drāvayām āsa yodhān vai śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
tato droṇo mahārāja nāma viśrāvya saṃyuge
pāṇḍupāñcālamatsyānāṃ pracakre kadanaṃ mahat
taṃ jayantam anīkāni bhāradvājaṃ tatas tataḥ
pāñcālaputro dyutimān vīraketuḥ samabhyayāt
sa droṇaṃ pañcabhir viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
tatrādbhutaṃ mahārāja dṛṣṭavān asmi saṃyuge
yad droṇo rabhasaṃ yuddhe pāñcālyaṃ nābhyavartata
saṃniruddhaṃ raṇe droṇaṃ pāñcālā vīkṣya māriṣa
āvavruḥ sarvato rājan dharmaputrajayaiṣiṇaḥ
te śarair agnisaṃkāśais tomaraiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
nihatya tān bāṇagaṇān droṇo rājan samantataḥ
mahājaladharān vyomni mātariśvā vivān iva
tataḥ śaraṃ mahāghoraṃ sūryapāvakasaṃnibham
sa bhittvā tu śaro rājan pāñcālyaṃ kulanandanam
abhyagād dharaṇīṃ tūrṇaṃ lohitārdro jvalann iva
tato 'patad rathāt tūrṇaṃ pāñcālyaḥ kulanandanaḥ
parvatāgrād iva mahāṃś campako vāyupīḍitaḥ
pāñcālās tvaritā droṇaṃ samantāt paryavārayan
tathā citrarathaś caiva bhrātṛvyasanakarṣitāḥ
muñcantaḥ śaravarṣāṇi tapānte jaladā iva
vyaśvasūtarathāṃś cakre kumārān kupito raṇe
tathāparaiḥ suniśitair bhallais teṣāṃ mahāyaśāḥ
puṣpāṇīva vicinvan hi sottamāṅgāny apātayat
devāsure purā yuddhe yathā daiteyadānavāḥ
tān nihatya raṇe rājan bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
kārmukaṃ bhrāmayām āsa hemapṛṣṭhaṃ durāsadam
pāñcālān nihatān dṛṣṭvā devakalpān mahārathān
dhṛṣṭadyumno bhṛśaṃ kruddho netrābhyāṃ pātayañ jalam
pāñcālyena raṇe dṛṣṭvā droṇam āvāritaṃ śaraiḥ
saṃchādyamāno bahudhā pārṣatena mahātmanā
tato droṇaṃ mahārāja pāñcālyaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
sa gāḍhaviddho balinā bhāradvājo mahāyaśāḥ
taṃ vai tathāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ parākramī
samutsṛjya dhanus tūrṇam asiṃ jagrāha vīryavān
āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ bhāradvājasya māriṣa
yodhayām āsa samare dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāratham
te hi vaitastikā nāma śarā āsannayodhinaḥ
droṇasya viditā rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnam avākṣipan
avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ bhagnavegaḥ parākramī
vivyādha samare droṇaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
kṣatriyāś ca mahārāja ye cānye tatra sainikāḥ
avaśyaṃ samare droṇo dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃgataḥ
vaśam eṣyati no rājñaḥ pāñcālā iti cukruśuḥ
śiraḥ pracyāvayām āsa phalaṃ pakvaṃ taror iva
tatas te pradrutā vāhā rājaṃs tasya mahātmanaḥ
teṣu pradravamāṇeṣu pāñcālān sṛñjayāṃs tathā
vijitya pāṇḍupāñcālān bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
svaṃ vyūhaṃ punar āsthāya sthiro 'bhavad ariṃdamaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
tato duḥśāsano rājañ śaineyaṃ samupādravat
kirañ śarasahasrāṇi parjanya iva vṛṣṭimān
sa viddhvā sātyakiṃ ṣaṣṭyā tathā ṣoḍaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
sa tu duḥśāsanaṃ vīraḥ sāyakair āvṛṇod bhṛśam
maśakaṃ samanuprāptam ūrṇanābhir ivorṇayā
dṛṣṭvā duḥśāsanaṃ rājā tathā śaraśatācitam
trigartāṃś codayām āsa yuyudhānarathaṃ prati
te 'gacchan yuyudhānasya samīpaṃ krūrakāriṇaḥ
trigartānāṃ trisāhasrā rathā yuddhaviśāradāḥ
sthirāṃ kṛtvā matiṃ yuddhe bhūtvā saṃśaptakā mithaḥ
teṣāṃ prayatatāṃ yuddhe śaravarṣāṇi muñcatām
yodhān pañcaśatān mukhyān agrānīke vyapothayat
te 'patanta hatās tūrṇaṃ śinipravarasāyakaiḥ
mahāmārutavegena rugṇā iva mahādrumāḥ
hayaiś ca kanakāpīḍaiḥ patitais tatra medinī
śaineyaśarasaṃkṛttaiḥ śoṇitaughapariplutaiḥ
aśobhata mahārāja kiṃśukair iva puṣpitaiḥ
te vadhyamānāḥ samare yuyudhānena tāvakāḥ
trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta paṅkamagnā iva dvipāḥ
bhayāt patagarājasya gartānīva mahoragāḥ
hatvā pañcaśatān yodhāñ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
taṃ prayāntaṃ naraśreṣṭhaṃ putro duḥśāsanas tava
vivyādha navabhis tūrṇaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
sa tu taṃ prativivyādha pañcabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
duḥśāsanas tribhir viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ
śaineyas tava putraṃ tu viddhvā pañcabhir āśugaiḥ
tato duḥśāsanaḥ kruddho vṛṣṇivīrāya gacchate
sarvapāraśavīṃ śaktiṃ visasarja jighāṃsayā
tāṃ tu śaktiṃ tadā ghorāṃ tava putrasya sātyakiḥ
ciccheda śatadhā rājan niśitaiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥ
sātyakiṃ daśabhir viddhvā siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ha
śarair agniśikhākārair ājaghāna stanāntare
sarvāyasais tīkṣṇavaktrair aṣṭābhir vivyadhe punaḥ
duḥśāsanas tu viṃśatyā sātyakiṃ pratyavidhyata
sātvato 'pi mahārāja taṃ vivyādha stanāntare
tato 'sya vāhān niśitaiḥ śarair jaghne mahārathaḥ
sārathiṃ ca susaṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
dhvajaṃ ca rathaśaktiṃ ca bhallābhyāṃ paramāstravit
ciccheda viśikhais tīkṣṇais tathobhau pārṣṇisārathī
bhīmasenena hi vadhaḥ sutānāṃ tava bhārata
pratijñātaḥ sabhāmadhye sarveṣām eva saṃyuge
tathā duḥśāsanaṃ jitvā sātyakiḥ saṃyuge prabho
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
kiṃ tasyāṃ mama senāyāṃ nāsan ke cin mahārathāḥ
ye tathā sātyakiṃ yāntaṃ naivāghnan nāpy avārayan
atha vā śūnyam āsīt tad yena yātaḥ sa sātyakiḥ
eko vai bahulāḥ senāḥ pramṛdnan puruṣarṣabhaḥ
kathaṃ ca yudhyamānānām apakrānto mahātmanām
eko bahūnāṃ śaineyas tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
saṃjaya uvāca
rājan senāsamudyogo rathanāgāśvapattimān
tumulas tava sainyānāṃ yugāntasadṛśo 'bhavat
āhṇikeṣu samūheṣu tava sainyasya mānada
tatra devāḥ sma bhāṣante cāraṇāś ca samāgatāḥ
etad antāḥ samūhā vai bhaviṣyanti mahītale
na caiva tādṛśaḥ kaś cid vyūha āsīd viśāṃ pate
caṇḍavātābhipannānāṃ samudrāṇām iva svanaḥ
pārthivānāṃ sametānāṃ bahūny āsan narottama
tvadbale pāṇḍavānāṃ ca sahasrāṇi śatāni ca
saṃrabdhānāṃ pravīrāṇāṃ samare dṛḍhakarmaṇām
tatrāsīt sumahāñ śabdas tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
athākrandad bhīmaseno dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca māriṣa
nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dharmarājaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
praviṣṭāv arisenāṃ hi vīrau mādhavapāṇḍavau
tayor abhāve kuravaḥ kṛtārthāḥ syur vayaṃ jitāḥ
te yūyaṃ sahitā bhūtvā tūrṇam eva balārṇavam
kṣobhayadhvaṃ mahāvegāḥ pavanāḥ sāgaraṃ yathā
bhīmasenena te rājan pāñcālyena ca coditāḥ
ājaghnuḥ kauravān saṃkhye tyaktvāsūn ātmanaḥ priyān
svargārthaṃ mitrakāryārthaṃ nābhyarakṣanta jīvitam
āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā yuddhāyaivopatasthire
hatvā sarvāṇi sainyāni prāyāt sātyakir arjunam
kavacānāṃ prabhās tatra sūryaraśmivicitritāḥ
dṛṣṭīḥ saṃkhye sainikānāṃ pratijaghnuḥ samantataḥ
tathā prayatamāneṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu nirbhayaḥ
sa saṃnipātas tumulas teṣāṃ tasya ca bhārata
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
kaccid duryodhanaḥ sūta nākārṣīt pṛṣṭhato raṇam
ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca saṃnipāto mahāhave
viśeṣato nṛpatinā viṣamaḥ pratibhāti me
eko bahūn samāsādya kaccin nāsīt parāṅmukhaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
rājan saṃgrāmam āścaryaṃ tava putrasya bhārata
ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca śṛṇuṣva gadato 'dbhutam
duryodhanena sahasā pāṇḍavī pṛtanā raṇe
tathā senāṃ kṛtāṃ dṛṣṭvā tava putreṇa kaurava
bhīmasenapurogās taṃ pāñcālāḥ samupādravan
virāṭadrupadau ṣaḍbhiḥ śatena ca śikhaṇḍinam
dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca viṃśatyā dharmaputraṃ ca saptabhiḥ
śataśaś cāparān yodhān sadvipāṃś ca rathān raṇe
na saṃdadhan vimuñcan vā maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ
adṛśyata ripūn nighnañ śikṣayāstrabalena ca
tasya tān nighnataḥ śatrūn hemapṛṣṭhaṃ mahad dhanuḥ
bhallābhyāṃ pāṇḍavo jyeṣṭhas tridhā ciccheda māriṣa
vivyādha cainaṃ bahubhiḥ samyag astaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
varmāṇy āśu samāsādya te bhagnāḥ kṣitim āviśan
tataḥ pramuditāḥ pārthāḥ parivavrur yudhiṣṭhiram
yathā vṛtravadhe devā mudā śakraṃ maharṣibhiḥ
atha duryodhano rājā dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam
tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti rājānaṃ bruvan pāṇḍavam abhyayāt
taṃ tathā vādinaṃ rājaṃs tava putraṃ mahāratham
pratyudyayuḥ pramuditāḥ pāñcālā jayagṛddhinaḥ
tān droṇaḥ pratijagrāha parīpsan yudhi pāṇḍavam
caṇḍavātoddhutān meghān sajalān acalo yathā
tatra rājan mahān āsīt saṃgrāmo bhūrivardhanaḥ
rudrasyākrīḍasaṃkāśaḥ saṃhāraḥ sarvadehinām
saṃjaya uvāca
aparāhṇe mahārāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata
śoṇāśvaṃ ratham āsthāya naravīraḥ samāhitaḥ
samare 'bhyadravat pāṇḍūñ javam āsthāya madhyamam
citrapuṅkhaiḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ kalaśottamasaṃbhavaḥ
varān varān hi yodhānāṃ vicinvann iva bhārata
akrīḍata raṇe rājan bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
tam abhyayād bṛhatkṣatraḥ kekayānāṃ mahārathaḥ
bhrātṝṇāṃ vīrapañcānāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ samarakarkaśaḥ
vimuñcan viśikhāṃs tīkṣṇān ācāryaṃ chādayan bhṛśam
mahāmegho yathā varṣaṃ vimuñcan gandhamādane
tasya droṇo mahārāja svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ sāyakān daśa sapta ca
tāṃs tu droṇadhanurmuktān ghorān āśīviṣopamān
ekaikaṃ daśabhir bāṇair yudhi ciccheda hṛṣṭavat
tasya tal lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā prahasan dvijasattamaḥ
preṣayām āsa viśikhān aṣṭau saṃnataparvaṇaḥ
tān dṛṣṭvā patataḥ śīghraṃ droṇacāpacyutāñ śarān
bṛhatkṣatreṇa tat karma kṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā suduṣkaram
tato droṇo mahārāja kekayaṃ vai viśeṣayan
prāduścakre raṇe divyaṃ brāhmam astraṃ mahātapāḥ
brāhmeṇaiva mahābāhur āhave samudīritam
vivyādha brāhmaṇaṃ ṣaṣṭyā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
taṃ droṇo dvipadāṃ śreṣṭho nārācena samarpayat
kṛṣṇasarpo yathā mukto valmīkaṃ nṛpasattama
tathābhyagān mahīṃ bāṇo bhittvā kaikeyam āhave
so 'tividdho mahārāja droṇenāstravidā bhṛśam
krodhena mahatāviṣṭo vyāvṛtya nayane śubhe
droṇaṃ vivyādha saptatyā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
droṇas tu bahudhā viddho bṛhatkṣatreṇa māriṣa
asṛjad viśikhāṃs tīkṣṇān kekayasya rathaṃ prati
vyākulīkṛtya taṃ droṇo bṛhatkṣatraṃ mahāratham
vyasṛjat sāyakaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ kekayaṃ prati bhārata
sa gāḍhaviddhas tenāśu mahārāja stanāntare
rathāt puruṣaśārdūlaḥ saṃbhinnahṛdayo 'patat
bṛhatkṣatre hate rājan kekayānāṃ mahārathe
śaiśupāliḥ susaṃkruddho yantāram idam abravīt
sārathe yāhi yatraiṣa droṇas tiṣṭhati daṃśitaḥ
vinighnan kekayān sarvān pāñcālānāṃ ca vāhinīm
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā sārathī rathināṃ varam
droṇāya prāpayām āsa kāmbojair javanair hayaiḥ
dhṛṣṭaketuś ca cedīnām ṛṣabho 'tibaloditaḥ
sahasā prāpatad droṇaṃ pataṃga iva pāvakam
so 'bhyavidhyat tato droṇaṃ ṣaṣṭyā sāśvarathadhvajam
punaś cānyaiḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ suptaṃ vyāghraṃ tudann iva
athānyad dhanur ādāya śaiśupālir mahārathaḥ
vivyādha sāyakair droṇaṃ punaḥ suniśitair dṛḍhaiḥ
tasya droṇo hayān hatvā sārathiṃ ca mahābalaḥ
athainaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānāṃ samārpayat
gadāṃ cikṣepa saṃkruddho bhāradvājarathaṃ prati
tām āpatantīṃ sahasā ghorarūpāṃ bhayāvahām
aśmasāramayīṃ gurvīṃ tapanīyavibhūṣitām
sā papāta gadā bhūmau bhāradvājena sāditā
gadāṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭaketur amarṣaṇaḥ
tomaraṃ vyasṛjat tūrṇaṃ śaktiṃ ca kanakojjvalām
tomaraṃ tu tribhir bāṇair droṇaś chittvā mahāmṛdhe
śaktiṃ ciccheda sahasā kṛtahasto mahābalaḥ
tato 'sya viśikhaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vadhārthaṃ vadhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
preṣayām āsa samare bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān
sa tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā hṛdayaṃ cāmitaujasaḥ
abhyagād dharaṇīṃ bāṇo haṃsaḥ padmasaro yathā
pataṃgaṃ hi grasec cāṣo yathā rājan bubhukṣitaḥ
tathā droṇo 'grasac chūro dhṛṣṭaketuṃ mahāmṛdhe
nihate cedirāje tu tat khaṇḍaṃ pitryam āviśat
mahāvyāghro mahāraṇye mṛgaśāvaṃ yathā balī
teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu bhārata
jarāsaṃdhasuto vīraḥ svayaṃ droṇam upādravat
sa tu droṇaṃ mahārāja chādayan sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ
adṛśyam akarot tūrṇaṃ jalado bhāskaraṃ yathā
tasya tal lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ kṣatriyamardanaḥ
vyasṛjat sāyakāṃs tūrṇaṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
chādayitvā raṇe droṇo rathasthaṃ rathināṃ varam
jārāsaṃdhim atho jaghne miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
yo yaḥ sma līyate droṇaṃ taṃ taṃ droṇo 'ntakopamaḥ
ādatta sarvabhūtāni prāpte kāle yathāntakaḥ
tato droṇo maheṣvāso nāma viśrāvya saṃyuge
śarair anekasāhasraiḥ pāṇḍaveyān vyamohayat
tato droṇāṅkitā bāṇāḥ svarṇapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥ
narān nāgān hayāṃś caiva nijaghnuḥ sarvato raṇe
te vadhyamānā droṇena śakreṇeva mahāsurāḥ
samakampanta pāñcālā gāvaḥ śītārditā iva
tato niṣṭānako ghoraḥ pāṇḍavānām ajāyata
mohitāḥ śaravarṣeṇa bhāradvājasya saṃyuge
ūrugrāhagṛhītā hi pāñcālānāṃ mahārathāḥ
cedayaś ca mahārāja sṛñjayāḥ somakās tathā
abhyadravanta saṃhṛṣṭā bhāradvājaṃ yuyutsayā
yatantaḥ puruṣavyāghrāḥ sarvaśaktyā mahādyutim
ninīṣanto raṇe droṇaṃ yamasya sadanaṃ prati
yatamānāṃs tu tān vīrān bhāradvājaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
yamāya preṣayām āsa cedimukhyān viśeṣataḥ
teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu cedimukhyeṣu bhārata
pāñcālāḥ samakampanta droṇasāyakapīḍitāḥ
prākrośan bhīmasenaṃ te dhṛṣṭadyumnarathaṃ prati
dṛṣṭvā droṇasya karmāṇi tathārūpāṇi māriṣa
brāhmaṇena tapo nūnaṃ caritaṃ duścaraṃ mahat
droṇāstram agnisaṃsparśaṃ praviṣṭāḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
yathābalaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathāsattvaṃ mahādyutiḥ
teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā kṣatradharmā vyavasthitaḥ
sa saṃrabdhataro bhūtvā droṇaḥ kṣatriyamardanaḥ
tatrādhāya śaraṃ tīkṣṇaṃ bhāraghnaṃ vimalaṃ dṛḍham
ākarṇapūrṇam ācāryo balavān abhyavāsṛjat
sa hatvā kṣatradharmāṇaṃ jagāma dharaṇītalam
atha droṇaṃ samārohac cekitāno mahārathaḥ
sa droṇaṃ daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntare
tasyācāryaḥ ṣoḍaśabhir avidhyad dakṣiṇaṃ bhujam
dhvajaṃ ṣoḍaśabhir bāṇair yantāraṃ cāsya saptabhiḥ
tasya sūte hate te 'śvā ratham ādāya vidrutāḥ
samare śarasaṃvītā bhāradvājena māriṣa
cekitānarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidrutaṃ hatasārathim
pāñcālān pāṇḍavāṃś caiva mahad bhayam athāviśat
tān sametān raṇe śūrāṃś cedipāñcālasṛñjayān
samantād drāvayan droṇo bahv aśobhata māriṣa
ākarṇapalitaḥ śyāmo vayasāśītikāt paraḥ
raṇe paryacarad droṇo vṛddhaḥ ṣoḍaśavarṣavat
lubdho 'yaṃ kṣatriyān hanti vyāghraḥ kṣudramṛgān iva
kṛcchrān duryodhano lokān pāpaḥ prāpsyati durmatiḥ
yasya lobhād vinihatāḥ samare kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
śataśaḥ śerate bhūmau nikṛttā govṛṣā iva
rudhireṇa parītāṅgāḥ śvasṛgālādanīkṛtāḥ
evam uktvā mahārāja drupado 'kṣauhiṇīpatiḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
vyūheṣv āloḍyamāneṣu pāṇḍavānāṃ tatas tataḥ
sudūram anvayuḥ pārthāḥ pāñcālāḥ saha somakaiḥ
vartamāne tathā raudre saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇe
pāñcāleṣu ca kṣīṇeṣu vadhyamāneṣu pāṇḍuṣu
nāpaśyac charaṇaṃ kiṃ cid dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
tatrāvekṣya diśaḥ sarvāḥ savyasācididṛkṣayā
yudhiṣṭhiro dadarśātha naiva pārthaṃ na mādhavam
so 'paśyan naraśārdūlaṃ vānararṣabhalakṣaṇam
gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣam aśṛṇvan vyathitendriyaḥ
apaśyan sātyakiṃ cāpi vṛṣṇīnāṃ pravaraṃ ratham
cintayābhiparītāṅgo dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
nādhyagacchat tadā śāntiṃ tāv apaśyan nararṣabhau
lokopakrośabhīrutvād dharmarājo mahāyaśāḥ
padavīṃ preṣitaś caiva phalgunasya mayā raṇe
śaineyaḥ sātyakiḥ satyo mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ
tad idaṃ hy ekam evāsīd dvidhā jātaṃ mamādya vai
sātyakiś ca hi me jñeyaḥ pāṇḍavaś ca dhanaṃjayaḥ
sātyakiṃ preṣayitvā tu pāṇḍavasya padānugam
sātvatasyāpi kaṃ yuddhe preṣayiṣye padānugam
kariṣyāmi prayatnena bhrātur anveṣaṇaṃ yadi
bhrātur anveṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
lokāpavādabhīrutvāt so 'haṃ pārthaṃ vṛkodaram
padavīṃ preṣayiṣyāmi mādhavasya mahātmanaḥ
praviṣṭo bhāratīṃ senāṃ makaraḥ sāgaraṃ yathā
asau hi śrūyate śabdaḥ śūrāṇām anivartinām
mithaḥ saṃyudhyamānānāṃ vṛṣṇivīreṇa dhīmatā
śakto hy eṣa raṇe yattān pṛthivyāṃ sarvadhanvinaḥ
svabāhubalam āsthāya prativyūhitum añjasā
yasya bāhubalaṃ sarve samāśritya mahātmanaḥ
vanavāsān nivṛttāḥ sma na ca yuddheṣu nirjitāḥ
ito gate bhīmasene sātvataṃ prati pāṇḍave
kāmaṃ tv aśocanīyau tau raṇe sātvataphalgunau
rakṣitau vāsudevena svayaṃ cāstraviśāradau
avaśyaṃ tu mayā kāryam ātmanaḥ śokanāśanam
tasmād bhīmaṃ niyokṣyāmi sātvatasya padānugam
tataḥ pratikṛtaṃ manye vidhānaṃ sātyakiṃ prati
dharmarājavacaḥ śrutvā sārathir hayakovidaḥ
rathaṃ hemapariṣkāraṃ bhīmāntikam upānayat
kaśmalaṃ prāviśad rājā bahu tatra samādiśan
naivādrākṣaṃ na cāśrauṣaṃ tava kaśmalam īdṛśam
purā hi duḥkhadīrṇānāṃ bhavān gatir abhūd dhi naḥ
uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha rājendra śādhi kiṃ karavāṇi te
ājñāpaya kuruśreṣṭha mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
tam abravīd aśrupūrṇaḥ kṛṣṇasarpa iva śvasan
bhīmasenam idaṃ vākyaṃ pramlānavadano nṛpaḥ
yathā śaṅkhasya nirghoṣaḥ pāñcajanyasya śrūyate
nūnam adya hataḥ śete tava bhrātā dhanaṃjayaḥ
yasya sattvavato vīryam upajīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ
yaṃ bhayeṣv abhigacchanti sahasrākṣam ivāmarāḥ
sa śūraḥ saindhavaprepsur anvayād bhāratīṃ camūm
śyāmo yuvā guḍākeśo darśanīyo mahābhujaḥ
arjunārthaṃ mahābāho sātvatasya ca kāraṇāt
vardhate haviṣevāgnir idhyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
taṃ viddhi puruṣavyāghraṃ sātvataṃ ca mahāratham
sa taṃ mahārathaṃ paścād anuyātas tavānujam
tam apaśyan mahābāhum ahaṃ vindāmi kaśmalam
tasmāt kṛṣṇo raṇe nūnaṃ yudhyate yuddhakovidaḥ
yasya vīryavato vīryam upajīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ
sātyakiś ca mahāvīryaḥ kartavyaṃ yadi manyase
vacanaṃ mama dharmajña jyeṣṭho bhrātā bhavāmi te
na te 'rjunas tathā jñeyo jñātavyaḥ sātyakir yathā
cikīrṣur matpriyaṃ pārtha prayātaḥ savyasācinaḥ
padavīṃ durgamāṃ ghorām agamyām akṛtātmabhiḥ
brahmeśānendravaruṇān avahad yaḥ purā rathaḥ
ājñāṃ tu śirasā bibhrad eṣa gacchāmi mā śucaḥ
sametya tān naravyāghrāṃs tava dāsyāmi saṃvidam
saṃjaya uvāca
dhṛṣṭadyumnāya balavān suhṛdbhyaś ca punaḥ punaḥ
dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ cedam āha bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
viditaṃ te mahābāho yathā droṇo mahārathaḥ
na ca me gamane kṛtyaṃ tādṛk pārṣata vidyate
yādṛśaṃ rakṣaṇe rājñaḥ kāryam ātyayikaṃ hi naḥ
prayāsye tatra yatrāsau mumūrṣuḥ saindhavaḥ sthitaḥ
etad dhi sarvakāryāṇāṃ paramaṃ kṛtyam āhave
tam abravīn mahārāja dhṛṣṭadyumno vṛkodaram
īpsitena mahābāho gaccha pārthāvicārayan
nāhatvā samare droṇo dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ kathaṃ cana
tato nikṣipya rājānaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnāya pāṇḍavaḥ
āghrātaś ca tathā mūrdhni śrāvitaś cāśiṣaḥ śubhāḥ
bhīmaseno mahābāhuḥ kavacī śubhakuṇḍalī
sāṅgadaḥ satanutrāṇaḥ saśarī rathināṃ varaḥ
pītaraktāsitasitair vāsobhiś ca suveṣṭitaḥ
kaṇṭhatrāṇena ca babhau sendrāyudha ivāmbudaḥ
pāñcajanyaravo ghoraḥ punar āsīd viśāṃ pate
taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ trailokyatrāsanaṃ mahat
eṣa vṛṣṇipravīreṇa dhmātaḥ salilajo bhṛśam
pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca vinādayati śaṅkharāṭ
nūnam āryā mahat kuntī pāpam adya nidarśanam
muhyantīva hi me sarvā dhanaṃjayadidṛkṣayā
diśaḥ sapradiśaḥ pārtha sātvatasya ca kāraṇāt
bhṛśaṃ sa prahito bhrātrā bhrātā bhrātuḥ priyaṃkaraḥ
āhatya dundubhiṃ bhīmaḥ śaṅkhaṃ pradhmāya cāsakṛt
vinadya siṃhanādaṃ ca jyāṃ vikarṣan punaḥ punaḥ
tam ūhur javanā dāntā vikurvāṇā hayottamāḥ
viśokenābhisaṃyattā manomārutaraṃhasaḥ
ārujan virujan pārtho jyāṃ vikarṣaṃś ca pāṇinā
so 'vakarṣan vikarṣaṃś ca senāgraṃ samaloḍayat
taṃ prayāntaṃ mahābāhuṃ pāñcālāḥ sahasomakāḥ
pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayuḥ śūrā maghavantam ivāmarāḥ
taṃ sasenā mahārāja sodaryāḥ paryavārayan
duḥśalaś citrasenaś ca kuṇḍabhedī viviṃśatiḥ
vṛndārakaḥ suhastaś ca suṣeṇo dīrghalocanaḥ
vividhai rathināṃ śreṣṭhāḥ saha sainyaiḥ sahānugaiḥ
saṃyattāḥ samare śūrā bhīmasenam upādravan
tān samīkṣya tu kaunteyo bhīmasenaḥ parākramī
te mahāstrāṇi divyāni tatra vīrā adarśayan
vārayantaḥ śarair bhīmaṃ meghāḥ sūryam ivoditam
sa tān atītya vegena droṇānīkam upādravat
agrataś ca gajānīkaṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
so 'cireṇaiva kālena tad gajānīkam āśugaiḥ
trāsitāḥ śarabhasyeva garjitena vane mṛgāḥ
punaś cātītya vegena droṇānīkam upādravat
lalāṭe 'tāḍayac cainaṃ nārācena smayann iva
ūrdhvaraśmir ivādityo vibabhau tatra pāṇḍavaḥ
sa manyamānas tv ācāryo mamāyaṃ phalguno yathā
bhīmaḥ kariṣyate pūjām ity uvāca vṛkodaram
bhīmasena na te śakyaṃ praveṣṭum arivāhinīm
yadi te so 'nujaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ praviṣṭo 'numate mama
anīkaṃ na tu śakyaṃ bhoḥ praveṣṭum iha vai tvayā
kruddhaḥ provāca vai droṇaṃ raktatāmrekṣaṇaḥ śvasan
praviṣṭaḥ sa hi durdharṣaḥ śakrasyāpi viśed balam
yena vai paramāṃ pūjāṃ kurvatā mānito hy asi
nārjuno 'haṃ ghṛṇī droṇa bhīmaseno 'smi te ripuḥ
iti manyāmahe sarve bhavantaṃ praṇatāḥ sthitāḥ
eṣa te sadṛśaṃ śatroḥ karma bhīmaḥ karomy aham
athodbhrāmya gadāṃ bhīmaḥ kāladaṇḍam ivāntakaḥ
droṇāyāvasṛjad rājan sa rathād avapupluve
sāśvasūtadhvajaṃ yānaṃ droṇasyāpothayat tadā
prāmṛdnāc ca bahūn yodhān vāyur vṛkṣān ivaujasā
anyaṃ ca ratham āsthāya droṇaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
tataḥ kruddho mahārāja bhīmasenaḥ parākramī
agrataḥ syandanānīkaṃ śaravarṣair avākirat
te vadhyamānāḥ samare tava putrā mahārathāḥ
bhīmaṃ bhīmabalaṃ yuddhe 'yodhayaṃs tu jayaiṣiṇaḥ
tato duḥśāsanaḥ kruddho rathaśaktiṃ samākṣipat
sarvapāraśavīṃ tīkṣṇāṃ jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍunandanam
āpatantīṃ mahāśaktiṃ tava putrapracoditām
athānyair niśitair bāṇaiḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kuṇḍabhedinam
suṣeṇaṃ dīrghanetraṃ ca tribhis trīn avadhīd balī
tato vṛndārakaṃ vīraṃ kurūṇāṃ kīrtivardhanam
putrāṇāṃ tava vīrāṇāṃ yudhyatām avadhīt punaḥ
vadhyamānā mahārāja putrās tava balīyasā
bhīmaṃ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ samantāt paryavārayan
tataḥ sudarśanaṃ vīraṃ putraṃ te bharatarṣabha
vivyādha samare tūrṇaṃ sa papāta mamāra ca
so 'cireṇaiva kālena tad rathānīkam āśugaiḥ
diśaḥ sarvāḥ samabhyasya vyadhamat pāṇḍunandanaḥ
vadhyamānāś ca samare putrās tava viśāṃ pate
prādravan sarathāḥ sarve bhīmasenabhayārditāḥ
anuyāya tu kaunteyaḥ putrāṇāṃ te mahad balam
vadhyamānā mahārāja bhīmasenena tāvakāḥ
siṃhanādaravaṃ cakre bāhuśabdaṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥ
talaśabdaṃ ca sumahat kṛtvā bhīmo mahābalaḥ
vyatītya rathinaś cāpi droṇānīkam upādravat
saṃjaya uvāca
tam uttīrṇaṃ rathānīkāt tamaso bhāskaraṃ yathā
didhārayiṣur ācāryaḥ śaravarṣair avākirat
pibann iva śaraughāṃs tān droṇacāpavarātigān
taṃ mṛdhe vegam āsthāya paraṃ paramadhanvinaḥ
sa tathā saṃvṛto bhīmaḥ prahasann iva bhārata
udayacchad gadāṃ tebhyo ghorāṃ tāṃ siṃhavan nadan
sendrāśanir ivendreṇa praviddhā saṃhatātmanā
ghoṣeṇa mahatā rājan pūrayitveva medinīm
jvalantī tejasā bhīmā trāsayām āsa te sutān
tāṃ patantīṃ mahāvegāṃ dṛṣṭvā tejobhisaṃvṛtām
prādravaṃs tāvakāḥ sarve nadanto bhairavān ravān
taṃ ca śabdam asaṃsahyaṃ tasyāḥ saṃlakṣya māriṣa
sa tān vidrāvya kaunteyaḥ saṃkhye 'mitrān durāsadaḥ
suparṇa iva vegena pakṣirāḍ atyagāc camūm
tathā taṃ viprakurvāṇaṃ rathayūthapayūthapam
bhāradvājo mahārāja bhīmasenaṃ samabhyayāt
droṇas tu samare bhīmaṃ vārayitvā śarormibhiḥ
akarot sahasā nādaṃ pāṇḍūnāṃ bhayam ādadhat
droṇasya ca mahārāja bhīmasya ca mahātmanaḥ
yadā tu viśikhais tīkṣṇair droṇacāpaviniḥsṛtaiḥ
vadhyante samare vīrāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
tato rathād avaplutya vegam āsthāya pāṇḍavaḥ
yathā hi govṛṣo varṣaṃ pratigṛhṇāti līlayā
tathā bhīmo naravyāghraḥ śaravarṣaṃ samagrahīt
sa vadhyamānaḥ samare rathaṃ droṇasya māriṣa
īṣāyāṃ pāṇinā gṛhya pracikṣepa mahābalaḥ
ratham anyaṃ samāsthāya vyūhadvāram upāyayau
tasmin kṣaṇe tasya yantā tūrṇam aśvān acodayat
tataḥ svaratham āsthāya bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
sa mṛdnan kṣatriyān ājau vāto vṛkṣān ivoddhataḥ
bhojānīkaṃ samāsādya hārdikyenābhirakṣitam
saṃtrāsayann anīkāni talaśabdena māriṣa
ajayat sarvasainyāni śārdūla iva govṛṣān
bhojānīkam atikramya kāmbojānāṃ ca vāhinīm
tathā mlecchagaṇāṃś cānyān bahūn yuddhaviśāradān
sātyakiṃ cāpi saṃprekṣya yudhyamānaṃ nararṣabham
bhīmaseno mahārāja draṣṭukāmo dhanaṃjayam
atītya samare yodhāṃs tāvakān pāṇḍunandanaḥ
saindhavasya vadhārthaṃ hi parākrāntaṃ parākramī
arjunaṃ tatra dṛṣṭvātha cukrośa mahato ravān
taṃ tu tasya mahānādaṃ pārthaḥ śuśrāva nardataḥ
tataḥ pārtho mahānādaṃ muñcan vai mādhavaś ca ha
abhyayātāṃ mahārāja nardantau govṛṣāv iva
vāsudevārjunau śrutvā ninādaṃ tasya śuṣmiṇaḥ
punaḥ punaḥ praṇadatāṃ didṛkṣantau vṛkodaram
aprīyata mahārāja dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
viśokaś cābhavad rājā śrutvā taṃ ninadaṃ mahat
dhanaṃjayasya ca raṇe jayam āśāstavān vibhuḥ
smitaṃ kṛtvā mahābāhur dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
hṛdgataṃ manasā prāha dhyātvā dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
dattā bhīma tvayā saṃvit kṛtaṃ guruvacas tathā
na hi teṣāṃ jayo yuddhe yeṣāṃ dveṣṭāsi pāṇḍava
diṣṭyā jīvati saṃgrāme savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ
diṣṭyā ca kuśalī vīraḥ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
diṣṭyā śṛṇomi garjantau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
yena śakraṃ raṇe jitvā tarpito havyavāhanaḥ
sa hantā dviṣatāṃ saṃkhye diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ
yasya bāhubalaṃ sarve vayam āśritya jīvitāḥ
sa hantā ripusainyānāṃ diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ
nirjitā rathinaikena diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati
yo 'jayan matsyanagare diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati
kālakeyasahasrāṇi caturdaśa mahāraṇe
yo 'vadhīd bhujavīryeṇa diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati
jitavān yo 'stravīryeṇa diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati
kirīṭamālī balavāñ śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ
mama priyaś ca satataṃ diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ
putraśokābhisaṃtaptaś cikīrṣuḥ karma duṣkaram
jayadrathavadhānveṣī pratijñāṃ kṛtavān hi yaḥ
kaccit tīrṇapratijñaṃ hi vāsudevena rakṣitam
dṛṣṭvā saindhavakaṃ saṃkhye śamam asmāsu dhāsyati
dṛṣṭvā vinihatān bhrātṝn bhīmasenena saṃyuge
dṛṣṭvā cānyān bahūn yodhān pātitān dharaṇītale
śeṣasya rakṣaṇārthaṃ ca saṃdhāsyati suyodhanaḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
tathā tu nardamānaṃ taṃ bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
meghastanitanirghoṣaṃ ke vīrāḥ paryavārayan
na hi paśyāmy ahaṃ taṃ vai triṣu lokeṣu saṃjaya
na hi paśyāmy ahaṃ tāta yas tiṣṭheta raṇājire
rathaṃ rathena yo hanyāt kuñjaraṃ kuñjareṇa ca
kas tasya samare sthātā sākṣād api śatakratuḥ
pradhakṣyato raṇamukhe ke vīrāḥ pramukhe sthitāḥ
kālyamānān hi me putrān bhīmenāvekṣya saṃyuge
kāleneva prajāḥ sarvāḥ ke bhīmaṃ paryavārayan
ke śūrāḥ paryavartanta tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
saṃjaya uvāca
tathā tu nardamānaṃ taṃ bhīmasenaṃ mahāratham
vyākṣipan balavac cāpam atimātram amarṣaṇaḥ
karṇas tu yuddham ākāṅkṣan darśayiṣyan balaṃ balī
prāvepann iva gātrāṇi karṇabhīmasamāgame
rathināṃ sādināṃ caiva tayoḥ śrutvā talasvanam
bhīmasenasya ninadaṃ ghoraṃ śrutvā raṇājire
khaṃ ca bhūmiṃ ca saṃbaddhāṃ menire kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
punar ghoreṇa nādena pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ
samare sarvayodhānāṃ dhanūṃṣy abhyapatan kṣitau
vitrastāni ca sarvāṇi śakṛnmūtraṃ prasusruvuḥ
vāhanāni mahārāja babhūvur vimanāṃsi ca
prādurāsan nimittāni ghorāṇi ca bahūni ca
tataḥ karṇas tu viṃśatyā śarāṇāṃ bhīmam ārdayat
vivyādha cāsya tvaritaḥ sūtaṃ pañcabhir āśugaiḥ
sāyakānāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā kṣiprakārī mahābalaḥ
tasya karṇo maheṣvāsaḥ sāyakāṃś caturo 'kṣipat
asaṃprāptāṃs tu tān bhīmaḥ sāyakair nataparvabhiḥ
ciccheda bahudhā rājan darśayan pāṇilāghavam
taṃ karṇaś chādayām āsa śaravrātair anekaśaḥ
saṃchādyamānaḥ karṇena bahudhā pāṇḍunandanaḥ
ciccheda cāpaṃ karṇasya muṣṭideśe mahārathaḥ
athānyad dhanur ādāya sajyaṃ kṛtvā ca sūtajaḥ
vivyādha samare bhīmaṃ bhīmakarmā mahārathaḥ
tasya bhīmo bhṛśaṃ kruddhas trīñ śarān nataparvaṇaḥ
dhātuprasyandinaḥ śailād yathā gairikarājayaḥ
kiṃ cid vicalitaḥ karṇaḥ suprahārābhipīḍitaḥ
sasāyakaṃ dhanuḥ kṛtvā bhīmaṃ vivyādha māriṣa
cikṣepa ca punar bāṇāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
sa chādyamānaḥ sahasā karṇena dṛḍhadhanvinā
dhanurjyām acchinat tūrṇam utsmayan pāṇḍunandanaḥ
sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena prāhiṇod yamasādanam
vāhāṃś ca caturaḥ saṃkhye vyasūṃś cakre mahārathaḥ
hatāśvāt tu rathāt karṇaḥ samāplutya viśāṃ pate
syandanaṃ vṛṣasenasya samārohan mahārathaḥ
nirjitya tu raṇe karṇaṃ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
tasya taṃ ninadaṃ śrutvā prahṛṣṭo 'bhūd yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
karṇaṃ ca nirjitaṃ matvā bhīmasenena bhārata
samantāc chaṅkhaninadaṃ pāṇḍusenākarot tadā
śatrusenādhvaniṃ śrutvā tāvakā hy api nānadan
gāṇḍīvaṃ prākṣipat pārthaḥ kṛṣṇo 'py abjam avādayat
aśrūyata mahārāja sarvasainyeṣu bhārata
mṛdupūrvaṃ ca rādheyo dṛḍhapūrvaṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
tūrṇam abhyapatad droṇaṃ manomārutavegavān
arjuno bhīmasenaś ca sātyakiś cāparājitaḥ
saṃprāptāḥ sindhurājasya samīpam arikarśanāḥ
vyāyacchanti ca tatrāpi sarva evāparājitāḥ
yadi tāvad raṇe pārtho vyatikrānto mahārathaḥ
kathaṃ sātyakibhīmābhyāṃ vyatikrānto 'si mānada
āścaryabhūtaṃ loke 'smin samudrasyeva śoṣaṇam
nāśa eva tu me nūnaṃ mandabhāgyasya saṃyuge
yatra tvāṃ puruṣavyāghram atikrāntās trayo rathāḥ
tad bravītu bhavān kṣipraṃ sādhu tat saṃvidhīyatām
droṇa uvāca
cintyaṃ bahu mahārāja kṛtyaṃ yat tatra me śṛṇu
trayo hi samatikrāntāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
yāvad eva bhayaṃ paścāt tāvad eṣāṃ puraḥsaram
sā purastāc ca paścāc ca gṛhītā bhāratī camūḥ
na sabhāyāṃ jayo vṛtto nāpi tatra parājayaḥ
yān sma tān glahate ghorāñ śakuniḥ kurusaṃsadi
akṣān saṃmanyamānaḥ sa prā kśarās te durāsadāḥ
senāṃ durodaraṃ viddhi śarān akṣān viśāṃ pate
atra sarve mahārāja tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ
tatra no glahamānānāṃ dhruvau tāta jayājayau
tatra yāhi svayaṃ śīghraṃ tāṃś ca rakṣasva rakṣiṇaḥ
ihaiva tv aham āsiṣye preṣayiṣyāmi cāparān
nirotsyāmi ca pāñcālān sahitān pāṇḍusṛñjayaiḥ
tato duryodhanaḥ prāyāt tūrṇam ācāryaśāsanāt
udyamyātmānam ugrāya karmaṇe sapadānugaḥ
tau hi pūrvaṃ mahārāja vāritau kṛtavarmaṇā
tvaritas tvaramāṇābhyāṃ bhrātṛbhyāṃ bhārato balī
yudhāmanyus tu saṃkruddhaḥ śarāṃs triṃśatam āyasān
jaghāna caturaś cāśvān ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī
uttamaujā hatāśvas tu hatasūtaś ca saṃyuge
sa rathaṃ prāpya taṃ bhrātur duryodhanahayāñ śaraiḥ
bahubhis tāḍayām āsa te hatāḥ prāpatan bhuvi
yudhāmanyur dhanuḥ śīghraṃ śarāvāpaṃ ca saṃyuge
hatāśvasūtāt sa rathād avaplutya mahārathaḥ
gadām ādāya te putraḥ pāñcālyāv abhyadhāvata
gadayā pothayām āsa sāśvasūtadhvajaṃ raṇe
hatvā cainaṃ sa putras te hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
madrarājarathaṃ tūrṇam āruroha paraṃtapaḥ
pāñcālānāṃ tu mukhyau tau rājaputrau mahābalau
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
arjunasya rathopānte kīdṛśaḥ so 'bhavad raṇaḥ
pūrvaṃ hi nirjitaḥ karṇo bhīmasenena saṃyuge
kathaṃ bhūyas tu rādheyo bhīmam āgān mahārathaḥ
bhīmo vā sūtatanayaṃ pratyudyātaḥ kathaṃ raṇe
mahārathasamākhyātaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pravaraṃ ratham
bhīṣmadroṇāv atikramya dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
kathaṃ karṇaṃ yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhīmo 'yudhyata saṃyuge
kathaṃ nu tāv ayudhyetāṃ sūtaputravṛkodarau
bhrātṛtvaṃ darśitaṃ pūrvaṃ ghṛṇī cāpi sa sūtajaḥ
bhīmo vā sūtaputreṇa smaran vairaṃ purā kṛtam
karṇo jeṣyati saṃgrāme sahitān pāṇḍavān iti
sa kathaṃ bhīmakarmāṇaṃ bhīmasenam ayudhyata
yaṃ samāśritya putrair me kṛtaṃ vairaṃ mahārathaiḥ
taṃ sūtatanayaṃ tāta kathaṃ bhīmo hy ayodhayat
anekān viprakārāṃś ca sūtaputrasamudbhavān
smaramāṇaḥ kathaṃ bhīmo yuyudhe sūtasūnunā
yo 'jayat pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ rathenaikena vīryavān
yo jātaḥ kuṇḍalābhyāṃ ca kavacena sahaiva ca
yathā tayor yuddham abhūd yaś cāsīd vijayī tayoḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
iyeṣa gantuṃ yatrāstāṃ vīrau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
abhyavarṣan mahārāja megho vṛṣṭyeva parvatam
ājuhāva raṇe yāntaṃ bhīmam ādhirathis tadā
bhīmasenas tadāhvānaṃ karṇān nāmarṣayad yudhi
dvairathe daṃśitaṃ yattaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
vidhitsuḥ kalahasyāntaṃ jighāṃsuḥ karṇam akṣiṇot
taṃ ca hatvetarān sarvān hantukāmo mahābalaḥ
tasmai prāsṛjad ugrāṇi vividhāni paraṃtapaḥ
amarṣī pāṇḍavaḥ kruddhaḥ śaravarṣāṇi māriṣa
tasya tānīṣuvarṣāṇi mattadviradagāminaḥ
sūtaputro 'stramāyābhir agrasat sumahāyaśāḥ
sa yathāvan mahārāja vidyayā vai supūjitaḥ
ācāryavan maheṣvāsaḥ karṇaḥ paryacarad raṇe
tan nāmṛṣyata kaunteyaḥ karṇasya smitam āhave
yudhyamāneṣu vīreṣu paśyatsu ca samantataḥ
taṃ bhīmasenaḥ saṃprāptaṃ vatsadantaiḥ stanāntare
sūtaṃ tu sūtaputrasya supuṅkhair niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
karṇo jāmbūnadair jālaiḥ saṃchannān vātaraṃhasaḥ
vivyādha turagān vīraḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
tato bāṇamayaṃ jālaṃ bhīmasenarathaṃ prati
karṇena vihitaṃ rājan nimeṣārdhād adṛśyata
sarathaḥ sadhvajas tatra sasūtaḥ pāṇḍavas tadā
prācchādyata mahārāja karṇacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
tasya karṇaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā vyadhamat kavacaṃ dṛḍham
kruddhaś cāpy ahanat pārśve nārācair marmabhedibhiḥ
tato 'cintya mahāvegān karṇakārmukaniḥsṛtān
samāśliṣyad asaṃbhrāntaḥ sūtaputraṃ vṛkodaraḥ
sa karṇacāpaprabhavān iṣūn āśīviṣopamān
bibhrad bhīmo mahārāja na jagāma vyathāṃ raṇe
vivyādha samare karṇaṃ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
bhīmasenaṃ mahābāhuṃ saindhavasya vadhaiṣiṇam
mṛdupūrvaṃ ca rādheyo bhīmam ājāv ayodhayat
taṃ bhīmaseno nāmṛṣyad avamānam amarṣaṇaḥ
te śarāḥ preṣitā rājan bhīmasenena saṃyuge
nipetuḥ sarvato bhīmāḥ kūjanta iva pakṣiṇaḥ
hemapuṅkhā mahārāja bhīmasenadhanuścyutāḥ
abhyadravaṃs te rādheyaṃ vṛkāḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā
karṇas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭhaś chādyamānaḥ samantataḥ
rājan vyasṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi saṃyuge
tasya tān aśaniprakhyān iṣūn samaraśobhinaḥ
punaś ca śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata
tatra bhārata bhīmaṃ tu dṛṣṭavantaḥ sma sāyakaiḥ
samācitatanuṃ saṃkhye śvāvidhaṃ śalalair iva
hemapuṅkhāñ śilādhautān karṇacāpacyutāñ śarān
dadhāra samare vīraḥ svaraśmīn iva bhāskaraḥ
tapanīyanibhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ palāśa iva kānane
tat tu bhīmo mahārāja karṇasya caritaṃ raṇe
nāmṛṣyata maheṣvāsaḥ krodhād udvṛtya cakṣuṣī
sa karṇaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānāṃ samārpayat
mahīdharam iva śvetaṃ gūḍhapādair viṣolbaṇaiḥ
taṃ vivyādha punar bhīmaḥ ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhir eva ca
marmasv amaravikrāntaḥ sūtaputraṃ mahāraṇe
tataḥ karṇasya saṃkruddho bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān
ciccheda kārmukaṃ tūrṇaṃ sarvopakaraṇāni ca
jaghāna caturaś cāśvān sūtaṃ ca tvaritaḥ śaraiḥ
nārācair arkaraśmyābhaiḥ karṇaṃ vivyādha corasi
te jagmur dharaṇīṃ sarve karṇaṃ nirbhidya māriṣa
yathā hi jaladaṃ bhittvā rājan sūryasya raśmayaḥ
tathā puruṣamānī sa pratyapāyād rathāntaram
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
yasmiñ jayāśā satataṃ putrāṇāṃ mama saṃjaya
taṃ dṛṣṭvā vimukhaṃ saṃkhye kiṃ nu duryodhano 'bravīt
karṇo vā samare tāta kim akārṣīd ataḥ param
saṃjaya uvāca
bhīmasenaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā jvalantam iva pāvakam
abhyayāt pāṇḍavaṃ karṇo vātoddhūta ivārṇavaḥ
kruddham ādhirathiṃ dṛṣṭvā putrās tava viśāṃ pate
cāpaśabdaṃ mahat kṛtvā talaśabdaṃ ca bhairavam
punar eva tato rājan mahān āsīt sudāruṇaḥ
vimardaḥ sūtaputrasya bhīmasya ca viśāṃ pate
saṃrabdhau hi mahābāhū parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
anyonyam īkṣāṃ cakrāte dahantāv iva locanaiḥ
vyāghrāv iva susaṃrabdhau śyenāv iva ca śīghragau
tato bhīmaḥ smaran kleśān akṣadyūte vane 'pi ca
virāṭanagare caiva prāptaṃ duḥkham ariṃdamaḥ
rāṣṭrāṇāṃ sphītaratnānāṃ haraṇaṃ ca tavātmajaiḥ
satataṃ ca parikleśān saputreṇa tvayā kṛtān
kṛṣṇāyāś ca parikleśaṃ sabhāmadhye durātmabhiḥ
narakaṃ patitāḥ pārthāḥ sarve ṣaṇḍhatilopamāḥ
dāsībhogena kṛṣṇāṃ ca bhoktukāmāḥ sutās tava
yac cāpi tān pravrajataḥ kṛṣṇājinanivāsinaḥ
paruṣāṇy uktavān karṇaḥ sabhāyāṃ saṃnidhau tava
tṛṇīkṛtya ca yat pārthāṃs tava putro vavalga ha
bālyāt prabhṛti cārighnas tāni duḥkhāni cintayan
cāpaṃ bharataśārdūlas tyaktātmā karṇam abhyayāt
bhānumadbhiḥ śilādhautair bhānoḥ pracchādayat prabhām
tataḥ prahasyādhirathis tūrṇam asyañ śitāñ śarān
mahāratho mahābāhur mahāvegair mahābalaḥ
vivyādhādhirathir bhīmaṃ navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
sa tottrair iva mātaṅgo vāryamāṇaḥ patatribhiḥ
abhyadhāvad asaṃbhrāntaḥ sūtaputraṃ vṛkodaraḥ
tam āpatantaṃ vegena rabhasaṃ pāṇḍavarṣabham
tataḥ pradhmāpya jalajaṃ bherīśatanināditam
akṣubhyata balaṃ harṣād uddhūta iva sāgaraḥ
tad uddhūtaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭva rathanāgāśvapattimat
bhīmaḥ karṇaṃ samāsādya chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
aśvān ṛśyasavarṇāṃs tu haṃsavarṇair hayottamaiḥ
vyāmiśrayad raṇe karṇaḥ pāṇḍavaṃ chādayañ śaraiḥ
ṛśyavarṇān hayān karkair miśrān mārutaraṃhasaḥ
nirīkṣya tava putrāṇāṃ hāhākṛtam abhūd balam
te hayā bahv aśobhanta miśritā vātaraṃhasaḥ
sitāsitā mahārāja yathā vyomni balāhakāḥ
saṃrabdhau krodhatāmrākṣau prekṣya karṇavṛkodarau
saṃtrastāḥ samakampanta tvadīyānāṃ mahārathāḥ
yamarāṣṭropamaṃ ghoram āsīd āyodhanaṃ tayoḥ
durdarśaṃ bharataśreṣṭha pretarājapuraṃ yathā
samājam iva tac citraṃ prekṣamāṇā mahārathāḥ
nālakṣayañ jayaṃ vyaktam ekaikasya nivāraṇe
tayoḥ praikṣanta saṃmardaṃ saṃnikṛṣṭamahāstrayoḥ
chādayantau hi śatrughnāv anyonyaṃ sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ
śarajālāvṛtaṃ vyoma cakrāte śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
tāv anyonyaṃ jighāṃsantau śarais tīkṣṇair mahārathau
prekṣaṇīyatarāv āstāṃ vṛṣṭimantāv ivāmbudau
suvarṇavikṛtān bāṇān pramuñcantāv ariṃdamau
tābhyāṃ muktā vyakāśanta kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥ
paṅktyaḥ śaradi mattānāṃ sārasānām ivāmbare
saṃsaktaṃ sūtaputreṇa dṛṣṭvā bhīmam ariṃdamam
atibhāram amanyetāṃ bhīme kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
tatrādhirathibhīmābhyāṃ śarair muktair dṛḍhāhatāḥ
kṛto mahān mahārāja putrāṇāṃ te janakṣayaḥ
manuṣyāśvagajānāṃ ca śarīrair gatajīvitaiḥ
kṣaṇena bhūmiḥ saṃjajñe saṃvṛtā bharatarṣabha
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
vārayed yo raṇe karṇaḥ sayakṣāsuramānavān
sa kathaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe bhrājamānam iva śriyā
nātarat saṃyuge tāta tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
kathaṃ ca yuddhaṃ bhūyo 'bhūt tayoḥ prāṇadurodare
karṇaṃ prāpya raṇe sūta mama putraḥ suyodhanaḥ
śrutvā tu nirjitaṃ karṇam asakṛd bhīmakarmaṇā
bhīmasenena samare moha āviśatīva mām
na hi karṇo maheṣvāsān pārthāñ jyeṣyati saṃjaya
kṛtavān yāni yuddhāni karṇaḥ pāṇḍusutaiḥ saha
sarvatra pāṇḍavāḥ karṇam ajayanta raṇājire
ajayyāḥ pāṇḍavās tāta devair api savāsavaiḥ
nikṛtyā nikṛtiprajño rājyaṃ hṛtvā mahātmanām
jitān ity eva manvānaḥ pāṇḍavān avamanyate
putrasnehābhibhūtena mayā cāpy akṛtātmanā
dharme sthitā mahātmāno nikṛtāḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ
śamakāmaḥ sadā pārtho dīrghaprekṣī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
aśakta iti manvānaiḥ putrair mama nirākṛtaḥ
tāni duḥkhāny anekāni viprakārāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
hṛdi kṛtvā mahābāhur bhīmo 'yudhyata sūtajam
tasmān me saṃjaya brūhi karṇabhīmau yathā raṇe
ayudhyetāṃ yudhi śreṣṭhau parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
saṃjaya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan yathā vṛttaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ karṇabhīmayoḥ
parākrāntaṃ parākramya vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ
mahāvegaiḥ prasannāgraiḥ śātakumbhapariṣkṛtaiḥ
āhanad bharataśreṣṭha bhīmaṃ vaikartanaḥ śaraiḥ
rathanīḍāc ca yantāraṃ bhallenāpātayat kṣitau
sa kāṅkṣan bhīmasenasya vadhaṃ vaikartano vṛṣaḥ
śaktiṃ kanakavaiḍūryacitradaṇḍāṃ parāmṛśat
pragṛhya ca mahāśaktiṃ kālaśaktim ivāparām
samutkṣipya ca rādheyaḥ saṃdhāya ca mahābalaḥ
cikṣepa bhīmasenāya jīvitāntakarīm iva
śaktiṃ visṛjya rādheyaḥ puraṃdara ivāśanim
nanāda sumahānādaṃ balavān sūtanandanaḥ
taṃ ca nādaṃ tataḥ śrutvā putrās te hṛṣitābhavan
tāṃ karṇabhujanirmuktām arkavaiśvānaraprabhām
śaktiṃ viyati ciccheda bhīmaḥ saptabhir āśugaiḥ
mārgamāṇa iva prāṇān sūtaputrasya māriṣa
prāhiṇon nava saṃrabdhaḥ śarān barhiṇavāsasaḥ
svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilādhautān yamadaṇḍopamān mṛdhe
karṇo 'py anyad dhanur gṛhya hemapṛṣṭhaṃ durāsadam
vikṛṣya ca mahātejā vyasṛjat sāyakān nava
vasuṣeṇena nirmuktān nava rājan mahāśarān
chittvā bhīmo mahārāja nādaṃ siṃha ivānadat
tau vṛṣāv iva nardantau balinau vāśitāntare
śārdūlāv iva cānyonyam atyarthaṃ ca hy agarjatām
anyonyaṃ prajihīrṣantāv anyonyasyāntaraiṣiṇau
mahāgajāv ivāsādya viṣāṇāgraiḥ parasparam
śaraiḥ pūrṇāyatotsṛṣṭair anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
nirdahantau mahārāja śaravṛṣṭyā parasparam
śaṅkhaśabdaṃ ca kurvāṇau yuyudhāte parasparam
tasya bhīmaḥ punaś cāpaṃ muṣṭau ciccheda māriṣa
śaṅkhavarṇāś ca tān aśvān bāṇair ninye yamakṣayam
tathā kṛcchragataṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ duryodhano nṛpaḥ
gaccha durjaya rādheyaṃ purā grasati pāṇḍavaḥ
jahi tūbarakaṃ kṣipraṃ karṇasya balam ādadhat
abhyadravad bhīmasenaṃ vyāsaktaṃ vikirañ śarān
sa bhīmaṃ navabhir bāṇair aśvān aṣṭabhir ardayat
ṣaḍbhiḥ sūtaṃ tribhiḥ ketuṃ punas taṃ cāpi saptabhiḥ
bhīmaseno 'pi saṃkruddhaḥ sāśvayantāram āśugaiḥ
svalaṃkṛtaṃ kṣitau kṣuṇṇaṃ ceṣṭamānaṃ yathoragam
samācinod bāṇagaṇaiḥ śataghnīm iva śaṅkubhiḥ
tathāpy atirathaḥ karṇo bhidyamānaḥ sma sāyakaiḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
ratham anyaṃ samāsthāya sadyo vivyādha pāṇḍavam
mahāgajāv ivāsādya viṣāṇāgraiḥ parasparam
śaraiḥ pūrṇāyatotsṛṣṭair anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
taṃ bhīmo daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyad ajihmagaiḥ
punar vivyādha viṃśatyā śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
sāyakānāṃ tataḥ pārthas triṣaṣṭyā pratyavidhyata
tottrair iva mahānāgaṃ kaśābhir iva vājinam
so 'tividdho mahārāja pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā
sṛkviṇī lelihan vīraḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ
tataḥ śaraṃ mahārāja sarvakāyāvadāraṇam
prāhiṇod bhīmasenāya balāyendra ivāśanim
agacchad dārayan bhūmiṃ citrapuṅkhaḥ śilīmukhaḥ
sarvaśaikyāṃ catuṣkiṣkuṃ gurvīṃ rukmāṅgadāṃ gadām
prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya ṣaḍasrām avicārayan
tayā jaghānādhiratheḥ sadaśvān sādhuvāhinaḥ
gadayā bhārataḥ kruddho vajreṇendra ivāsurān
tato bhīmo mahābāhuḥ kṣurābhyāṃ bharatarṣabha
viratho rathināṃ śreṣṭho vārayām āsa yad ripum
virathaṃ taṃ rathaśreṣṭhaṃ dṛṣṭvādhirathim āhave
eṣa durmukha rādheyo bhīmena virathīkṛtaḥ
taṃ rathena naraśreṣṭhaṃ saṃpādaya mahāratham
tvaramāṇo 'byayāt karṇaṃ bhīmaṃ cāvārayac charaiḥ
vāyuputraḥ prahṛṣṭo 'bhūt sṛkkiṇī parilelihan
tataḥ karṇaṃ mahārāja vārayitvā śilīmukhaiḥ
