durmukhāya rathaṃ śīghraṃ preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
āsthitaḥ prababhau rājan dīpyamāna ivāṃśumān
śayānaṃ bhinnamarmāṇaṃ durmukhaṃ śoṇitokṣitam
dṛṣṭvā karṇo 'śrupūrṇākṣo muhūrtaṃ nābhyavartata
taṃ gatāsum atikramya kṛtvā karṇaḥ pradakṣiṇam
dīrgham uṣṇaṃ śvasan vīro na kiṃ cit pratyapadyata
tasmiṃs tu vivare rājan nārācān gārdhravāsasaḥ
prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya bhīmasenaś caturdaśa
apiban sūtaputrasya śoṇitaṃ raktabhojanāḥ
kruddhā iva manuṣyendra bhujagāḥ kālacoditāḥ
prasarpamāṇā medinyāṃ te vyarocanta mārgaṇāḥ
ardhapraviṣṭāḥ saṃrabdhā bilānīva mahoragāḥ
taṃ pratyavidhyad rādheyo jāmbūnadavibhūṣitaiḥ
prāviśan medinīṃ bhīmāḥ krauñcaṃ patrarathā iva
te vyarocanta nārācāḥ praviśanto vasuṃdharām
gacchaty astaṃ dinakare dīpyamānā ivāṃśavaḥ
susrāva rudhiraṃ bhūri parvataḥ salilaṃ yathā
sa vihvalo mahārāja karṇo bhīmabalārditaḥ
prādravaj javanair aśvai raṇaṃ hitvā mahāyaśāḥ
bhīmasenas tu visphārya cāpaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam
āhave 'tiratho 'tiṣṭhaj jvalann iva hutāśanaḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
yatrādhirathir āyasto nātarat pāṇḍavaṃ raṇe
karṇaḥ pārthān sagovindāñ jetum utsahate raṇe
na ca karṇasamaṃ yodhaṃ loke paśyāmi kaṃ cana
karṇo hi balavāñ śūro dṛḍhadhanvā jitaklamaḥ
vasuṣeṇasahāyaṃ māṃ nālaṃ devāpi saṃyuge
kim pāṇḍusutā rājan gatasattvā vicetasaḥ
tatra taṃ nirjitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhujaṃgam iva nirviṣam
aśvatthāmā madrarājaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaś ca saṃgatāḥ
na śaktāḥ pramukhe sthātuṃ nūnaṃ bhīmasya saṃjaya
te 'pi cāsya mahāghoraṃ balaṃ nāgāyutopamam
jānanto vyavasāyaṃ ca krūraṃ mārutatejasaḥ
kimarthaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ yamakālāntakopamam
balasaṃrambhavīryajñāḥ kopayiṣyanti saṃyuge
karṇas tv eko mahābāhuḥ svabāhubalam āśritaḥ
bhīmasenam anādṛtya raṇe 'yudhyata sūtajaḥ
na sa pāṇḍusuto jetuṃ śakyaḥ kena cid āhave
droṇaṃ yaḥ saṃpramathyaikaḥ praviṣṭo mama vāhinīm
bhīmo dhanaṃjayānveṣī kas tam archej jijīviṣuḥ
pretarājapuraṃ prāpya nivartetāpi mānavaḥ
pataṃgā iva vahniṃ te prāviśann alpacetasaḥ
śaptaṃ saṃrambhiṇogreṇa kurūṇāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ tadā
tan nūnam abhisaṃcintya dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ ca nirjitam
duḥśāsanaḥ saha bhrātrā bhayād bhīmād upāramat
karṇo duḥśāsano 'haṃ ca jeṣyāmo yudhi pāṇḍavān
sa nūnaṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ bhīmena nirjitam
pratyākhyānāc ca kṛṣṇasya bhṛśaṃ tapyati saṃjaya
dṛṣṭvā bhrātṝn hatān yuddhe bhīmasenena daṃśitān
ātmāparādhāt sumahan nūnaṃ tapyati putrakaḥ
ko hi jīvitam anvicchan pratīpaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ vrajet
bhīmaṃ bhīmāyudhaṃ kruddhaṃ sākṣāt kālam iva sthitam
na pāṇḍavā na pāñcālā na ca keśavasātyakī
jānanti yudhi saṃrabdhā jīvitaṃ parirakṣitum
saṃjaya uvāca
tvam asya jagato mūlaṃ vināśasya na saṃśayaḥ
svayaṃ vairaṃ mahat kṛtvā putrāṇāṃ vacane sthitaḥ
ucyamāno na gṛhṇīṣe martyaḥ pathyam ivauṣadham
svayaṃ pītvā mahārāja kālakūṭaṃ sudurjaram
tasyedānīṃ phalaṃ kṛtsnam avāpnuhi narottama
dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ tu putrās te bhīmasenaparājitam
nāmṛṣyanta maheṣvāsāḥ sodaryāḥ pañca māriṣa
pāṇḍavaṃ citrasaṃnāhās taṃ pratīpam upādravan
te samantān mahābāhuṃ parivārya vṛkodaram
diśaḥ śaraiḥ samāvṛṇvañ śalabhānām iva vrajaiḥ
āgacchatas tān sahasā kumārān devarūpiṇaḥ
tava dṛṣṭvā tu tanayān bhīmasenasamīpagān
visṛjan viśikhān rājan svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitān
taṃ tu bhīmo 'bhyayāt tūrṇaṃ vāryamāṇaḥ sutais tava
avākiran bhīmasenaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
tān bāṇaiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā sāśvān rājan nararṣabhān
sasūtān bhīmadhanuṣo bhīmo ninye yamakṣayam
citrapuṣpadharā bhagnā vāteneva mahādrumāḥ
saṃvāryādhirathiṃ bāṇair yaj jaghāna tavātmajān
sa vāryamāṇo bhīmena śitair bāṇaiḥ samantataḥ
taṃ bhīmasenaḥ saṃrambhāt krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
tavātmajāṃs tu patitān dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ pratāpavān
krodhena mahatāviṣṭo nirviṇṇo 'bhūt sa jīvitāt
āgaskṛtam ivātmānaṃ mene cādhirathis tadā
bhīmasenaṃ tataḥ kruddhaḥ samādravata saṃbhramāt
punar vivyādha saptatyā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
avahāsaṃ tu taṃ pārtho nāmṛṣyata vṛkodaraḥ
tato vivyādha rādheyaṃ śatena nataparvaṇām
punaś ca viśikhais tīkṣṇair viddhvā pañcabhir āśugaiḥ
athānyad dhanur ādāya karṇo bhārata durmanāḥ
iṣubhiś chādayām āsa bhīmasenaṃ samantataḥ
prajahāsa mahāhāsaṃ kṛte pratikṛtaṃ punaḥ
iṣubhiḥ kārmukaṃ cāsya cakarta puruṣarṣabhaḥ
tat papāta mahārāja svarṇapṛṣṭhaṃ mahāsvanam
avārohad rathāt tasmād atha karṇo mahārathaḥ
gadāṃ gṛhītvā samare bhīmasenāya cākṣipat
tām āpatantīṃ sahasā gadāṃ dṛṣṭvā vṛkodaraḥ
tato bāṇasahasrāṇi preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
sūtaputravadhākāṅkṣī tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī
tān iṣūn iṣubhiḥ karṇo vārayitvā mahāmṛdhe
kavacaṃ bhīmasenasya pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
athainaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇāṃ samārpayat
paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tad adbhutam ivābhavat
raṇe 'preṣayata kruddhaḥ sūtaputrasya māriṣa
te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā tathā bāhuṃ ca dakṣiṇam
abhyagur dharaṇīṃ tīkṣṇā valmīkam iva pannagāḥ
rādheyaṃ tu raṇe dṛṣṭvā padātinam avasthitam
abhyayuḥ pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe visṛjantaḥ śitāñ śarān
citropacitraś citrākṣaś cārucitraḥ śarāsanaḥ
āgacchatas tān sahasā bhīmo rājan mahārathaḥ
sāśvasūtadhvajān yattān pātayām āsa saṃyuge
te hatā nyapatan bhūmau vātanunnā iva drumāḥ
dṛṣṭvā vinihatān putrāṃs tava rājan mahārathān
aśrupūrṇamukhaḥ karṇaḥ kaśmalaṃ samapadyata
abhyayāt pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī
tāv anyonyaṃ śarair viddhvā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
vyabhrājetāṃ mahārāja puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukau
vyadhamat kavacaṃ kruddhaḥ sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavaḥ
raktacandanadigdhāṅgau śaraiḥ kṛtamahāvraṇau
śoṇitāktau vyarājetāṃ kālasūryāv ivoditau
tau śoṇitokṣitair gātraiḥ śaraiś chinnatanucchadau
vivarmāṇau vyarājetāṃ nirmuktāv iva pannagau
vyāghrāv iva naravyāghrau daṃṣṭrābhir itaretaram
śaradaṃṣṭrā vidhunvānau tatakṣatur ariṃdamau
vāraṇāv iva saṃsaktau raṅgamadhye virejatuḥ
rathābhyāṃ nādayantau ca diśaḥ sarvā viceratuḥ
tau rathābhyāṃ mahārāja maṇḍalāvartanādiṣu
vyarocetāṃ mahātmānau vṛtravajradharāv iva
sahastābharaṇābhyāṃ tu bhujābhyāṃ vikṣipan dhanuḥ
sa cāpaghoṣastanitaḥ śaradhārāmbudo mahān
pāṇḍavo vyakirat karṇaṃ ghano 'drim iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ
supuṅkhaiḥ kaṅkavāsobhir yat karṇaṃ chādayac charaiḥ
sa nandayan raṇe pārthaṃ keśavaṃ ca yaśasvinam
putrās tava mahārāja dadṛśuḥ pāṇḍavasya ha
saṃjaya uvāca
tava cādhirathir dṛṣṭvā syandanebhyaś cyutān sutān
niḥśvasan dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca punaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyayāt
babhau karṇaḥ śarān asyan raśmivān iva bhāskaraḥ
karṇacāpacyutair bāṇaiḥ prācchādyata vṛkodaraḥ
karṇacāpacyutāś citrāḥ śarā barhiṇavāsasaḥ
viviśuḥ sarvataḥ pārthaṃ vāsāyevāṇḍajā drumam
karṇacāpacyutā bāṇāḥ saṃpatantas tatas tataḥ
rukmapuṅkhā vyarājanta haṃsāḥ śreṇīkṛtā iva
cāpadhvajopaskarebhyaś chatrād īṣāmukhād yugāt
prabhavanto vyadṛśyanta rājann ādhiratheḥ śarāḥ
khaṃ pūrayan mahāvegān khagamān khagavāsasaḥ
suvarṇavikṛtāṃś citrān mumocādhirathiḥ śarān
tyaktvā prāṇān abhikrudhya vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
tasya vegam asaṃsahyaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇasya pāṇḍavaḥ
mahataś ca śaraughāṃs tān naivāvyathata vīryavān
tato vidhamyādhiratheḥ śarajālāni pāṇḍavaḥ
vivyādha karṇaṃ viṃśatyā punar anyaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
yathaiva hi śaraiḥ pārthaḥ sūtaputreṇa chāditaḥ
tathaiva karṇaṃ samare chādayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ
dṛṣṭvā tu bhīmasenasya vikramaṃ yudhi bhārata
abhyanandaṃs tvadīyāś ca saṃprahṛṣṭāś ca cāraṇāḥ
bhūriśravāḥ kṛpo drauṇir madrarājo jayadrathaḥ
uttamaujā yudhāmanyuḥ sātyakiḥ keśavārjunau
kurupāṇḍavānāṃ pravarā daśa rājan mahārathāḥ
rājñaś ca rājaputrāṃś ca sodaryāṃś ca viśeṣataḥ
karṇaṃ gacchata bhadraṃ vaḥ parīpsanto vṛkodarāt
purā nighnanti rādheyaṃ bhīmacāpacyutāḥ śarāḥ
te yatadhvaṃ maheṣvāsāḥ sūtaputrasya rakṣaṇe
duryodhanasamādiṣṭāḥ sodaryāḥ sapta māriṣa
te samāsādya kaunteyam āvṛṇvañ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakāḥ
te 'pīḍayan bhīmasenaṃ kruddhāḥ sapta mahārathāḥ
prajāsaṃharaṇe rājan somaṃ sapta grahā iva
tato vāmena kaunteyaḥ pīḍayitvā śarāsanam
muṣṭinā pāṇḍavo rājan dṛḍhena supariṣkṛtam
manuṣyasamatāṃ jñātvā sapta saṃdhāya sāyakān
tebhyo vyasṛjad āyastaḥ sūryaraśminibhān prabhuḥ
te kṣiptā bhīmasenena śarā bhārata bhāratān
vidārya khaṃ samutpetuḥ svarṇapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥ
teṣāṃ vidārya cetāṃsi śarā hemavibhūṣitāḥ
vyarājanta mahārāja suparṇā iva khecarāḥ
śoṇitādigdhavājāgrāḥ sapta hemapariṣkṛtāḥ
putrāṇāṃ tava rājendra pītvā śoṇitam udgatāḥ
girisānuruhā bhagnā dvipeneva mahādrumāḥ
śatruṃjayaḥ śatrusahaś citraś citrāyudho dṛḍhaḥ
tān nihatya mahābāhū rādheyasyaiva paśyataḥ
siṃhanādaravaṃ ghoram asṛjat pāṇḍunandanaḥ
taṃ śrutvā sumahānādaṃ bhīmasenasya dhanvinaḥ
tato hṛṣṭo mahārāja vāditrāṇāṃ mahāsvanaiḥ
bhīmasenaravaṃ pārthaḥ pratijagrāha sarvaśaḥ
harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ kṛtasaṃjñe vṛkodare
ekatriṃśan mahārāja putrāṃs tava mahārathān
hatān duryodhano dṛṣṭvā kṣattuḥ sasmāra tad vacaḥ
yac ca karṇo 'bravīt kṛṣṇāṃ sabhāyāṃ paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
pramukhe pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ tava caiva viśāṃ pate
kauravāṇāṃ ca sarveṣām ācāryasya ca saṃnidhau
vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvataṃ narakaṃ gatāḥ
patim anyaṃ vṛṇīṣveti tasyedaṃ phalam āgatam
yat sma tāṃ paruṣāṇy āhuḥ sabhām ānāyya draupadīm
pāṇḍavān ugradhanuṣaḥ krodhayantas tavātmajāḥ
taṃ bhīmasenaḥ krodhāgniṃ trayodaśa samāḥ sthitam
visṛjaṃs tava putrāṇām antaṃ gacchati kaurava
vilapaṃś ca bahu kṣattā śamaṃ nālabhata tvayi
pravarān ātmajānāṃ te sutāṃś cānyān mahārathān
yān yāṃś ca dadṛśe bhīmaś cakṣurviṣayam āgatān
putrāṃs tava mahābāho tvarayā tāñ jaghāna ha
tvatkṛte hy aham adrākṣaṃ dahyamānāṃ varūthinīm
sahasraśaḥ śarair muktaiḥ pāṇḍavena vṛṣeṇa ca
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
mahān apanayaḥ sūta mamaivātra viśeṣataḥ
sa idānīm anuprāpto manye saṃjaya śocataḥ
idānīm atra kiṃ kāryaṃ prakariṣyāmi saṃjaya
yathā tv eṣa kṣayo vṛtto mamāpanayasaṃbhavaḥ
vīrāṇāṃ tan mamācakṣva sthirībhūto 'smi saṃjaya
saṃjaya uvāca
karṇabhīmau mahārāja parākrāntau mahāhave
bāṇavarṣāṇy avarṣetāṃ vṛṣṭimantāv ivāmbudau
bhīmanāmāṅkitā bāṇāḥ svarṇapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥ
viviśuḥ karṇam āsādya bhindanta iva jīvitam
ākīryata raṇe bhīmaḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
tayoḥ śarair mahārāja saṃpatadbhiḥ samantataḥ
babhūva tava sainyānāṃ saṃkṣobhaḥ sāgaropamaḥ
avadhyata camūmadhye ghorair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
vāraṇaiḥ patitai rājan vājibhiś ca naraiḥ saha
adṛśyata mahī kīrṇā vātanunnair drumair iva
te vadhyamānāḥ samare bhīmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ
prādravaṃs tāvakā yodhāḥ kim etad iti cābruvan
protsāritaṃ mahāvegaiḥ karṇapāṇḍavayoḥ śaraiḥ
te śarāturabhūyiṣṭhā hatāśvanaravāhanāḥ
utsṛjya karṇaṃ bhīmaṃ ca prādravan sarvatodiśam
nūnaṃ pārthārtham evāsmān mohayanti divaukasaḥ
evaṃ bruvanto yodhās te tāvakā bhayapīḍitāḥ
śarapātaṃ samutsṛjya sthitā yuddhadidṛkṣavaḥ
tataḥ prāvartata nadī ghorarūpā mahāhave
babhūva ca viśeṣeṇa bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinī
vāraṇāśvamanuṣyāṇāṃ rudhiraughasamudbhavā
saṃvṛtā gatasattvaiś ca manuṣyagajavājibhiḥ
sānukarṣapatākaiś ca dvipāśvarathabhūṣaṇaiḥ
jātarūpapariṣkārair dhanurbhiḥ sumahādhanaiḥ
suvarṇapuṅkhair iṣubhir nārācaiś ca sahasraśaḥ
prāsatomarasaṃghātaiḥ khaḍgaiś ca saparaśvadhaiḥ
suvarṇavikṛtaiś cāpi gadāmusalapaṭṭiśaiḥ
kanakāṅgadakeyūraiḥ kuṇḍalair maṇibhiḥ śubhaiḥ
gajāśvamanujair bhinnaiḥ śastraiḥ syandanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
dṛṣṭvā cāraṇasiddhānāṃ vismayaḥ samapadyata
gajābhyāṃ saṃprayuktābhyām āsīn naḍavanaṃ yathā
tathābhūtaṃ mahat sainyam āsīd bhārata saṃyuge
vimardaḥ karṇabhīmābhyām āsīc ca paramo raṇe
saṃjaya uvāca
tataḥ karṇo mahārāja bhīmaṃ viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
mumoca śaravarṣāṇi citrāṇi ca bahūni ca
vadhyamāno mahārāja sūtaputreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ
sa karṇaṃ karṇinā karṇe pītena niśitena ca
vivyādha yudhi rājendra bhīmasenaḥ patatriṇā
sa kuṇḍalaṃ mahat karṇāt karṇasyāpātayad bhuvi
tapanīyaṃ mahārāja dīptaṃ jyotir ivāmbarāt
ājaghāna bhṛśaṃ bhīmaḥ smayann iva mahābalaḥ
punar asya tvaran bhīmo nārācān daśa bhārata
raṇe praiṣīn mahāvegān yamadaṇḍopamāṃs tathā
te lalāṭaṃ samāsādya sūtaputrasya māriṣa
viviśuś coditās tena valmīkam iva pannagāḥ
nīlotpalamayīṃ mālāṃ dhārayan sa purā yathā
tataḥ kruddho raṇe karṇaḥ pīḍito dṛḍhadhanvanā
tasmai karṇaḥ śataṃ rājann iṣūṇāṃ gārdhravāsasām
amarṣī balavān kruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata
tataḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ
tataḥ karṇo mahārāja pāṇḍavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
ājaghānorasi kruddhaḥ kruddharūpaṃ paraṃtapaḥ
jīmūtāv iva cānyonyaṃ tau vavarṣatur āhave
śarajālaiś ca vividhaiś chādayām āsatur mṛdhe
tato bhīmo mahābāhū rādheyasya mahātmanaḥ
kṣurapreṇa dhanuś chittvā karṇaṃ vivyādha patriṇā
tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ sūtaputro mahāmanāḥ
dṛṣṭvā ca kurusauvīrasaindhavānāṃ balakṣayam
savarmadhvajaśastraiś ca patitaiḥ saṃvṛtāṃ mahīm
hastyaśvanaradehāṃś ca gatāsūn prekṣya sarvataḥ
sūtaputrasya saṃrambhād dīptaṃ vapur ajāyata
bhīmaṃ praikṣata rādheyo rājan ghoreṇa cakṣuṣā
madhyaṃdinagato 'rciṣmāñ śaradīva divākaraḥ
āsīd ādhirather ghoraṃ vapuḥ śaraśatārciṣaḥ
karābhyām ādadānasya saṃdadhānasya cāśugān
vikarṣato muñcato vā nāntaraṃ dadṛśū raṇe
agnicakropamaṃ ghoraṃ maṇḍalīkṛtam āyudham
karṇasyāsīn mahārāja savyadakṣiṇam asyataḥ
svarṇapuṅkhāḥ suniśitāḥ karṇacāpacyutāḥ śarāḥ
prācchādayan mahārāja diśaḥ sūryasya ca prabhām
tataḥ kanakapuṅkhānāṃ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
dhanuścyutānāṃ viyati dadṛśe bahudhā vrajaḥ
śarāsanād ādhiratheḥ prabhavantaḥ sma sāyakāḥ
śreṇīkṛtā vyarājanta rājan krauñcā ivāmbare
gārdhrapatrāñ śilādhautān kārtasvaravibhūṣitān
mahāvegān pradīptāgrān mumocādhirathiḥ śarān
te tu cāpabaloddhūtāḥ śātakumbhavibhūṣitāḥ
te vyomni ratnavikṛtā vyakāśanta sahasraśaḥ
śalabhānām iva vrātāḥ śarāḥ karṇasamīritāḥ
cāpād ādhirather muktāḥ prapatantaḥ sma sāyakāḥ
eko dīrgha iva prāṃśuḥ prabhavan dṛśyate śaraḥ
parvataṃ vāridhārābhiś chādayann iva toyadaḥ
karṇaḥ prācchādayat kruddho bhīmaṃ sāyakavṛṣṭibhiḥ
tāṃ samudram ivoddhūtāṃ śaravṛṣṭiṃ samutthitām
rukmapṛṣṭhaṃ mahac cāpaṃ bhīmasyāsīd viśāṃ pate
ākarṣān maṇḍalībhūtaṃ śakracāpam ivāparam
tasmāc charāḥ prādurāsan pūrayanta ivāmbaram
gagane racitā mālā kāñcanīva vyarājata
tato vyomni viṣaktāni śarajālāni bhāgaśaḥ
āhatāni vyaśīryanta bhīmasenasya patribhiḥ
tais taiḥ kanakapuṅkhānāṃ dyaur āsīt saṃvṛtā vrajaiḥ
sa bhīmaṃ chādayan bāṇaiḥ sūtaputraḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ
upārohad anādṛtya tasya vīryaṃ mahātmanaḥ
tayor visṛjatos tatra śarajālāni māriṣa
vāyubhūtāny adṛśyanta saṃsaktānītaretaram
tasmai karṇaḥ śitān bāṇān karmāraparimārjitān
suvarṇavikṛtān kruddhaḥ prāhiṇod vadhakāṅkṣayā
viśeṣayan sūtaputraṃ bhīmas tiṣṭheti cābravīt
punaś cāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ
amarṣī balavān kruddho didhakṣann iva pāvakaḥ
tasya tāny ādade karṇaḥ sarvāṇy astrāṇy abhītavat
yudhyataḥ pāṇḍuputrasya sūtaputro 'stramāyayā
tasyeṣudhī dhanurjyāṃ ca bāṇaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
raśmīn yoktrāṇi cāśvānāṃ karṇo vaikartano 'cchinat
athāsyāśvān punar hatvā tribhir vivyādha sārathim
dhvajaṃ ciccheda rādheyaḥ patākāś ca nyapātayat
sa vidhanvā mahārāja rathaśaktiṃ parāmṛśat
tām avāsṛjad āvidhya kruddhaḥ karṇarathaṃ prati
tām ādhirathir āyastaḥ śaktiṃ hemapariṣkṛtām
āpatantīṃ maholkābhāṃ ciccheda daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
sāpatad daśadhā rājan nikṛttā karṇasāyakaiḥ
sa vicarmā mahārāja virathaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
sa dhanuḥ sūtaputrasya chittvā jyāṃ ca susaṃśitaḥ
tasya tac caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme vijayaiṣiṇaḥ
tad asya kuravaḥ sarve cāraṇāś cābhyapūjayan
yad iyeṣa rathāt karṇaṃ hantuṃ tārkṣya ivoragam
svarathaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā yuddhāyaiva vyavasthitaḥ
saṃrabdhaḥ pāṇḍavaṃ saṃkhye yuddhāya samupasthitam
tayor āsīt saṃprahāraḥ kruddhayor narasiṃhayoḥ
amṛṣyamāṇayoḥ saṃkhye devadānavayor iva
kṣīṇaśastras tu kaunteyaḥ karṇena samabhidrutaḥ
dṛṣṭvārjunahatān nāgān patitān parvatopamān
rathamārgavighātārthaṃ vyāyudhaḥ praviveśa ha
pāṇḍavo jīvitākāṅkṣī rādheyaṃ nābhyahārayat
vyavasthānam athākāṅkṣan dhanaṃjayaśarair hatam
hastyaṅgāny atha karṇāya prāhiṇot pāṇḍavo nadan
cakrāṇy aśvāṃs tathā vāhān yad yat paśyati bhūtale
tat tad ādāya cikṣepa kruddhaḥ karṇāya pāṇḍavaḥ
tad asya sarvaṃ ciccheda kṣiptaṃ kṣiptaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
vyāyudhaṃ nāvadhīc cainaṃ karṇaḥ kuntyā vacaḥ smaran
dhanuṣo 'greṇa taṃ karṇas tv abhidrutya parāmṛśat
akṛtāstraka mā yotsīr bāla saṃgrāmakātara
yatra bhojyaṃ bahuvidhaṃ bhakṣyaṃ peyaṃ ca pāṇḍava
puṣpamūlaphalāhāro vrateṣu niyameṣu ca
ucitas tvaṃ vane bhīma na tvaṃ yuddhaviśāradaḥ
sūdān bhṛtyajanān dāsāṃs tvaṃ gṛhe tvarayan bhṛśam
yogyas tāḍayituṃ krodhād bhojanārthaṃ vṛkodara
kaumāre yāni cāpy āsann apriyāṇi viśāṃ pate
pūrvavṛttāni cāpy enaṃ rūkṣāṇy aśrāvayad bhṛśam
athainaṃ tatra saṃlīnam aspṛśad dhanuṣā punaḥ
prahasaṃś ca punar vākyaṃ bhīmam āha vṛṣas tadā
yoddhavyam āviśānyatra na yoddhavyaṃ tu mādṛśaiḥ
mādṛśair yudhyamānānām etac cānyac ca vidyate
gaccha vā yatra tau kṛṣṇau tau tvā rakṣiṣyato raṇe
evaṃ taṃ virathaṃ kṛtvā karṇo rājan vyakatthata
pramukhe vṛṣṇisiṃhasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ
tato rājañ śilādhautāñ śarāñ śākhāmṛgadhvajaḥ
prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya keśavena pracoditaḥ
tataḥ pārthabhujotsṛṣṭāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥ
gāṇḍīvaprabhavāḥ karṇaṃ haṃsāḥ krauñcam ivāviśan
sa bhujaṃgair ivāyastair gāṇḍīvapreṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ
bhīmasenād apāsedhat sūtaputraṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
sa chinnadhanvā bhīmena dhanaṃjayaśarāhataḥ
karṇo bhīmād apāyāsīd rathena mahatā drutam
bhīmo 'pi sātyaker vāhaṃ samāruhya nararṣabhaḥ
anvayād bhrātaraṃ saṃkhye pāṇḍavaṃ savyasācinam
tataḥ karṇaṃ samuddiśya tvaramāṇo dhanaṃjayaḥ
nārācaṃ krodhatāmrākṣaḥ praiṣīn mṛtyum ivāntakaḥ
nārāco 'bhyapatat karṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ gāṇḍīvacoditaḥ
tam antarikṣe nārācaṃ drauṇiś ciccheda patriṇā
dhanaṃjayabhayāt karṇam ujjihīrṣur mahārathaḥ
tato drauṇiṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā vivyādha kupito 'rjunaḥ
śilīmukhair mahārāja mā gās tiṣṭheti cābravīt
sa tu mattagajākīrṇam anīkaṃ rathasaṃkulam
tūrṇam abhyāviśad drauṇir dhanaṃjayaśarārditaḥ
tataḥ suvarṇapṛṣṭhānāṃ dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ raṇe
śabdaṃ gāṇḍīvaghoṣeṇa kaunteyo 'bhyabhavad balī
dhanaṃjayas tathā yāntaṃ pṛṣṭhato drauṇim abhyayāt
nātidīrgham ivādhvānaṃ śaraiḥ saṃtrāsayan balam
vidārya dehān nārācair naravāraṇavājinām
tad balaṃ bharataśreṣṭha savājidvipamānavam
pākaśāsanir āyastaḥ pārthaḥ saṃnijaghāna ha
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
dhanaṃjayas tu saṃkruddhaḥ praviṣṭo māmakaṃ balam
rakṣitaṃ droṇakarṇābhyām apraveśyaṃ surair api
tābhyām ūrjitavīryābhyām āpyāyitaparākramaḥ
sahitaḥ kṛṣṇabhīmābhyāṃ śinīnām ṛṣabheṇa ca
tadā prabhṛti mā śoko dahaty agnir ivāśayam
grastān hi pratipaśyāmi bhūmipālān sasaindhavān
apriyaṃ sumahat kṛtvā sindhurājaḥ kirīṭinaḥ
cakṣurviṣayam āpannaḥ kathaṃ mucyeta jīvitaḥ
anumānāc ca paśyāmi nāsti saṃjaya saindhavaḥ
yuddhaṃ tu tad yathā vṛttaṃ tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ
yac ca vikṣobhya mahatīṃ senāṃ saṃloḍya cāsakṛt
ekaḥ praviṣṭaḥ saṃkruddho nalinīm iva kuñjaraḥ
tasya vṛṣṇipravīrasya brūhi yuddhaṃ yathātatham
saṃjaya uvāca
tathā tu vaikartanapīḍitaṃ taṃ bhīmaṃ prayāntaṃ puruṣapravīram
nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ tvadīyāḥ sarve rathā bhārata mādhavāgryam
amarṣapūrṇas tv anivṛttayodhī śarāsanī kāñcanavarmadhārī
anāgatān eva tu tān pṛṣatkāṃś ciccheda bāṇaiḥ śinipuṃgavo 'pi
punaḥ sa bāṇais tribhir agnikalpair ākarṇapūrṇair niśitaiḥ supuṅkhaiḥ
vivyādha dehāvaraṇaṃ vidārya te sātyaker āviviśuḥ śarīram
ājaghnivāṃs tān rajataprakāśān aśvāṃś caturbhiś caturaḥ prasahya
sakuṇḍalaṃ pūrṇaśaśiprakāśaṃ bhrājiṣṇu vaktraṃ nicakarta dehāt
nihatya taṃ pārthivaputrapautraṃ saṃkhye madhūnām ṛṣabhaḥ pramāthī
tato 'nvayād arjunam eva vīraḥ sainyāni rājaṃs tava saṃnivārya
anvāgataṃ vṛṣṇivaraṃ samīkṣya tathārimadhye parivartamānam
ghnantaṃ kurūṇām iṣubhir balāni punaḥ punar vāyur ivābhrapūgān
tato 'vahan saindhavāḥ sādhu dāntā gokṣīrakundenduhimaprakāśāḥ
suvarṇajālāvatatāḥ sadaśvā yato yataḥ kāmayate nṛsiṃhaḥ
kṛtvā mukhaṃ bhārata yodhamukhyaṃ duḥśāsanaṃ tvatsutam ājamīḍha
te sarvataḥ saṃparivārya saṃkhye śaineyam ājaghnur anīkasāhāḥ
sa cāpi tān pravaraḥ sātvatānāṃ nyavārayad bāṇajālena vīraḥ
nivārya tāṃs tūrṇam amitraghātī naptā śineḥ patribhir agnikalpaiḥ
duḥśāsanasyāpi jaghāna vāhān udyamya bāṇāsanam ājamīḍha
saṃjaya uvāca
tam udyataṃ mahābāhuṃ duḥśāsanarathaṃ prati
tvaritaṃ tvaraṇīyeṣu dhanaṃjayahitaiṣiṇam
trigartānāṃ maheṣvāsāḥ suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥ
senāsamudram āviṣṭam ānartaṃ paryavārayan
athainaṃ rathavaṃśena sarvataḥ saṃnivārya te
avākirañ śaravrātaiḥ kruddhāḥ paramadhanvinaḥ
ajayad rājaputrāṃs tān yatamānān mahāraṇe
ekaḥ pañcāśataṃ śatrūn sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
saṃprāpya bhāratīmadhyaṃ talaghoṣasamākulam
asiśaktigadāpūrṇam aplavaṃ salilaṃ yathā
tatrādbhutam apaśyāma śaineyacaritaṃ raṇe
pratīcyāṃ diśi taṃ dṛṣṭvā prācyāṃ paśyāma lāghavāt
udīcīṃ dakṣiṇāṃ prācīṃ pratīcīṃ prasṛtas tathā
nṛtyann ivācarac chūro yathā rathaśataṃ tathā
tad dṛṣṭvā caritaṃ tasya siṃhavikrāntagāminaḥ
trigartāḥ saṃnyavartanta saṃtaptāḥ svajanaṃ prati
tam anye śūrasenānāṃ śūrāḥ saṃkhye nyavārayan
niyacchantaḥ śaravrātair mattaṃ dvipam ivāṅkuśaiḥ
tān nyavārayad āyastān muhūrtam iva sātyakiḥ
tāṃ ca senām atikramya kaliṅgānāṃ duratyayām
atha pārthaṃ mahābāhur dhanaṃjayam upāsadat
taṃ dṛṣṭvā puruṣavyāghraṃ yuyudhānaḥ samāśvasat
asāv āyāti śaineyas tava pārtha padānugaḥ
eṣa śiṣyaḥ sakhā caiva tava satyaparākramaḥ
sarvān yodhāṃs tṛṇīkṛtya vijigye puruṣarṣabhaḥ
eṣa kauravayodhānāṃ kṛtvā ghoram upadravam
tava prāṇaiḥ priyataraḥ kirīṭinn eti sātyakiḥ
eṣa droṇaṃ tathā bhojaṃ kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca
kadarthīkṛtya viśikhaiḥ phalgunābhyeti sātyakiḥ
dharmarājapriyānveṣī hatvā yodhān varān varān
śūraś caiva kṛtāstraś ca phalgunābhyeti sātyakiḥ
tava darśanam anvicchan pāṇḍavābhyeti sātyakiḥ
ācāryapramukhān pārtha āyāty eṣa hi sātyakiḥ
svabāhubalam āśritya vidārya ca varūthinīm
nihatya bahulāḥ senāḥ pārthaiṣo 'bhyeti sātyakiḥ
eṣa rājasahasrāṇāṃ vaktraiḥ paṅkajasaṃnibhaiḥ
āstīrya vasudhāṃ pārtha kṣipram āyāti sātyakiḥ
eṣa duryodhanaṃ jitvā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaṃ raṇe
nihatya jalasaṃdhaṃ ca kṣipram āyāti sātyakiḥ
rudhiraughavatīṃ kṛtvā nadīṃ śoṇitakardamām
tṛṇavan nyasya kauravyān eṣa āyāti sātyakiḥ
tato 'prahṛṣṭaḥ kaunteyaḥ keśavaṃ vākyam abravīt
na me priyaṃ mahābāho yan mām abhyeti sātyakiḥ
na hi jānāmi vṛttāntaṃ dharmarājasya keśava
sātvatena vihīnaḥ sa yadi jīvati vā na vā
etena hi mahābāho rakṣitavyaḥ sa pārthivaḥ
tam eṣa katham utsṛjya mama kṛṣṇa padānugaḥ
rājā droṇāya cotsṛṣṭaḥ saindhavaś cānipātitaḥ
pratyudyātaś ca śaineyam eṣa bhūriśravā raṇe
so 'yaṃ gurutaro bhāraḥ saindhavān me samāhitaḥ
jñātavyaś ca hi me rājā rakṣitavyaś ca sātyakiḥ
śrāntaś caiṣa mahābāhur alpaprāṇaś ca sāṃpratam
pariśrāntā hayāś cāsya hayayantā ca mādhava
na ca bhūriśravāḥ śrāntaḥ sasahāyaś ca keśava
apīdānīṃ bhaved asya kṣemam asmin samāgame
kaccin na sāgaraṃ tīrtvā sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ
goṣpadaṃ prāpya sīdeta mahaujāḥ śinipuṃgavaḥ
ācāryād bhayam utsṛjya yaḥ preṣayati sātyakim
grahaṇaṃ dharmarājasya khagaḥ śyena ivāmiṣam
nityam āśaṃsate droṇaḥ kaccit syāt kuśalī nṛpaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
krodhād bhūriśravā rājan sahasā samupādravat
tam abravīn mahābāhuḥ kauravyaḥ śinipuṃgavam
adya prāpto 'si diṣṭyā me cakṣurviṣayam ity uta
cirābhilaṣitaṃ kāmam adya prāpsyāmi saṃyuge
adya tvāṃ samare hatvā nityaṃ śūrābhimāninam
nandayiṣyāmi dāśārha kururājaṃ suyodhanam
adya madbāṇanirdagdhaṃ patitaṃ dharaṇītale
drakṣyatas tvāṃ raṇe vīrau sahitau keśavārjunau
adya dharmasuto rājā śrutvā tvāṃ nihataṃ mayā
savrīḍo bhavitā sadyo yenāsīha praveśitaḥ
adya yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ tava dāsyāmi sātvata
adya saṃyamanīṃ yātā mayā tvaṃ nihato raṇe
yathā rāmānujenājau rāvaṇir lakṣmaṇena vai
adya kṛṣṇaś ca pārthaś ca dharmarājaś ca mādhava
hate tvayi nirutsāhā raṇaṃ tyakṣyanty asaṃśayam
adya te 'pacitiṃ kṛtvā śitair mādhava sāyakaiḥ
cakṣurviṣayasaṃprāpto na tvaṃ mādhava mokṣyase
siṃhasya viṣayaṃ prāpto yathā kṣudramṛgas tathā
sa māṃ nihanyāt saṃgrāme yo māṃ kuryān nirāyudham
samās tu śāśvatīr hanyād yo māṃ hanyād dhi saṃyuge
kiṃ mṛṣoktena bahunā karmaṇā tu samācara
śrutvaitad garjitaṃ vīra hāsyaṃ hi mama jāyate
tvarate me matis tāta tvayi yuddhābhikāṅkṣiṇi
nāhatvā saṃnivartiṣye tvām adya puruṣādhama
bhūriśravāḥ sātyakiś ca vavarṣatur ariṃdamau
śaravarṣāṇi bhīmāni meghāv iva parasparam
saumadattis tu śaineyaṃ pracchādyeṣubhir āśugaiḥ
jighāṃsur bharataśreṣṭha vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
daśabhiḥ sātyakiṃ viddhvā saumadattir athāparān
mumoca niśitān bāṇāñ jighāṃsuḥ śinipuṃgavam
tān asya viśikhāṃs tīkṣṇān antarikṣe viśāṃ pate
tau pṛthak śaravarṣābhyām avarṣetāṃ parasparam
uttamābhijanau vīrau kuruvṛṣṇiyaśaskarau
rathaśaktibhir anyonyaṃ viśikhaiś cāpy akṛntatām
vyaṣṭambhayetām anyonyaṃ prāṇadyūtābhidevinau
evam uttamakarmāṇau kuruvṛṣṇiyaśaskarau
parasparam ayudhyetāṃ vāraṇāv iva yūthapau
sātyakiḥ saumadattiś ca śaravṛṣṭyā parasparam
hṛṣṭavad dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ paśyatām abhyavarṣatām
saṃpraikṣanta janās tatra yudhyamānau yudhāṃ patī
yūthapau vāśitāhetoḥ prayuddhāv iva kuñjarau
virathāv asiyuddhāya sameyātāṃ mahāraṇe
ārṣabhe carmaṇī citre pragṛhya vipule śubhe
vikośau cāpy asī kṛtvā samare tau viceratuḥ
carantau vividhān mārgān maṇḍalāni ca bhāgaśaḥ
sakhaḍgau citravarmāṇau saniṣkāṅgadabhūṣaṇau
raṇe raṇotkaṭau rājann anyonyaṃ paryakarṣatām
paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ vīrāv āśvasatāṃ punaḥ
asibhyāṃ carmaṇī śubhre vipule ca śarāvare
śikṣābalasamudbhūtāḥ sarvayodhapraharṣaṇāḥ
dvipāv iva viṣāṇāgraiḥ śṛṅgair iva maharṣabhau
kṣīṇāyudhe sātvate yudhyamāne tato 'bravīd arjunaṃ vāsudevaḥ
paśyasvainaṃ virathaṃ yudhyamānaṃ raṇe ketuṃ sarvadhanurdharāṇām
praviṣṭo bhāratīṃ senāṃ tava pāṇḍava pṛṣṭhataḥ
yodhitaś ca mahāvīryaiḥ sarvair bhārata bhārataiḥ
pariśrānto yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ saṃprāpto bhūridakṣiṇam
yuddhakāṅkṣiṇam āyāntaṃ naitat samam ivārjuna
tato bhūriśravāḥ kruddhaḥ sātyakiṃ yuddhadurmadam
keśavārjunayo rājan samare prekṣamāṇayoḥ
atha kṛṣṇo mahābāhur arjunaṃ pratyabhāṣata
paśya vṛṣṇyandhakavyāghraṃ saumadattivaśaṃ gatam
pariśrāntaṃ gataṃ bhūmau kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
tavāntevāsinaṃ śūraṃ pālayārjuna sātyakim
na vaśaṃ yajñaśīlasya gacched eṣa varārihan
tvatkṛte puruṣavyāghra tad āśu kriyatāṃ vibho
athābravīd dhṛṣṭamanā vāsudevaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
paśya vṛṣṇipravīreṇa krīḍantaṃ kurupuṃgavam
hāhākāro mahān āsīt sainyānāṃ bharatarṣabha
sa siṃha iva mātaṅgaṃ vikarṣan bhūridakṣiṇaḥ
atha kośād viniṣkṛṣya khaḍgaṃ bhūriśravā raṇe
mūrdhajeṣu nijagrāha padā corasy atāḍayat
tathā tu parikṛṣyantaṃ dṛṣṭvā sātvatam āhave
paśya vṛṣṇyandhakavyāghraṃ saumadattivaśaṃ gatam
tava śiṣyaṃ mahābāho dhanuṣy anavaraṃ tvayā
asatyo vikramaḥ pārtha yatra bhūriśravā raṇe
viśeṣayati vārṣṇeyaṃ sātyakiṃ satyavikramam
evam ukto mahābāhur vāsudevena pāṇḍavaḥ
manasā pūjayām āsa bhūriśravasam āhave
vikarṣan sātvataśreṣṭhaṃ krīḍamāna ivāhave
saṃharṣayati māṃ bhūyaḥ kurūṇāṃ kīrtivardhanaḥ
pravaraṃ vṛṣṇivīrāṇāṃ yan na hanyād dhi sātyakim
evaṃ tu manasā rājan pārthaḥ saṃpūjya kauravam
vāsudevaṃ mahābāhur arjunaḥ pratyabhāṣata
saindhavāsaktadṛṣṭitvān nainaṃ paśyāmi mādhava
ity uktvā vacanaṃ kurvan vāsudevasya pāṇḍavaḥ
sakhaḍgaṃ yajñaśīlasya patriṇā bāhum acchinat
saṃjaya uvāca
sa bāhur apatad bhūmau sakhaḍgaḥ saśubhāṅgadaḥ
prahariṣyan hṛto bāhur adṛśyena kirīṭinā
sa moghaṃ kṛtam ātmānaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthena kauravaḥ
utsṛjya sātyakiṃ krodhād garhayām āsa pāṇḍavam
nṛśaṃsaṃ bata kaunteya karmedaṃ kṛtavān asi
kiṃ nu vakṣyasi rājānaṃ dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
kiṃ kurvāṇo mayā saṃkhye hato bhūriśravā iti
idam indreṇa te sākṣād upadiṣṭaṃ mahātmanā
astraṃ rudreṇa vā pārtha droṇenātha kṛpeṇa vā
āryeṇa sukaraṃ hy āhur āryakarma dhanaṃjaya
āśu tacchīlatām eti tad idaṃ tvayi dṛśyate
kathaṃ hi rājavaṃśyas tvaṃ kauraveyo viśeṣataḥ
kṣatradharmād apakrāntaḥ suvṛttaś caritavrataḥ
idaṃ tu yad atikṣudraṃ vārṣṇeyārthe kṛtaṃ tvayā
īdṛśaṃ vyasanaṃ dadyād yo na kṛṣṇasakho bhavet
vrātyāḥ saṃśliṣṭakarmāṇaḥ prakṛtyaiva vigarhitāḥ
vṛṣṇyandhakāḥ kathaṃ pārtha pramāṇaṃ bhavatā kṛtāḥ
evam uktvā mahābāhur yūpaketur mahāyaśāḥ
yuyudhānaṃ parityajya raṇe prāyam upāviśat
śarān āstīrya savyena pāṇinā puṇyalakṣaṇaḥ
yiyāsur brahmalokāya prāṇān prāṇeṣv athājuhot
sūrye cakṣuḥ samādhāya prasannaṃ salile manaḥ
tataḥ sa sarvasenāyāṃ janaḥ kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
garhayām āsa taṃ cāpi śaśaṃsa puruṣarṣabham
nindyamānau tathā kṛṣṇau nocatuḥ kiṃ cid apriyam
praśasyamānaś ca tathā nāhṛṣyad yūpaketanaḥ
tāṃs tathā vādino rājan putrāṃs tava dhanaṃjayaḥ
amṛṣyamāṇo manasā teṣāṃ tasya ca bhāṣitam
asaṃkruddhamanā vācā smārayann iva bhārata
uvāca pāṇḍutanayaḥ sākṣepam iva phalgunaḥ
na śakyo māmako hantuṃ yo me syād bāṇagocare
yūpaketo samīkṣya tvaṃ na māṃ garhitum arhasi
āttaśastrasya hi raṇe vṛṣṇivīraṃ jighāṃsataḥ
evam uktas tu pārthena śirasā bhūmim aspṛśat
pāṇinā caiva savyena prāhiṇod asya dakṣiṇam
yūpaketur mahārāja tūṣṇīm āsīd avāṅmukhaḥ
yā prītir dharmarāje me bhīme ca vadatāṃ vare
mayā tu samanujñātaḥ kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā
gaccha puṇyakṛtāṃl lokāñ śibir auśīnaro yathā
saṃjaya uvāca
khaḍgam ādāya cicchitsuḥ śiras tasya mahātmanaḥ
nihataṃ pāṇḍuputreṇa pramattaṃ bhūridakṣiṇam
iyeṣa sātyakir hantuṃ śalāgrajam akalmaṣam
krośatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ nindyamānaḥ sudurmanāḥ
vāryamāṇaḥ sa kṛṣṇena pārthena ca mahātmanā
bhīmena cakrarakṣābhyām aśvatthāmnā kṛpeṇa ca
vikrośatāṃ ca sainyānām avadhīt taṃ yatavratam
prāyopaviṣṭāya raṇe pārthena chinnabāhave
sātyakiḥ kauravendrāya khaḍgenāpāharac chiraḥ
nābhyanandanta tatsainyāḥ sātyakiṃ tena karmaṇā
sahasrākṣasamaṃ tatra siddhacāraṇamānavāḥ
pakṣavādāṃś ca bahuśaḥ prāvadaṃs tasya sainikāḥ
na vārṣṇeyasyāparādho bhavitavyaṃ hi tat tathā
tasmān manyur na vaḥ kāryaḥ krodho duḥkhakaro nṛṇām
hantavyaś caiṣa vīreṇa nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
sātyakir uvāca
dharmavādair adharmiṣṭhā dharmakañcukam āsthitāḥ
yadā bālaḥ subhadrāyāḥ sutaḥ śastravinākṛtaḥ
mayā tv etat pratijñātaṃ kṣepe kasmiṃś cid eva hi
yo māṃ niṣpiṣya saṃgrāme jīvan hanyāt padā ruṣā
ceṣṭamānaṃ pratīghāte sabhujaṃ māṃ sacakṣuṣaḥ
yukto hy asya pratīghātaḥ kṛto me kurupuṃgavāḥ
yat tu pārthena matsnehāt svāṃ pratijñāṃ ca rakṣatā
sakhaḍgo 'sya hṛto bāhur etenaivāsmi vañcitaḥ
bhavitavyaṃ ca yad bhāvi daivaṃ ceṣṭayatīva ca
api cāyaṃ purā gītaḥ śloko vālmīkinā bhuvi
pīḍākaram amitrāṇāṃ yat syāt kartavyam eva tat
saṃjaya uvāca
evam ukte mahārāja sarve kauravapāṇḍavāḥ
sunīlakeśaṃ varadasya tasya śūrasya pārāvatalohitākṣam
ākrāmad ūrdhvaṃ varado varārho vyāvṛtya dharmeṇa pareṇa rodasī
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
tīrṇaḥ sainyārṇavaṃ vīraḥ pratiśrutya yudhiṣṭhire
nigṛhya bhūriśravasā balād bhuvi nipātitaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
śṛṇu rājann ihotpattiṃ śaineyasya yathā purā
yathā ca bhūriśravaso yatra te saṃśayo nṛpa
budhasyāsīn mahendrābhaḥ putra ekaḥ purūravāḥ
purūravasa āyus tu āyuṣo nahuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
nahuṣasya yayātis tu rājarṣir devasaṃmitaḥ
yayāter devayānyāṃ tu yadur jyeṣṭho 'bhavat sutaḥ
yador abhūd anvavāye devamīḍha iti śrutaḥ
śūrasya śaurir nṛvaro vasudevo mahāyaśāḥ
dhanuṣy anavaraḥ śūraḥ kārtavīryasamo yudhi
tadvīryaś cāpi tatraiva kule śinir abhūn nṛpaḥ
tatra vai devakīṃ devīṃ vasudevārtham āptavān
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā devakīṃ śaure rathasthāṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
nāmṛṣyata mahātejāḥ somadattaḥ śiner nṛpa
madhye rājasahasrāṇāṃ prekṣakāṇāṃ samantataḥ
prasādayan mahādevam amarṣavaśam āsthitaḥ
tasya tuṣṭo mahādevo varāṇāṃ varadaḥ prabhuḥ
vareṇa chandayām āsa sa tu vavre varaṃ nṛpaḥ
madhye rājasahasrāṇāṃ padā hanyāc ca saṃyuge
na hi śakyā raṇe jetuṃ sātvatā manujarṣabha
labdhalakṣyāś ca saṃgrāme bahavaś citrayodhinaḥ
na tulyaṃ vṛṣṇibhir iha dṛśyate kiṃ cana prabho
na jñātim avamanyante vṛddhānāṃ śāsane ratāḥ
na devāsuragandharvā na yakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
jetāro vṛṣṇivīrāṇāṃ na punar mānuṣā raṇe
eteṣāṃ rakṣitāraś ca ye syuḥ kasyāṃ cid āpadi
nityaṃ devaparā dāntā dātāraś cāvikatthanāḥ
tena vṛṣṇipravīrāṇāṃ cakraṃ na pratihanyate
na tu vṛṣṇipravīrāṇāṃ sametyāntaṃ vrajen nṛpa
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
saṃjaya uvāca
bhūriśravasi saṃkrānte paralokāya bhārata
vāsudevaṃ mahābāhur arjunaḥ samacūcudat
codayāśvān bhṛśaṃ kṛṣṇa yato rājā jayadrathaḥ
astam eti mahābāho tvaramāṇo divākaraḥ
kāryaṃ saṃrakṣyate caiṣa kurusenāmahārathaiḥ
codayāśvāṃs tathā kṛṣṇa yathā hanyāṃ jayadratham
tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahābāhū rajatapratimān hayān
tvaramāṇā mahārāja senāmukhyāḥ samāvrajan
duryodhanaś ca karṇaś ca vṛṣaseno 'tha madrarāṭ
netrābhyāṃ krodhadīptābhyāṃ saṃpraikṣan nirdahann iva
arjunaṃ vīkṣya saṃyāntaṃ jayadratharathaṃ prati
alpāvaśiṣṭaṃ divasaṃ nṛvīra vighātayasvādya ripuṃ śaraughaiḥ
mithyāpratijñaḥ kaunteyaḥ pravekṣyati hutāśanam
jīvituṃ notsaheran vai bhrātaro 'sya sahānugāḥ
vinaṣṭaiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiś ca saśailavanakānanām
vasuṃdharām imāṃ karṇa bhokṣyāmo hatakaṇṭakām
kāryākāryam ajānan vai pratijñāṃ kṛtavān raṇe
nūnam ātmavināśāya pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā
rakṣitaṃ madrarājena kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanā
drauṇinā rakṣyamāṇaṃ ca mayā duḥśāsanena ca
kathaṃ prāpsyati bībhatsuḥ saindhavaṃ kālacoditaḥ
yudhyante bahavaḥ śūrā lambate ca divākaraḥ
sa tvaṃ karṇa mayā sārdhaṃ śūraiś cānyair mahārathaiḥ
dṛḍhalakṣyeṇa śūreṇa bhīmasenena dhanvinā
bhṛśam udvejitaḥ saṃkhye śarajālair anekaśaḥ
sthātavyam iti tiṣṭhāmi raṇe saṃprati mānada
naivāṅgam iṅgati kiṃ cin me saṃtaptasya raṇeṣubhiḥ
yotsyāmi tu tathā rājañ śaktyāhaṃ parayā raṇe
na hi me yudhyamānasya sāyakāṃś cāsyataḥ śitān
saindhavaṃ prāpsyate vīraḥ savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ
yat tu śaktimatā kāryaṃ satataṃ hitakāriṇā
adya yotsye 'rjunam ahaṃ pauruṣaṃ svaṃ vyapāśritaḥ
paśyantu sarvabhūtāni dāruṇaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
karṇakauravayor evaṃ raṇe saṃbhāṣamāṇayoḥ
arjuno niśitair bāṇair jaghāna tava vāhinīm
ciccheda tīkṣṇāgramukhaiḥ śūrāṇām anivartinām
bhujān parighasaṃkāśān hastihastopamān raṇe
śirāṃsi ca mahābāhuś ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
hastihastān hayagrīvā rathākṣāṃś ca samantataḥ
śoṇitāktān hayārohān gṛhītaprāsatomarān
hayavāraṇamukhyāś ca prāpatanta sahasraśaḥ
dhvajāś chatrāṇi cāpāni cāmarāṇi śirāṃsi ca
acireṇa mahīṃ pārthaś cakāra rudhirottarām
hatabhūyiṣṭhayodhaṃ tat kṛtvā tava balaṃ balī
āsasāda durādharṣaḥ saindhavaṃ satyavikramaḥ
taṃ tathāvasthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tvadīyā vīryasaṃmatāḥ
nāmṛṣyanta maheṣvāsāḥ phalgunaṃ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
duryodhanaś ca karṇaś ca vṛṣaseno 'tha madrarāṭ
saṃrabdhāḥ saindhavasyārthe samāvṛṇvan kirīṭinam
saṃgrāmakovidaṃ pārthaṃ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
abhītāḥ paryavartanta vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
saindhavaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā jighāṃsanto 'rjunācyutau
te bhujair bhogibhogābhair dhanūṃṣy āyamya sāyakān
mumucuḥ sūryaraśmyābhāñ śataśaḥ phalgunaṃ prati
tān astān asyamānāṃś ca kirīṭī yuddhadurmadaḥ
dvidhā tridhāṣṭadhaikaikaṃ chittvā vivyādha tān raṇe
siṃhalāṅgūlaketus tu darśayañ śaktim ātmanaḥ
śāradvatīsuto rājann arjunaṃ pratyavārayat
sa viddhvā daśabhiḥ pārthaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca saptabhiḥ
athainaṃ kauravaśreṣṭhāḥ sarva eva mahārathāḥ
visphārayantaś cāpāni visṛjantaś ca sāyakān
tatra pārthasya śūrasya bāhvor balam adṛśyata
iṣūṇām akṣayatvaṃ ca dhanuṣo gāṇḍivasya ca
astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya ca
taṃ drauṇiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā vṛṣasenaś ca saptabhiḥ
duryodhanaś ca viṃśatyā karṇaśalyau tribhis tribhiḥ
śliṣṭaṃ tu sarvataś cakrū rathamaṇḍalam āśu te
sūryāstamayam icchantas tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥ
siṣicur mārgaṇair ghorair giriṃ meghā ivāmbubhiḥ
te mahāstrāṇi divyāni tatra rājan vyadarśayan
dhanaṃjayasya gātreṣu śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
hatabhūyiṣṭhayodhaṃ tat kṛtvā tava balaṃ balī
āsasāda durādharṣaḥ saindhavaṃ satyavikramaḥ
taṃ karṇaḥ saṃyuge rājan pratyavārayad āśugaiḥ
taṃ pārtho daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyad raṇājire
sūtaputraṃ mahābāhuḥ sarvasainyasya paśyataḥ
sātvataś ca tribhir bāṇaiḥ karṇaṃ vivyādha māriṣa
tān karṇaḥ prativivyādha ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā mahārathaḥ
tatrādbhutam apaśyāma sūtaputrasya māriṣa
phalgunas tu mahābāhuḥ karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ raṇe
sāyakānāṃ śatenaiva sarvamarmasv atāḍayat
rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgaḥ sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
śaraiḥ pañcāśatā vīraḥ phalgunaṃ pratyavidhyata
tasya tal lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā nāmṛṣyata raṇe 'rjunaḥ
tataḥ pārtho dhanuś chittvā vivyādhainaṃ stanāntare
cikṣepa tvarayā yuktas tvarākāle dhanaṃjayaḥ
athānyad dhanur ādāya sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān
karṇo 'pi dviṣatāṃ hantā chādayām āsa phalgunam
sāyakair bahusāhasraiḥ kṛtapratikṛtepsayā
pārtho 'ham asmi tiṣṭha tvaṃ karṇo 'haṃ tiṣṭha phalguna
prekṣaṇīyau cābhavatāṃ sarvayodhasamāgame
praśasyamānau samare siddhacāraṇavātikaiḥ
ayudhyetāṃ mahārāja parasparavadhaiṣiṇau
tato duryodhano rājaṃs tāvakān abhyabhāṣata
yattā rakṣata rādheyaṃ nāhatvā samare 'rjunam
nivartiṣyati rādheya iti mām uktavān vṛṣaḥ
ākarṇamuktair iṣubhiḥ karṇasya caturo hayān
sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apāharat
chādayām āsa ca śarais tava putrasya paśyataḥ
sa chādyamānaḥ samare hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
taṃ tathā virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā ratham āropya svaṃ tadā
aśvatthāmā mahārāja bhūyo 'rjunam ayodhayat
śāradvatas tu viṃśatyā vāsudevaṃ samārpayat
dhanaṃjayaṃ dvādaśabhir ājaghāna śilīmukhaiḥ
caturbhiḥ sindhurājaś ca vṛṣasenaś ca saptabhiḥ
pṛthak pṛthaṅ mahārāja kṛṣṇapārthāv avidhyatām
droṇaputraṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā madrarājaṃ śatena ca
saindhavaṃ daśabhir bhallair vṛṣasenaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ
śāradvataṃ ca viṃśatyā viddhvā pārthaḥ samunnadat
te pratijñāpratīghātam icchantaḥ savyasācinaḥ
sahitās tāvakās tūrṇam abhipetur dhanaṃjayam
athārjunaḥ sarvatodhāram astraṃ prāduścakre trāsayan dhārtarāṣṭrān
taṃ pratyudīyuḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍusūnuṃ rathair mahārhaiḥ śaravarṣāṇy avarṣan
nāmuhyata prāpya sa rājaputraḥ kirīṭamālī visṛjan pṛṣatkān
rājyaprepsuḥ savyasācī kurūṇāṃ smaran kleśān dvādaśavarṣavṛttān
gāṇḍīvamuktair iṣubhir mahātmā sarvā diśo vyāvṛṇod aprameyaiḥ
pradīptolkam abhavac cāntarikṣaṃ deheṣu bhūrīṇy apatan vayāṃsi
kirīṭamālī mahatā mahāyaśāḥ śarāsanenāsya śarān anīkajit
gadāś ca gurvīḥ parighān ayasmayān asīṃś ca śaktīś ca raṇe narādhipāḥ
mahānti śastrāṇi ca bhīmadarśanāḥ pragṛhya pārthaṃ sahasābhidudruvuḥ
sa tān udīrṇān sarathāśvavāraṇān padātisaṃghāṃś ca mahādhanurdharaḥ
vipannasarvāyudhajīvitān raṇe cakāra vīro yamarāṣṭravardhanān
saṃjaya uvāca
sa raṇe vyacarat pārthaḥ prekṣaṇīyo dhanaṃjayaḥ
yugapad dikṣu sarvāsu citrāṇy astrāṇi darśayan
na śekuḥ sarvabhūtāni pāṇḍavaṃ prativīkṣitum
prasṛtāṃs tasya gāṇḍīvāc charavrātān mahātmanaḥ
saṃgrāme samapaśyāma haṃsapaṅktīr ivāmbare
vinivārya sa vīrāṇām astrair astrāṇi sarvaśaḥ
darśayan raudram ātmānam ugre karmaṇi dhiṣṭhitaḥ
visṛjan dikṣu sarvāsu śarān asitasārathiḥ
sa raṇe vyacarat tūrṇaṃ prekṣaṇīyo dhanaṃjayaḥ
bhramanta iva śūrasya śaravrātā mahātmanaḥ
adṛśyantāntarikṣasthāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
ādadānaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ saṃdadhānaṃ ca pāṇḍavam
visṛjantaṃ ca kaunteyaṃ nānupaśyāmahe tadā
tathā sarvā diśo rājan sarvāṃś ca rathino raṇe
vivyādha ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
saindhavas tu tathā viddhaḥ śarair gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
sa varāhadhvajas tūrṇaṃ gārdhrapatrān ajihmagān
āśīviṣasamaprakhyān karmāraparimārjitān
mumoca niśitān saṃkhye sāyakān savyasācini
tribhis tu viddhvā gāṇḍīvaṃ nārācaiḥ ṣaḍbhir arjunam
aṣṭābhir vājino 'vidhyad dhvajaṃ caikena patriṇā
sa vikṣipyārjunas tīkṣṇān saindhavapreṣitāñ śarān
sāratheś ca śiraḥ kāyād dhvajaṃ ca samalaṃkṛtam
sa chinnayaṣṭiḥ sumahāñ śīryamāṇaḥ śarāhataḥ
varāhaḥ sindhurājasya papātāgniśikhopamaḥ
abravīt pāṇḍavaṃ tatra tvaramāṇo janārdanaḥ
astaṃ mahīdharaśreṣṭhaṃ yiyāsati divākaraḥ
śṛṇuṣvaiva ca me vākyaṃ jayadrathavadhaṃ prati
antarhitā tadā vāṇī meghadundubhinisvanā
tavātmajo 'yaṃ martyeṣu kulaśīladamādibhiḥ
guṇair bhaviṣyati vibho sadṛśo vaṃśayor dvayoḥ
kṣatriyapravaro loke nityaṃ śūrābhisatkṛtaḥ
śiraś chetsyati saṃkruddhaḥ śatrur nālakṣito bhuvi
jñātīn sarvān uvācedaṃ putrasnehābhipīḍitaḥ
dharaṇyāṃ mama putrasya pātayiṣyati yaḥ śiraḥ
tasyāpi śatadhā mūrdhā phaliṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
vṛddhakṣatro vanaṃ yātas tapaśceṣṭaṃ samāsthitaḥ
tasmāj jayadrathasya tvaṃ śiraś chittvā mahāmṛdhe
divyenāstreṇa ripuhan ghoreṇādbhutakarmaṇā
sakuṇḍalaṃ sindhupateḥ prabhañjanasutānuja
utsaṅge pātayasvāśu vṛddhakṣatrasya bhārata
atha tvam asya mūrdhānaṃ pātayiṣyasi bhūtale
tavāpi śatadhā mūrdhā phaliṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
yathā caitan na jānīyāt sa rājā pṛthivīpatiḥ
tathā kuru kuruśreṣṭha divyam astram upāśritaḥ
etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihan
sarvabhārasahaṃ śaśvadgandhamālyārcitaṃ śaram
sa tu gāṇḍīvanirmuktaḥ śaraḥ śyena ivāśugaḥ
durhṛdām apraharṣāya suhṛdāṃ harṣaṇāya ca
śaraiḥ kadambakīkṛtya kāle tasmiṃś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
saṃdhyām upāste tejasvī saṃbandhī tava māriṣa
upāsīnasya tasyātha kṛṣṇakeśaṃ sakuṇḍalam
tasyotsaṅge nipatitaṃ śiras tac cārukuṇḍalam
gate tasyāpi śatadhā mūrdhāgacchad ariṃdama
tataḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni vismayaṃ jagmur uttamam
vāsudevaś ca bībhatsuṃ praśaśaṃsa mahāratham
tato dṛṣṭvā vinihataṃ sindhurājaṃ jayadratham
bhīmaseno 'pi saṃgrāme bodhayann iva pāṇḍavam
siṃhanādena mahatā pūrayām āsa rodasī
taṃ śrutvā tu mahānādaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
tato vāditraghoṣeṇa svān yodhān abhiharṣayan
abhyavartata saṃgrāme bhāradvājaṃ yuyutsayā
droṇasya somakaiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
pāṇḍavās tu jayaṃ labdhvā saindhavaṃ vinihatya ca
arjuno 'pi raṇe yodhāṃs tāvakān rathasattamān
sa devaśatrūn iva devarājaḥ kirīṭamālī vyadhamat samantāt
yathā tamāṃsy abhyuditas tamoghnaḥ pūrvāṃ pratijñāṃ samavāpya vīraḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
saṃjaya uvāca
saindhavaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā raṇe pārthena māriṣa
amarṣavaśam āpannaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvatas tadā
mahatā śaravarṣeṇa pāṇḍavaṃ samavākirat
tāv enaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhau rathābhyāṃ rathasattamam
ubhāv ubhayatas tīkṣṇair viśikhair abhyavarṣatām
sa tathā śaravarṣābhyāṃ sumahadbhyāṃ mahābhujaḥ
pīḍyamānaḥ parām ārtim agamad rathināṃ varaḥ
cakārācāryakaṃ tatra kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya ca
mandavegān iṣūṃs tābhyām ajighāṃsur avāsṛjat
te nātibhṛśam abhyaghnan viśikhā jayacoditāḥ
bahutvāt tu parām ārtiṃ śarāṇāṃ tāv agacchatām
atha śāradvato rājan kaunteyaśarapīḍitaḥ
vihvalaṃ tam abhijñāya bhartāraṃ śarapīḍitam
aśvatthāmāpy apāyāsīt pāṇḍaveyād rathāntaram
dṛṣṭvā śāradvataṃ pārtho mūrchitaṃ śarapīḍitam
ratha eva maheṣvāsaḥ kṛpaṇaṃ paryadevayat
paśyann idaṃ mahāprājñaḥ kṣattā rājānam uktavān
nīyatāṃ paralokāya sādhv ayaṃ kulapāṃsanaḥ
tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ satyavādinaḥ
tatkṛte hy adya paśyāmi śaratalpagataṃ kṛpam
ko hi brāhmaṇam ācāryam abhidruhyeta mādṛśaḥ
ṛṣiputro mamācāryo droṇasya dayitaḥ sakhā
eṣa śete rathopasthe madbāṇair abhipīḍitaḥ
akāmayānena mayā viśikhair ardito bhṛśam
avāsīdad rathopasthe prāṇān pīḍayatīva me
śarārditena hi mayā prekṣaṇīyo mahādyutiḥ
kṛpaṇaṃ svarathe sannaṃ paśya kṛṣṇa yathā gatam
upākṛtya tu vai vidyām ācāryebhyo nararṣabhāḥ
ye tu vidyām upādāya gurubhyaḥ puruṣādhamāḥ
tad idaṃ narakāyādya kṛtaṃ karma mayā dhruvam
ācāryaṃ śaravarṣeṇa rathe sādayatā kṛpam
yat tat pūrvam upākurvann astraṃ mām abravīt kṛpaḥ
tad idaṃ vacanaṃ sādhor ācāryasya mahātmanaḥ
nānuṣṭhitaṃ tam evājau viśikhair abhivarṣatā
saindhavaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rādheyaḥ samupādravat
upāyāntaṃ tu rādheyaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārtho mahārathaḥ
eṣa prayāty ādhirathiḥ sātyakeḥ syandanaṃ prati
na mṛṣyati hataṃ nūnaṃ bhūriśravasam āhave
yatra yāty eṣa tatra tvaṃ codayāśvāñ janārdana
mā somadatteḥ padavīṃ gamayet sātyakiṃ vṛṣaḥ
evam ukto mahābāhuḥ keśavaḥ savyasācinā
pratyuvāca mahātejāḥ kālayuktam idaṃ vacaḥ
alam eṣa mahābāhuḥ karṇāyaiko hi pāṇḍava
kiṃ punar draupadeyābhyāṃ sahitaḥ sātvatarṣabhaḥ
na ca tāvat kṣamaḥ pārtha karṇena tava saṃgaraḥ
tvadarthaṃ pūjyamānaiṣā rakṣyate paravīrahan
ataḥ karṇaḥ prayātv atra sātvatasya yathā tathā
ahaṃ jñāsyāmi kauravya kālam asya durātmanaḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
yo 'sau karṇena vīreṇa vārṣṇeyasya samāgamaḥ
sātyakiś cāpi virathaḥ kaṃ samārūḍhavān ratham
cakrarakṣau ca pāñcālyau tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
saṃjaya uvāca
hanta te varṇayiṣyāmi yathāvṛttaṃ mahāraṇe
śuśrūṣasva sthiro bhūtvā durācaritam ātmanaḥ
vijetavyo yathā vīraḥ sātyakir yūpaketunā
atītānāgataṃ rājan sa hi vetti janārdanaḥ
ataḥ sūtaṃ samāhūya dārukaṃ saṃdideśa ha
ratho me yujyatāṃ kālyam iti rājan mahābalaḥ
na hi devā na gandharvā na yakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
mānavā vā vijetāraḥ kṛṣṇayoḥ santi ke cana
pitāmahapurogāś ca devāḥ siddhāś ca taṃ viduḥ
tayoḥ prabhāvam atulaṃ śṛṇu yuddhaṃ ca tad yathā
sātyakiṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ cābhyudyatāyudham
dadhmau śaṅkhaṃ mahāvegam ārṣabheṇātha mādhavaḥ
dāruko 'vetya saṃdeśaṃ śrutvā śaṅkhasya ca svanam
hayodagrair mahāvegair hemabhāṇḍavibhūṣitaiḥ
dhanaṃjayarathaṃ hitvā rādheyaṃ pratyudīyayuḥ
rādheyo 'pi mahārāja śaravarṣaṃ samutsṛjan
tādṛśaṃ bhuvi vā yuddhaṃ divi vā śrutam ity uta
tayor dṛṣṭvā mahārāja karma saṃmūḍhacetanam
gatapratyāgatāvṛttair maṇḍalaiḥ saṃnivartanaiḥ
atīvāvahitā draṣṭuṃ karṇaśaineyayo raṇam
mitrārthe tau parākrāntau spardhinau śuṣmiṇau raṇe
karṇaś cāmarasaṃkāśo yuyudhānaś ca sātyakiḥ
anyonyaṃ tau mahārāja śaravarṣair avarṣatām
pramamātha śineḥ pautraṃ karṇaḥ sāyakavṛṣṭibhiḥ
amṛṣyamāṇo nidhanaṃ kauravyajalasaṃdhayoḥ
karṇaḥ śokasamāviṣṭo mahoraga iva śvasan
sa śaineyaṃ raṇe kruddhaḥ pradahann iva cakṣuṣā
mahatā śaravarṣeṇa gajaḥ pratigajaṃ yathā
tataḥ karṇaṃ śineḥ pautraḥ sarvapāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ
sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apāharat
aśvāṃś ca caturaḥ śvetān nijaghne niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
chittvā dhvajaṃ śatenaiva śatadhā puruṣarṣabhaḥ
cakāra virathaṃ karṇaṃ tava putrasya paśyataḥ
tato vimanaso rājaṃs tāvakāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
vṛṣasenaḥ karṇasutaḥ śalyo madrādhipas tathā
tataḥ paryākulaṃ sarvaṃ na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
tathā sātyakinā vīre virathe sūtaje kṛte
hāhākāras tato rājan sarvasainyeṣu cābhavat
karṇo 'pi vihvalo rājan sātvatenārditaḥ śaraiḥ
kṛtāṃ rājyapradānena pratijñāṃ paripālayan
duḥśāsanamukhāñ śūrān nāvadhīt sātyakir vaśī
rakṣan pratijñāṃ ca punar bhīmasenakṛtāṃ purā
bhīmasenena tu vadhaḥ putrāṇāṃ te pratiśrutaḥ
punardyūte ca pārthena vadhaḥ karṇasya śaṃśrutaḥ
nāśaknuvaṃś ca taṃ hantuṃ sātyakiṃ pravarā rathāḥ
drauṇiś ca kṛtavarmā ca tathaivānye mahārathāḥ
nirjitā dhanuṣaikena śataśaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
kāṅkṣatā paralokaṃ ca dharmarājasya ca priyam
kṛṣṇayoḥ sadṛśo vīrye sātyakiḥ śatrukarśanaḥ
kṛṣṇo vāpi bhavel loke pārtho vāpi dhanurdharaḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
ajayyaṃ ratham āsthāya vāsudevasya sātyakiḥ
virathaṃ kṛtavān karṇaṃ vāsudevasamo yuvā
dārukeṇa samāyuktaṃ svabāhubaladarpitaḥ
kaccid anyaṃ samārūḍhaḥ sa rathaṃ sātyakiḥ punaḥ
etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ kuśalo hy asi bhāṣitum
saṃjaya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan yathā tasya ratham anyaṃ mahāmatiḥ
dārukasyānujas tūrṇaṃ kalpanāvidhikalpitam
āyasaiḥ kāñcanaiś cāpi paṭṭair naddhaṃ sakūbaram
aśvair vātajavair yuktaṃ hemabhāṇḍaparicchadaiḥ
pāṇḍurair indusaṃkāśaiḥ sarvaśabdātigair dṛḍhaiḥ
citrakāñcanasaṃnāhair vājimukhyair viśāṃ pate
ghaṇṭājālākularavaṃ śaktitomaravidyutam
rathaṃ saṃpādayām āsa meghagambhīranisvanam
dāruko 'pi yathākāmaṃ prayayau keśavāntikam
karṇasyāpi mahārāja śaṅkhagokṣīrapāṇḍuraiḥ
citrakāñcanasaṃnāhaiḥ sadaśvair vegavattaraiḥ
etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
bhūyaś cāpi nibodha tvaṃ tavāpanayajaṃ kṣayam
ekatriṃśat tava sutā bhīmasenena pātitāḥ
śataśo nihatāḥ śūrāḥ sātvatenārjunena ca
bhīṣmaṃ pramukhataḥ kṛtvā bhagadattaṃ ca māriṣa
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
tathā gateṣu śūreṣu teṣāṃ mama ca saṃjaya
kiṃ vai bhīmas tadākārṣīt tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
saṃjaya uvāca
viratho bhīmaseno vai karṇavākśalyapīḍitaḥ
amarṣavaśam āpannaḥ phalgunaṃ vākyam abravīt
akṛtāstraka mā yodhīr bāla saṃgrāmakātara
iti mām abravīt karṇaḥ paśyatas te dhanaṃjaya
etad vrataṃ mahābāho tvayā saha kṛtaṃ mayā
karṇa karṇa vṛthādṛṣṭe sūtaputrātmasaṃstuta
adharmabuddhe śṛṇu me yat tvā vakṣyāmi sāṃpratam
dvividhaṃ karma śūrāṇāṃ yuddhe jayaparājayau
yadṛcchayā bhīmasenaṃ virathaṃ kṛtavān asi
pūrayantaṃ yathāśakti śūrakarmāhave tathā
paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ keśavasya mamaiva ca
na ca tvāṃ paruṣaṃ kiṃ cid uktavān paṇḍunandanaḥ
yasmāt tu bahu rūkṣaṃ ca śrāvitas te vṛkodaraḥ
tvayā tasya dhanuś chinnam ātmanāśāya durmate
tasmād vadhyo 'si me mūḍha sabhṛtyabalavāhanaḥ
hantāsmi vṛṣasenaṃ te prekṣamāṇasya saṃyuge
ye cānye 'py upayāsyanti buddhimohena māṃ nṛpāḥ
tāṃś ca sarvān haniṣyāmi satyenāyudham ālabhe
tvāṃ ca mūḍhākṛtaprajñam atimāninam āhave
dṛṣṭvā duryodhano mando bhṛśaṃ tapsyati pātitam
mahān sutumulaḥ śabdo babhūva rathināṃ tadā
mandaraśmiḥ sahasrāṃśur astaṃ girim upāgamat
tato rājan hṛṣīkeśaḥ saṃgrāmaśirasi sthitam
tīrṇapratijñaṃ bībhatsuṃ pariṣvajyedam abravīt
diṣṭyā saṃpāditā jiṣṇo pratijñā mahatī tvayā
diṣṭyā ca nihataḥ pāpo vṛddhakṣatraḥ sahātmajaḥ
dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ prāpya devasenāpi bhārata
sīdeta samare jiṣṇo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
na taṃ paśyāmi lokeṣu cintayan puruṣaṃ kva cit
mahāprabhāvā bahavas tvayā tulyādhikāpi vā
sametāḥ pṛthivīpālā dhārtarāṣṭrasya kāraṇāt
te tvāṃ prāpya raṇe kruddhaṃ nābhyavartanta daṃśitāḥ
nedṛśaṃ śaknuyāt kaś cid raṇe kartuṃ parākramam
yādṛśaṃ kṛtavān adya tvam ekaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ
vardhayiṣyāmi bhūyas tvāṃ vijitāriṃ hatadviṣam
pratijñeyaṃ mayottīrṇā vibudhair api dustarā
anāścaryo jayas teṣāṃ yeṣāṃ nātho 'si mādhava
tvatprasādān mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ saṃprāpsyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
vardhanīyās tava vayaṃ preṣyāś ca madhusūdana
evam uktaḥ smayan kṛṣṇaḥ śanakair vāhayan hayān
darśayām āsa pārthāya krūram āyodhanaṃ mahat
śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca
pṛthivyāṃ śerate śūrāḥ pārthivās tvaccharair hatāḥ
vikīrṇaśastrābharaṇā vipannāśvarathadvipāḥ
saṃchinnabhinnavarmāṇo vaiklavyaṃ paramaṃ gatāḥ
sasattvā gatasattvāś ca prabhayā parayā yutāḥ
sajīvā iva lakṣyante gatasattvā narādhipāḥ
teṣāṃ śaraiḥ svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śastraiś ca vividhaiḥ śitaiḥ
vāhanair āyudhaiś caiva saṃpūrṇāṃ paśya medinīm
varmabhiś carmabhir hāraiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥ
uṣṇīṣair mukuṭaiḥ sragbhiś cūḍāmaṇibhir ambaraiḥ
kaṇṭhasūtrair aṅgadaiś ca niṣkair api ca suprabhaiḥ
anyaiś cābharaṇaiś citrair bhāti bhārata medinī
vividhaiś ca paristomair aśvānāṃ ca prakīrṇakaiḥ
kuthābhiś ca vicitrābhir varūthaiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
saṃstīrṇāṃ vasudhāṃ paśya citrapaṭṭair ivāvṛtām
saṃsyūtān vājibhiḥ sārdhaṃ dharaṇyāṃ paśya cāparān
padātisādisaṃghāṃś ca kṣatajaughapariplutān
saṃjaya uvāca
evaṃ saṃdarśayan kṛṣṇo raṇabhūmiṃ kirīṭinaḥ
svaiḥ sametaḥ sa muditaḥ pāñcajanyaṃ vyanādayat
saṃjaya uvāca
tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā rathād āplutya bhārata
paryaṣvajat tadā kṛṣṇāv ānandāśrupariplutaḥ
pramṛjya vadanaṃ śubhraṃ puṇḍarīkasamaprabham
abravīd vāsudevaṃ ca pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃgrāme tīrṇabhārau mahārathau
diṣṭyā ca nihataḥ pāpaḥ saindhavaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ
kṛṣṇa diṣṭyā mama prītir mahatī pratipāditā
diṣṭyā śatrugaṇāś caiva nimagnāḥ śokasāgare
na teṣāṃ duṣkaraṃ kiṃ cit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate
sarvalokagurur yeṣāṃ tvaṃ nātho madhusūdana
tava prasādād govinda vayaṃ jeṣyāmahe ripūn
yathā pūrvaṃ prasādāt te dānavān pākaśāsanaḥ
dhruvo hi teṣāṃ vārṣṇeya yeṣāṃ tuṣṭo 'si mādhava
na teṣāṃ vidyate pāpaṃ saṃgrāme vā parājayaḥ
tridaśeśvaranāthas tvaṃ yeṣāṃ tuṣṭo 'si mādhava
tvatprasādād dhṛṣīkeśa śakraḥ suragaṇeśvaraḥ
trailokyavijayaṃ śrīmān prāptavān raṇamūrdhani
amaratvaṃ gatāḥ kṛṣṇa lokāṃś cāśnuvate 'kṣayān
sureśatvaṃ gataḥ śakro hatvā daityān sahasraśaḥ
tvatprasādād dhṛṣīkeśa jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam
ekārṇavam idaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvam āsīt tamomayam
tvatprasādāt prakāśatvaṃ jagat prāptaṃ narottama
sraṣṭāraṃ sarvalokānāṃ paramātmānam acyutam
ye prapannā hṛṣīkeśaṃ na te muhyanti karhi cit
tvāṃ bhaktā ye hṛṣīkeśa durgāṇy atitaranti te
paraṃ purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇānāṃ paraṃ ca yat
taṃ prapadya mahātmānaṃ bhūtim āpnoty anuttamām
dhanaṃjayasakhā yaś ca dhanaṃjayahitaś ca yaḥ
ity uktau tau mahātmānāv ubhau keśavapāṇḍavau
tāv abrūtāṃ tadā hṛṣṭau rājānaṃ pṛthivīpatim
tava kopāgninā dagdhaḥ pāpo rājā jayadrathaḥ
udīrṇaṃ cāpi sumahad dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ raṇe
tvāṃ hi cakṣurhaṇaṃ vīraṃ kopayitvā suyodhanaḥ
samitrabandhuḥ samare prāṇāṃs tyakṣyati durmatiḥ
śaratalpagataḥ śete bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
durlabho hi jayas teṣāṃ saṃgrāme ripusūdana
yātā mṛtyuvaśaṃ te vai yeṣāṃ kruddho 'si pāṇḍava
rājyaṃ prāṇāḥ priyāḥ putrāḥ saukhyāni vividhāni ca
acirāt tasya naśyanti yeṣāṃ kruddho 'si mānada
vinaṣṭān kauravān manye saputrapaśubāndhavān
tato bhīmo mahābāhuḥ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
abhivādya guruṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ mārgaṇaiḥ kṣatavikṣatau
sthitāv āstāṃ maheṣvāsau pāñcālyaiḥ parivāritau
tau dṛṣṭva muditau vīrau prāñjalī cāgrataḥ sthitau
diṣṭyā paśyāmi vāṃ vīrau vimuktau sainyasāgarāt
droṇagrāhād durādharṣād dhārdikyamakarālayāt
diṣṭyā ca nirjitāḥ saṃkhye pṛthivyāṃ sarvapārthivāḥ
yuvāṃ vijayinau cāpi diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃyuge
diṣṭyā droṇo jitaḥ saṃkhye hārdikyaś ca mahābalaḥ
sainyārṇavaṃ samuttīrṇau diṣṭyā paśyāmi cānaghau
mama prāṇasamau caiva diṣṭyā paśyāmi vām aham
ity uktvā pāṇḍavo rājā yuyudhānavṛkodarau
sasvaje puruṣavyāghrau harṣād bāṣpaṃ mumoca ha
tataḥ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ balam āsīd viśāṃ pate
pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaṃ dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya ca mano dadhe
saṃjaya uvāca
na droṇo na ca rādheyo nāśvatthāmā kṛpo na ca
na hy asya vidyate trātā sākṣād api puraṃdaraḥ
yam upāśritya saṃgrāme kṛtaḥ śastrasamudyamaḥ
paruṣāṇi sabhāmadhye proktavān yaḥ sma pāṇḍavān
yasya vīryaṃ samāśritya śamaṃ yācantam acyutam
evaṃ klāntamanā rājann upāyād droṇam īkṣitum
tatas tat sarvam ācakhyau kurūṇāṃ vaiśasaṃ mahat
parān vijayataś cāpi dhārtarāṣṭrān nimajjataḥ
paśya mūrdhāvasiktānām ācārya kadanaṃ kṛtam
kṛtvā pramukhataḥ śūraṃ bhīṣmaṃ mama pitāmaham
taṃ nihatya pralubdho 'yaṃ śikhaṇḍī pūrṇamānasaḥ
pāñcālaiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ senāgram abhikarṣati
aparaś cāpi durdharṣaḥ śiṣyas te savyasācinā
akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta hatvā hato rājā jayadrathaḥ
asmadvijayakāmānāṃ suhṛdām upakāriṇām
gantāsmi katham ānṛṇyaṃ gatānāṃ yamasādanam
ye madarthaṃ parīpsanti vasudhāṃ vasudhādhipāḥ
so 'haṃ kāpuruṣaḥ kṛtvā mitrāṇāṃ kṣayam īdṛśam
nāśvamedhasahasreṇa pātum ātmānam utsahe
vyāyacchanto jigīṣantaḥ prāptā vaivasvatakṣayam
kathaṃ patitavṛttasya pṛthivī suhṛdāṃ druhaḥ
vivaraṃ nāśakad dātuṃ mama pārthivasaṃsadi
so 'haṃ rudhirasiktāṅgaṃ rājñāṃ madhye pitāmaham
śayānaṃ nāśakaṃ trātuṃ bhīṣmam āyodhane hatam
taṃ mām anāryapuruṣaṃ mitradruham adhārmikam
jalasaṃdhaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ paśya sātyakinā hatam
madartham udyataṃ śūraṃ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā mahāratham
kāmbojaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā tathālambusam eva ca
anyān bahūṃś ca suhṛdo jīvitārtho 'dya ko mama
vyāyacchanto hatāḥ śūrā madarthe ye 'parāṅmukhāḥ
yatamānāḥ paraṃ śaktyā vijetum ahitān mama
teṣāṃ gatvāham ānṛṇyam adya śaktyā paraṃtapa
satyaṃ te pratijānāmi sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ vara
iṣṭāpūrtena ca śape vīryeṇa ca sutair api
nihatya tān raṇe sarvān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
śāntiṃ labdhāsmi teṣāṃ vā raṇe gantā salokatām
na hīdānīṃ sahāyā me parīpsanty anupaskṛtāḥ
śreyo hi pāṇḍūn manyante na tathāsmān mahābhuja
bhavān upekṣāṃ kurute suśiṣyatvād dhanaṃjaye
yo hi mitram avijñāya yāthātathyena mandadhīḥ
tādṛgrūpam idaṃ kāryaṃ kṛtaṃ mama suhṛdbruvaiḥ
abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayo 'tha vasātayaḥ
so 'ham adya gamiṣyāmi yatra te puruṣarṣabhāḥ
hatā madarthaṃ saṃgrāme yudhyamānāḥ kirīṭinā
na hi me jīvitenārthas tān ṛte puruṣarṣabhān
ācāryaḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇām anujānātu no bhavān
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
saṃjaya uvāca
niṣṭānako mahān āsīt sainyānāṃ tava bhārata
saindhavaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā bhūriśravasam eva ca
yena mantreṇa nihatāḥ śataśaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
muhūrtam iva tu dhyātvā bhṛśam ārto 'bhyabhāṣata
duryodhana kim evaṃ māṃ vākśarair abhikṛntasi
ajayyaṃ samare nityaṃ bruvāṇaṃ savyasācinam
etenaivārjunaṃ jñātum alaṃ kaurava saṃyuge
yac chikhaṇḍy avadhīd bhīṣmaṃ pālyamānaḥ kirīṭinā
avadhyaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃyuge devamānuṣaiḥ
tadaivājñāsiṣam ahaṃ neyam astīti bhāratī
yaṃ puṃsāṃ triṣu lokeṣu sarvaśūram amaṃsmahi
tasmin vinihate śūre kiṃ śeṣaṃ paryupāsmahe
yān sma tān glahate tātaḥ śakuniḥ kurusaṃsadi
akṣān na te 'kṣā niśitā bāṇās te śatrutāpanāḥ
yāṃs tadā khyāpyamānāṃs tvaṃ vidureṇa na budhyase
tās tā vilapataś cāpi vidurasya mahātmanaḥ
dhīrasya vāco nāśrauṣīḥ kṣemāya vadataḥ śivāḥ
yac ca naḥ prekṣamāṇānāṃ kṛṣṇām ānāyayaḥ sabhām
anarhatīṃ kule jātāṃ sarvadharmānucāriṇīm
tasyādharmasya gāndhāre phalaṃ prāptam idaṃ tvayā
yac ca tān pāṇḍavān dyūte viṣameṇa vijitya ha
prāvrājayas tadāraṇye rauravājinavāsasaḥ
putrāṇām iva caiteṣāṃ dharmam ācaratāṃ sadā
pāṇḍavānām ayaṃ kopas tvayā śakuninā saha
āhṛto dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saṃmate kurusaṃsadi
duḥśāsanena saṃyuktaḥ karṇena parivardhitaḥ
kṣattur vākyam anādṛtya tvayābhyastaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
āśaṃsata paritrāṇam arjunāt sa mahīpatiḥ
na kiṃ cid anupaśyāmi jīvitatrāṇam ātmanaḥ
majjantam iva cātmānaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya kilbiṣe
paśyāmy ahatvā pāñcālān saha tena śikhaṇḍinā
aśaktaḥ sindhurājasya bhūtvā trāṇāya bhārata
sauvarṇaṃ satyasaṃdhasya dhvajam akliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
apaśyan yudhi bhīṣmasya katham āśaṃsase jayam
hato bhūriśravāś caiva kiṃ śeṣaṃ tatra manyase
yac cāpaśyaṃ hataṃ bhīṣmaṃ paśyatas te 'nujasya vai
duḥśāsanasya kauravya kurvāṇaṃ karma duṣkaram
imāni pāṇḍavānāṃ ca sṛñjayānāṃ ca bhārata
anīkāny ādravante māṃ sahitāny adya māriṣa
nāhatvā sarvapāñcālān kavacasya vimokṣaṇam
kartāsmi samare karma dhārtarāṣṭra hitaṃ tava
rājan brūyāḥ sutaṃ me tvam aśvatthāmānam āhave
na somakāḥ pramoktavyā jīvitaṃ parirakṣatā
yac ca pitrānuśiṣṭo 'si tad vacaḥ paripālaya
dharmārthakāmakuśalo dharmārthāv apy apīḍayan
dharmapradhānaḥ kāryāṇi kuryāś ceti punaḥ punaḥ
cakṣurmanobhyāṃ saṃtoṣyā viprāḥ sevyāś ca śaktitaḥ
na caiṣāṃ vipriyaṃ kāryaṃ te hi vahniśikhopamāḥ
eṣa tv aham anīkāni praviśāmy arisūdana
raṇāya mahate rājaṃs tvayā vākśalyapīḍitaḥ
rātrāv api hi yotsyante saṃrabdhāḥ kurusṛñjayāḥ
evam uktvā tataḥ prāyād droṇaḥ pāṇḍavasṛñjayān
muṣṇan kṣatriyatejāṃsi nakṣatrāṇām ivāṃśumān
saṃjaya uvāca
paśya kṛṣṇasahāyena pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā
ācāryavihitaṃ vyūhaṃ bhinnaṃ devaiḥ sudurbhidam
miṣatāṃ yodhamukhyānāṃ saindhavo vinipātitaḥ
paśya rādheya rājānaḥ pṛthivyāṃ pravarā yudhi
pārthenaikena nihatāḥ siṃhenevetarā mṛgāḥ
alpāvaśeṣaṃ sainyaṃ me kṛtaṃ śakrātmajena ha
abhayaṃ saindhavasyājau dattvā droṇaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
prādāt kirīṭine dvāraṃ paśya nirguṇatāṃ mama
yady adāsyam anujñāṃ vai pūrvam eva gṛhān prati
jayadratho jīvitārthī gacchamāno gṛhān prati
mayānāryeṇa saṃruddho droṇāt prāpyābhayaṃ raṇe
adya me bhrātaraḥ kṣīṇāś citrasenādayo yudhi
bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya paśyatāṃ no durātmanām
karṇa uvāca
ācāryaṃ mā vigarhasva śaktyā yudhyaty asau dvijaḥ
ajayyān pāṇḍavān manye droṇenāstravidā mṛdhe
tathā hy enam atikramya praviṣṭaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
tato no yudhyamānānāṃ paraṃ śaktyā suyodhana
paraṃ yatnaṃ kurvatāṃ ca tvayā sārdhaṃ raṇājire
hatvāsmākaṃ pauruṣaṃ hi daivaṃ paścāt karoti naḥ
satataṃ ceṣṭamānānāṃ nikṛtyā vikrameṇa ca
yat kartavyaṃ manuṣyeṇa vyavasāyavatā satā
nikṛtyā nikṛtāḥ pārthā viṣayogaiś ca bhārata
dagdhā jatugṛhe cāpi dyūtena ca parājitāḥ
rājanītiṃ vyapāśritya prahitāś caiva kānanam
yatatas tava teṣāṃ ca daivaṃ mārgeṇa yāsyati
na teṣāṃ matipūrvaṃ hi sukṛtaṃ dṛśyate kva cit
duṣkṛtaṃ tava vā vīra buddhyā hīnaṃ kurūdvaha
daivaṃ pramāṇaṃ sarvasya sukṛtasyetarasya vā
na tathā pāṇḍuputrāṇām evaṃ yuddham avartata
tair alpair bahavo yūyaṃ kṣayaṃ nītāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
śaṅke daivasya tat karma pauruṣaṃ yena nāśitam
saṃjaya uvāca
evaṃ saṃbhāṣamāṇānāṃ bahu tat taj janādhipa
pāṇḍavānām anīkāni samadṛśyanta saṃyuge
tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ sārdhaṃ rājan durmantrite tava
saṃjaya uvāca
tad udīrṇagajāśvaughaṃ balaṃ tava janādhipa
pāṇḍusenām abhidrutya yodhayām āsa sarvataḥ
pāñcālāḥ kuravaś caiva yodhayantaḥ parasparam
yamarāṣṭrāya mahate paralokāya dīkṣitāḥ
śūrāḥ śūraiḥ samāgamya śaratomaraśaktibhiḥ
rathināṃ rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ rudhirasrāvi dāruṇam
vāraṇāś ca mahārāja samāsādya parasparam
viṣāṇair dārayām āsuḥ saṃkruddhāś ca madotkaṭāḥ
hayārohān hayārohāḥ prāsaśaktiparaśvadhaiḥ
pattayaś ca mahābāho śataśaḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ
gotrāṇāṃ nāmadheyānāṃ kulānāṃ caiva māriṣa
śravaṇād dhi vijānīmaḥ pāñcālān kurubhiḥ saha
anyonyaṃ samare yodhāḥ śaraśaktiparaśvadhaiḥ
śarair daśa diśo rājaṃs teṣāṃ muktaiḥ sahasraśaḥ
tathā prayudhyamāneṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu nirbhayaḥ
abhyavartata putras te pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
sa saṃnipātas tumulas tasya teṣāṃ ca bhārata
na śekur bhārataṃ yuddhe pāṇḍavāḥ samavekṣitum
palāyane kṛtotsāhā nirutsāhā dviṣajjaye
paryadhāvanta pāñcālā vadhyamānā mahātmanā
ardyamānāḥ śarais tūrṇaṃ nyapatan pāṇḍusainikāḥ
na tādṛśaṃ raṇe karma kṛtavantas tu tāvakāḥ
yādṛśaṃ kṛtavān rājā putras tava viśāṃ pate
putreṇa tava sā senā pāṇḍavī mathitā raṇe
kṣīṇatoyānilārkābhyāṃ hatatviḍ iva padminī
babhūva pāṇḍavī senā tava putrasya tejasā
pāṇḍusenāṃ hatāṃ dṛṣṭvā tava putreṇa bhārata
bhīmasenapurogās tu pāñcālāḥ samupādravan
virāṭadrupadau ṣaḍbhiḥ śatena ca śikhaṇḍinam
dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca saptatyā dharmaputraṃ ca saptabhiḥ
kekayāṃś caiva cedīṃś ca bahubhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
śataśaś cāparān yodhān sadvipāśvarathān raṇe
tasya tān nighnataḥ śatrūn rukmapṛṣṭhaṃ mahad dhanuḥ
bhallābhyāṃ pāṇḍavo jyeṣṭhas tridhā ciccheda māriṣa
vivyādha cainaṃ daśabhiḥ samyagastaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
marmāṇi bhittvā te sarve saṃbhagnāḥ kṣitim āviśan
tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā tava putrasya māriṣa
śaraṃ paramadurvāraṃ preṣayām āsa saṃyuge
tataḥ pāñcālasainyānāṃ bhṛśam āsīd ravo mahān
hato rājeti rājendra muditānāṃ samantataḥ
bāṇaśabdaravaś cograḥ śuśruve tatra māriṣa
hṛṣṭo duryodhanaś cāpi dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam
tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti rājānaṃ bruvan pāṇḍavam abhyayāt
pratyudyayus taṃ tvaritāḥ pāñcālā rājagṛddhinaḥ
caṇḍavātoddhatān meghān nighnan raśmimuco yathā
tato rājan mahān āsīt saṃgrāmo bhūrivardhanaḥ
tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca sametānāṃ yuyutsayā
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
yat tadā prāviśat pāṇḍūn ācāryaḥ kupito vaśī
uktvā duryodhanaṃ samyaṅ mama śāstrātigaṃ sutam
kathaṃ droṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ paryavārayan
ke 'rakṣan dakṣiṇaṃ cakram ācāryasya mahātmanaḥ
ke cottaram arakṣanta nighnataḥ śātravān raṇe
nṛtyan sa rathamārgeṣu sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
sāyāhne saindhavaṃ hatvā rājñā pārthaḥ sametya ca
sātyakiś ca maheṣvāso droṇam evābhyadhāvatām
tathā yudhiṣṭhiras tūrṇaṃ bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
pṛthak camūbhyāṃ saṃsaktau droṇam evābhyadhāvatām
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śatānīko virāṭaś ca sakekayaḥ
matsyāḥ śālveyasenāś ca droṇam eva yayur yudhi
drupadaś ca tathā rājā pāñcālair abhirakṣitaḥ
dhṛṣṭadyumnapitā rājan droṇam evābhyavartata
draupadeyā maheṣvāsā rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
prabhadrakāś ca pāñcālāḥ ṣaṭsahasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
tathetare naravyāghrāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
teṣu śūreṣu yuddhāya gateṣu bharatarṣabha
babhūva rajanī ghorā bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinī
yodhānām aśivā raudrā rājann antakagāminī
kuñjarāśvamanuṣyāṇāṃ prāṇāntakaraṇī tadā
tasyāṃ rajanyāṃ ghorāyāṃ nadantyaḥ sarvataḥ śivāḥ
ulūkāś cāpy adṛśyanta śaṃsanto vipulaṃ bhayam
viśeṣataḥ kauravāṇāṃ dhvajinyām atidāruṇam
bherīśabdena mahatā mṛdaṅgānāṃ svanena ca
gajānāṃ garjitaiś cāpi turaṅgāṇāṃ ca heṣitaiḥ
tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ saṃdhyāyām atidāruṇam
droṇasya ca mahārāja sṛñjayānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
tamasā cāvṛte loke na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
nāpaśyāma rajo bhaumaṃ kaśmalenābhisaṃvṛtāḥ
ghoraś caṭacaṭāśabdaḥ śastrāṇāṃ patatām abhūt
bhaumaṃ rajo 'tha rājendra śoṇitena praśāmitam
śātakaumbhaiś ca kavacair bhūṣaṇaiś ca tamo 'bhyagāt
tataḥ sā bhāratī senā maṇihemavibhūṣitā
dyaur ivāsīt sanakṣatrā rajanyāṃ bharatarṣabha
gomāyubaḍasaṃghuṣṭā śaktidhvajasamākulā
dāruṇābhirutā ghorā kṣveḍitotkruṣṭanāditā
samāvṛṇvan diśaḥ sarvā mahendrāśaninisvanaḥ
sā niśīthe mahārāja senādṛśyata bhāratī
aṅgadaiḥ kuṇḍalair niṣkaiḥ śastraiś caivāvabhāsitā
tatra nāgā rathāś caiva jāmbūnadavibhūṣitāḥ
niśāyāṃ pratyadṛśyanta meghā iva savidyutaḥ
ṛṣṭiśaktigadābāṇamusalaprāsapaṭṭiśāḥ
saṃpatanto vyadṛśyanta bhrājamānā ivāgnayaḥ
duryodhanapurovātāṃ rathanāgabalāhakām
vāditraghoṣastanitāṃ cāpavidyuddhvajair vṛtām
droṇapāṇḍavaparjanyāṃ khaḍgaśaktigadāśanim
śaradhārāstrapavanāṃ bhṛśaṃ śītoṣṇasaṃkulām
ghorāṃ vismāpanīm ugrāṃ jīvitacchidam aplavām
tāṃ prāviśann atibhayāṃ senāṃ yuddhacikīrṣavaḥ
bhīrūṇāṃ trāsajanane śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhane
droṇam abhyadravan kruddhāḥ sahitāḥ pāṇḍusṛñjayāḥ
tān sarvān vimukhāṃś cakre kāṃś cin ninye yamakṣayam
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
amṛṣyamāṇe saṃrabdhe kā vo 'bhūd vai matis tadā
duryodhanaṃ tathā putram uktvā śāstrātigaṃ mama
yat prāviśad ameyātmā kiṃ pārthaḥ pratyapadyata
yad abhyagān mahātejāḥ pāñcālān aparājitaḥ
kim amanyata durdharṣaḥ praviṣṭe śatrutāpane
ke cāsya pṛṣṭhato 'gacchan vīrāḥ śūrasya yudhyataḥ
manye 'haṃ pāṇḍavān sarvān bhāradvājaśarārditān
śiśire kampamānā vai kṛśā gāva ivābhibho
praviśya sa maheṣvāsaḥ pāñcālān arimardanaḥ
sarveṣu sainyeṣu ca saṃgateṣu rātrau sameteṣu mahāratheṣu
saṃloḍyamāneṣu pṛthagvidheṣu ke vas tadānīṃ matimanta āsan
hatāṃś caiva viṣaktāṃś ca parābhūtāṃś ca śaṃsasi
rathino virathāṃś caiva kṛtān yuddheṣu māmakān
katham eṣāṃ tadā tatra pārthānām apalāyinām
prakāśam abhavad rātrau kathaṃ kuruṣu saṃjaya
saṃjaya uvāca
rātriyuddhe tadā rājan vartamāne sudāruṇe
droṇam abhyadravan rātrau pāṇḍavāḥ sahasainikāḥ
tato droṇaḥ kekayāṃś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnasya cātmajān
preṣayan mṛtyulokāya sarvān iṣubhir āśugaiḥ
tān sarvān preṣayām āsa paralokāya bhārata
pramathnantaṃ tadā vīraṃ bhāradvājaṃ mahāratham
abhyavartata saṃkruddhaḥ śibī rājan pratāpavān
tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāratham
vivyādha daśabhir droṇaḥ sarvapāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ
taṃ śibiḥ prativivyādha triṃśatā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
tasya droṇo hayān hatvā sārathiṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
athāsya saśirastrāṇaṃ śiraḥ kāyād apāharat
kaliṅgānāṃ ca sainyena kaliṅgasya suto raṇe
kaliṅgānāṃ tu taṃ śūraṃ kruddhaṃ kruddho vṛkodaraḥ
tasya muṣṭihatasyājau pāṇḍavena balīyasā
sarvāṇy asthīni sahasā prāpatan vai pṛthak pṛthak
taṃ karṇo bhrātaraś cāsya nāmṛṣyanta mahārathāḥ
te bhīmasenaṃ nārācair jaghnur āśīviṣopamaiḥ
tataḥ śatrurathaṃ tyaktvā bhīmo dhruvarathaṃ gataḥ
dhruvaṃ cāsyantam aniśaṃ muṣṭinā samapothayat
sa tathā pāṇḍuputreṇa balinā nihato 'patat
taṃ nihatya mahārāja bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
jayarātarathaṃ prāpya muhuḥ siṃha ivānadat
jayarātam athākṣipya nadan savyena pāṇinā
talena nāśayām āsa karṇasyaivāgrataḥ sthitam
karṇas tu pāṇḍave śaktiṃ kāñcanīṃ samavāsṛjat
tatas tām eva jagrāha prahasan pāṇḍunandanaḥ
karṇāyaiva ca durdharṣaś cikṣepājau vṛkodaraḥ
mahatā śaravarṣeṇa chādayanto vṛkodaram
sārathiṃ ca hayāṃś caiva śarair ninye yamakṣayam
tāv ekaratham ārūḍhau bhrātarau paratāpanau
saṃgrāmaśiraso madhye bhīmaṃ dvāv abhyadhāvatām
ratham ekaṃ samāruhya bhīmaṃ bāṇair avidhyatām
kṛpasya somadattasya bāhlīkasya ca pāṇḍavaḥ
pādaprahāreṇa dharāṃ prāveśayad ariṃdamaḥ
tato hāhākṛte sainye dṛṣṭvā bhīmaṃ nṛpābruvan
rudro 'yaṃ bhīmarūpeṇa dhārtarāṣṭreṣu gṛdhyati
evam uktvāpalāyanta sarve bhārata pārthivāḥ
visaṃjñāvāhayan vāhān na ca dvau saha dhāvataḥ
tato bale bhṛśalulite niśāmukhe supūjito nṛpavṛṣabhair vṛkodaraḥ
tato yamau drupadavirāṭakekayā yudhiṣṭhiraś cāpi parāṃ mudaṃ yayuḥ
vṛkodaraṃ bhṛśam abhipūjayaṃś ca te yathāndhake pratinihate haraṃ surāḥ
tataḥ sutās tava varuṇātmajopamā ruṣānvitāḥ saha guruṇā mahātmanā
niśāmukhe baḍavṛkagṛdhramodanaṃ mahātmanāṃ nṛpavarayuddham adbhutam
saṃjaya uvāca
prāyopaviṣṭe tu hate putre sātyakinā tataḥ
somadatto bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ sātyakiṃ vākyam abravīt
kṣatradharmaḥ purā dṛṣṭo yas tu devair mahātmabhiḥ
parāṅmukhāya dīnāya nyastaśastrāya yācate
kṣatradharmarataḥ prājñaḥ kathaṃ nu prahared raṇe
dvāv eva kila vṛṣṇīnāṃ tatra khyātau mahārathau
kathaṃ prāyopaviṣṭāya pārthena chinnabāhave
nṛśaṃsaṃ patanīyaṃ ca tādṛśaṃ kṛtavān asi
śape sātvata putrābhyām iṣṭena sukṛtena ca
anatītām imāṃ rātriṃ yadi tvāṃ vīramāninam
arakṣyamāṇaṃ pārthena jiṣṇunā sasutānujam
na hanyāṃ niraye ghore pateyaṃ vṛṣṇipāṃsana
dadhmau śaṅkhaṃ ca tāreṇa siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ca
tataḥ kamalapatrākṣaḥ siṃhadaṃṣṭro mahābalaḥ
sātvato bhṛśasaṃkruddhaḥ somadattam athābravīt
hato bhūriśravā vīras tava putro mahārathaḥ
śalaś caiva tathā rājan bhrātṛvyasanakarśitaḥ
tvāṃ cāpy adya vadhiṣyāmi saputrapaśubāndhavam
tiṣṭhedānīṃ raṇe yattaḥ kauravo 'si viśeṣataḥ
yasmin dānaṃ damaḥ śaucam ahiṃsā hrīr dhṛtiḥ kṣamā
anapāyīni sarvāṇi nityaṃ rājñi yudhiṣṭhire
mṛdaṅgaketos tasya tvaṃ tejasā nihataḥ purā
sakarṇasaubalaḥ saṃkhye vināśaṃ samupeṣyasi
śape 'haṃ kṛṣṇacaraṇair iṣṭāpūrtena caiva ha
yadi tvāṃ sasutaṃ pāpaṃ na hanyāṃ yudhi roṣitaḥ
pravṛttau śarasaṃpātaṃ kartuṃ puruṣasattamau
śakuniś ca susaṃkruddhaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
sāgraṃ śatasahasraṃ tu hayānāṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
somadattaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ samantāt paryarakṣata
rakṣyamāṇaś ca balibhiś chādayām āsa sātyakim
taṃ chādyamānaṃ viśikhair dṛṣṭvā saṃnataparvabhiḥ
dhṛṣṭadyumno 'bhyayāt kruddhaḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ camūm
caṇḍavātābhisṛṣṭānām udadhīnām iva svanaḥ
taṃ vimūḍhaṃ samālakṣya sārathis tvarayānvitaḥ
apovāha raṇād vīraṃ somadattaṃ mahāratham
taṃ visaṃjñaṃ samālokya yuyudhānaśarārditam
kārṣṇāyasamayaṃ ghoram ṛkṣacarmāvṛtaṃ mahat
vikṣiptam aṣṭacakreṇa vivṛtākṣeṇa kūjatā
dhvajenocchritatuṇḍena gṛdhrarājena rājatā
lohitārdrapatākaṃ tam antramālāvibhūṣitam
aṣṭacakrasamāyuktam āsthāya vipulaṃ ratham
śūlamudgaradhāriṇyā śailapādapahastayā
rakṣasāṃ ghorarūpāṇām akṣauhiṇyā samāvṛtaḥ
tam udyatamahācāpaṃ niśāmya vyathitā nṛpāḥ
vāyunā kṣobhitāvartā gaṅgevordhvataraṅgiṇī
ghaṭotkacaprayuktena siṃhanādena bhīṣitāḥ
prasusruvur gajā mūtraṃ vivyathuś ca narā bhṛśam
tato 'śmavṛṣṭir atyartham āsīt tatra samantataḥ
saṃdhyākālādhikabalaiḥ pramuktā rākṣasaiḥ kṣitau
āyasāni ca cakrāṇi bhuśuṇḍyaḥ prāsatomarāḥ
patanty aviralāḥ śūlāḥ śataghnyaḥ paṭṭiśās tathā
tad ugram atiraudraṃ ca dṛṣṭvā yuddhaṃ narādhipāḥ
tanayās tava karṇaś ca vyathitāḥ prādravan diśaḥ
nihatāyāṃ tu māyāyām amarṣī sa ghaṭotkacaḥ
visasarja śarān ghorāṃs te 'śvatthāmānam āviśan
bhujagā iva vegena valmīkaṃ krodhamūrchitāḥ
te śarā rudhirābhyaktā bhittvā śāradvatīsutam
viviśur dharaṇīṃ śīghrā rukmapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥ
aśvatthāmā tu saṃkruddho laghuhastaḥ pratāpavān
cakraṃ śatasahasrāram agṛhṇād vyathito bhṛśam
kṣurāntaṃ bālasūryābhaṃ maṇivajravibhūṣitam
vegena mahatā gacchad vikṣiptaṃ drauṇinā śaraiḥ
ghaṭotkacas tatas tūrṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakraṃ nipātitam
drauṇiṃ prācchādayad bāṇaiḥ svarbhānur iva bhāskaram
ghaṭotkacasutaḥ śrīmān bhinnāñjanacayopamaḥ
rurodha drauṇim āyāntaṃ prabhañjanam ivādrirāṭ
pautreṇa bhīmasenasya śaraiḥ so 'ñjanaparvaṇā
dhvajam ekena bāṇena cicchedāñjanaparvaṇaḥ
dvābhyāṃ tu rathayantāraṃ tribhiś cāsya triveṇukam
gadā hemāṅgadā rājaṃs tūrṇaṃ haiḍimbasūnunā
bhrāmyotkṣiptā śaraiḥ sāpi drauṇinābhyāhatāpatat
vavarṣāñjanaparvā sa drumavarṣaṃ nabhastalāt
tato māyādharaṃ drauṇir ghaṭotkacasutaṃ divi
mārgaṇair abhivivyādha ghanaṃ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥ
mahīdhara ivātyuccaḥ śrīmān añjanaparvataḥ
tam ayasmayavarmāṇaṃ drauṇir bhīmātmajātmajam
jaghānāñjanaparvāṇaṃ maheśvara ivāndhakam
atha dṛṣṭvā hataṃ putram aśvatthāmnā mahābalam
drauṇeḥ sakāśam abhyetya roṣāt pracalitāṅgadaḥ
prāha vākyam asaṃbhrānto vīraṃ śāradvatīsutam
dahantaṃ pāṇḍavānīkaṃ vanam agnim ivoddhatam
tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi
aśvatthāmovāca
kiṃ tu roṣānvito jantur hanyād ātmānam apy uta
saṃjaya uvāca
śrutvaitat krodhatāmrākṣaḥ putraśokasamanvitaḥ
aśvatthāmānam āyasto bhaimasenir abhāṣata
bhīmāt khalv aham utpannaḥ kurūṇāṃ vipule kule
pāṇḍavānām ahaṃ putraḥ samareṣv anivartinām
rakṣasām adhirājo 'haṃ daśagrīvasamo bale
tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi
yuddhaśraddhām ahaṃ te 'dya vineṣyāmi raṇājire
ity uktvā roṣatāmrākṣo rākṣasaḥ sumahābalaḥ
rathākṣamātrair iṣubhir abhyavarṣad ghaṭotkacaḥ
rathinām ṛṣabhaṃ drauṇiṃ dhārābhir iva toyadaḥ
śaravṛṣṭiṃ śarair drauṇir aprāptāṃ tāṃ vyaśātayat
tato 'ntarikṣe bāṇānāṃ saṃgrāmo 'nya ivābhavat
athāstrasaṃgharṣakṛtair visphuliṅgaiḥ samābabhau
niśāmya nihatāṃ māyāṃ drauṇinā raṇamāninā
ghaṭotkacas tato māyāṃ sasarjāntarhitaḥ punaḥ
śūlaprāsāsimusalajalaprasravaṇo mahān
tam añjanacayaprakhyaṃ drauṇir dṛṣṭvā mahīdharam
sa tenāstreṇa śailendraḥ kṣiptaḥ kṣipram anaśyata
tataḥ sa toyado bhūtvā nīlaḥ sendrāyudho divi
aśmavṛṣṭibhir atyugro drauṇim ācchādayad raṇe
sa mārgaṇagaṇair drauṇir diśaḥ pracchādya sarvataḥ
śataṃ rathasahasrāṇāṃ jaghāna dvipadāṃ varaḥ
sa dṛṣṭvā punar āyāntaṃ rathenāyatakārmukam
ghaṭotkacam asaṃbhrāntaṃ rākṣasair bahubhir vṛtam
siṃhaśārdūlasadṛśair mattadviradavikramaiḥ
vivṛtāsyaśirogrīvair haiḍimbānucaraiḥ saha
nānāśastradharair vīrair nānākavacabhūṣaṇaiḥ
viṣaṇṇam abhisaṃprekṣya putraṃ te drauṇir abravīt
tiṣṭha duryodhanādya tvaṃ na kāryaḥ saṃbhramas tvayā
nihaniṣyāmy amitrāṃs te na tavāsti parājayaḥ
satyaṃ te pratijānāmi paryāśvāsaya vāhinīm
saṃjaya uvāca
vṛtaḥ śatasahasreṇa rathānāṃ raṇaśobhinām
ṣaṣṭyā gajasahasraiś ca prayāhi tvaṃ dhanaṃjayam
karṇaś ca vṛṣasenaś ca kṛpo nīlas tathaiva ca
udīcyāḥ kṛtavarmā ca purumitraḥ śrutārpaṇaḥ
duḥśāsano nikumbhaś ca kuṇḍabhedī urukramaḥ
puraṃjayo dṛḍharathaḥ patākī hemapaṅkajaḥ
śalyāruṇīndrasenāś ca saṃjayo vijayo jayaḥ
kamalākṣaḥ puruḥ krāthī jayavarmā sudarśanaḥ
ete tvām anuyāsyanti pattīnām ayutāni ṣaṭ
dāritān drauṇinā bāṇair bhṛśaṃ vikṣatavigrahān
piprīṣus te sutān rājan didhakṣuś caiva pāṇḍavān
vibhāvaryāṃ sutumulaṃ śakraprahrādayor iva
jaghānorasi saṃkruddho viṣāgnipratimair dṛḍhaiḥ
sa tair abhyāhato gāḍhaṃ śarair bhīmasuteritaiḥ
bhūyaś cāñjalikenāsya mārgaṇena mahāprabham
drauṇihastasthitaṃ cāpaṃ cicchedāśu ghaṭotkacaḥ
vavarṣa viśikhāṃs tīkṣṇān vāridhārā ivāmbudaḥ
tataḥ śāradvatīputraḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata
suvarṇapuṅkhāñ śatrughnān khacarān khacarān prati
tadbāṇair arditaṃ yūthaṃ rakṣasāṃ pīnavakṣasām
siṃhair iva babhau mattaṃ gajānām ākulaṃ kulam
vidhamya rākṣasān bāṇaiḥ sāśvasūtarathān vibhuḥ
dadāha bhagavān vahnir bhūtānīva yugakṣaye
sa dagdhvākṣauhiṇīṃ bāṇair nairṛtān ruruce bhṛśam
rarāja jayatāṃ śreṣṭho droṇaputras tavāhitān
teṣu rājasahasreṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu bhārata
nainaṃ nirīkṣituṃ kaś cic chaknoti drauṇim āhave
ṛte ghaṭotkacād vīrād rākṣasendrān mahābalāt
sa cikṣepa tataḥ kruddho droṇaputrāya rākṣasaḥ
aṣṭacakrāṃ mahāraudrām aśanīṃ rudranirmitām
sāśvasūtadhvajaṃ vāhaṃ bhasma kṛtvā mahāprabhā
viveśa vasudhāṃ bhittvā sāśanir bhṛśadāruṇā
drauṇes tat karma dṛṣṭvā tu sarvabhūtāny apūjayan
yad avaplutya jagrāha ghorāṃ śaṃkaranirmitām
mumoca niśitān bāṇān punar drauṇer mahorasi
dhṛṣṭadyumno 'py asaṃbhrānto mumocāśīviṣopamān
suvarṇapuṅkhān viśikhān droṇaputrasya vakṣasi
tato mumoca nārācān drauṇis tābhyāṃ sahasraśaḥ
atitīvram abhūd yuddhaṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
yodhānāṃ prītijananaṃ drauṇeś ca bharatarṣabha
ṣaḍbhir vājisahasraiś ca bhīmas taṃ deśam āvrajat
tato bhīmātmajaṃ rakṣo dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca sānugam
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa sāśvasūtarathadvipām
akṣauhiṇīṃ rākṣasānāṃ śitair bāṇair aśātayat
miṣato bhīmasenasya haiḍimbeḥ pārṣatasya ca
pragāḍham añjogatibhir nārācair abhitāḍitāḥ
nipetur dviradā bhūmau dviśṛṅgā iva parvatāḥ
rarāja vasudhā kīrṇā visarpadbhir ivoragaiḥ
kṣiptaiḥ kāñcanadaṇḍaiś ca nṛpacchatraiḥ kṣitir babhau
dyaur ivoditacandrārkā grahākīrṇā yugakṣaye
pravṛddhadhvajamaṇḍūkāṃ bherīvistīrṇakacchapām
chatrahaṃsāvalījuṣṭāṃ phenacāmaramālinīm
kaṅkagṛdhramahāgrāhāṃ naikāyudhajhaṣākulām
rathakṣiptamahāvaprāṃ patākāruciradrumām
śaramīnāṃ mahāraudrāṃ prāsaśaktyugraḍuṇḍubhām
majjāmāṃsamahāpaṅkāṃ kabandhāvarjitoḍupām
keśaśaivalakalmāṣāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ kaśmalāvahām
nāgendrahayayodhānāṃ śarīravyayasaṃbhavām
śoṇitaughamahāvegāṃ drauṇiḥ prāvartayan nadīm
yodhārtaravanirghoṣāṃ kṣatajormisamākulām
nihatya rākṣasān bāṇair drauṇir haiḍimbam ārdayat
punar apy atisaṃkruddhaḥ savṛkodarapārṣatān
sa nārācagaṇaiḥ pārthān drauṇir viddhvā mahābalaḥ
punaḥ śrutaṃjayaṃ nāma surathasyānujaṃ raṇe
balānīkaṃ jayānīkaṃ jayāśvaṃ cābhijaghnivān
tribhiś cānyaiḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ supuṅkhai rukmamālinam
śatruṃjayaṃ ca balinaṃ śakralokaṃ nināya ha
jaghāna sa pṛṣadhraṃ ca candradevaṃ ca māninam
kuntibhojasutāṃś cājau daśabhir daśa jaghnivān
aśvatthāmā susaṃkruddhaḥ saṃdhāyogram ajihmagam
mumocākarṇapūrṇena dhanuṣā śaram uttamam
yamadaṇḍopamaṃ ghoram uddiśyāśu ghaṭotkacam
sa bhittvā hṛdayaṃ tasya rākṣasasya mahāśaraḥ
viveśa vasudhāṃ śīghraṃ sapuṅkhaḥ pṛthivīpate
taṃ hataṃ patitaṃ jñātvā dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥ
drauṇeḥ sakāśād rājendra apaninye rathāntaram
tathā parāṅmukharathaṃ sainyaṃ yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ nṛpa
taṃ siddhagandharvapiśācasaṃghā nāgāḥ suparṇāḥ pitaro vayāṃsi
rakṣogaṇā bhūtagaṇāś ca drauṇim apūjayann apsarasaḥ surāś ca
saṃjaya uvāca
drupadasyātmajān dṛṣṭvā kuntibhojasutāṃs tathā
droṇaputreṇa nihatān rākṣasāṃś ca sahasraśaḥ
yudhiṣṭhiro bhīmaseno dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
somadattaḥ punaḥ kurddho dṛṣṭvā sātyakim āhave
mahatā śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa sarvataḥ
tvadīyānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca ghoraṃ vijayakāṅkṣiṇām
vṛddham ṛddhaṃ guṇaiḥ sarvair yayātim iva nāhuṣam
vivyādha daśabhis tīkṣṇaiḥ śarair vajranipātibhiḥ
sātyakiś cāgnisaṃkāśaṃ mumoca śaram uttamam
visṛjañ śaravarṣāṇi kālavarṣīva toyadaḥ
bhīmo 'tha sātvatasyārthe bāhlīkaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
pīḍayan vai mahātmānaṃ vivyādha raṇamūrdhani
prātipīyas tu saṃkruddhaḥ śaktiṃ bhīmasya vakṣasi
nicakhāna mahābāhuḥ puraṃdara ivāśanim
sā pāṇḍavena prahitā bāhlīkasya śiro 'harat
sa papāta hataḥ pṛthvyāṃ vajrāhata ivādrirāṭ
putrās te 'bhyardayan bhīmaṃ daśa dāśaratheḥ samāḥ
nārācair daśabhir bhīmas tān nihatya tavātmajān
karṇasya dayitaṃ putraṃ vṛṣasenam avākirat
tato vṛṣaratho nāma bhrātā karṇasya viśrutaḥ
jaghāna bhīmaṃ nārācais tam apy abhyavadhīd balī
tataḥ sapta rathān vīraḥ syālānāṃ tava bhārata
śakuner bhrātaro vīrā gajākṣaḥ śarabho vibhuḥ
abhidrutya śarais tīkṣṇair bhīmasenam atāḍayan
sa tudyamāno nārācair vṛṣṭivegair ivarṣabhaḥ
jaghāna pañcabhir bāṇaiḥ pañcaivātibalo rathān
tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān vīrān vicelur nṛpasattamāḥ
tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kruddhas tavānīkam aśātayat
miṣataḥ kumbhayoneś ca putrāṇāṃ ca tavānagha
ambaṣṭhān mālavāñ śūrāṃs trigartān saśibīn api
prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya gaṇān yuddhe yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
abhīṣāhāñ śūrasenān bāhlīkān savasātikān
nikṛtya pṛthivīṃ rājā cakre śoṇitakardamām
yaudheyāraṭṭarājanyamadrakāṇāṃ gaṇān yudhi
prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya śūrān bāṇair yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdo yudhiṣṭhirarathaṃ prati
sainyāni drāvayantaṃ taṃ droṇo dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiram
vāruṇaṃ yāmyam āgneyaṃ tvāṣṭraṃ sāvitram eva ca
cikṣepa paramakruddho jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍunandanam
kṣiptāni kṣipyamāṇāni tāni cāstrāṇi dharmajaḥ
satyāṃ cikīrṣamāṇas tu pratijñāṃ kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ
prāduścakre 'stram aindraṃ vai prājāpatyaṃ ca bhārata
patiḥ kurūṇāṃ gajasiṃhagāmī viśālavakṣāḥ pṛthulohitākṣaḥ
tato nājñāsiṣaṃ kiṃ cid ghoreṇa tamasāvṛte
sarvabhūtāni ca paraṃ trāsaṃ jagmur mahīpate
brahmāstram udyataṃ dṛṣṭvā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
vyadhamad roṣatāmrākṣo vāyavyāstreṇa bhārata
te hanyamānā droṇena pāñcālāḥ prādravan bhayāt
tataḥ kirīṭī bhīmaś ca sahasā saṃnyavartatām
mahadbhyāṃ rathavaṃśābhyāṃ parigṛhya balaṃ tava
bībhatsur dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvam uttaraṃ tu vṛkodaraḥ
bhāradvājaṃ śaraughābhyāṃ mahadbhyām abhyavarṣatām
tau tadā sṛñjayāś caiva pāñcālāś ca mahaujasaḥ
tataḥ sā bhāratī senā vadhyamānā kirīṭinā
droṇena vāryamāṇās te svayaṃ tava sutena ca
nāśakyanta mahārāja yodhā vārayituṃ tadā
saṃjaya uvāca
udīryamāṇaṃ tad dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam
aviṣahyaṃ ca manvānaḥ karṇaṃ duryodhano 'bravīt
ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāpto mitrāṇāṃ mitravatsala
pāñcālair matsyakaikeyaiḥ pāṇḍavaiś ca mahārathaiḥ
ete nadanti saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavā jitakāśinaḥ
śakropamāś ca bahavaḥ pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajāḥ
karṇa uvāca
paritrātum iha prāpto yadi pārthaṃ puraṃdaraḥ
tam apy āśu parājitya tato hantāsmi pāṇḍavam
satyaṃ te pratijānāmi samāśvasihi bhārata
hantāsmi pāṇḍutanayān pāñcālāṃś ca samāgatān
jayaṃ te pratijānāmi vāsavasyeva pāvakiḥ
priyaṃ tava mayā kāryam iti jīvāmi pārthiva
sarveṣām eva pārthānāṃ phalguno balavattaraḥ
tasyāmoghāṃ vimokṣyāmi śaktiṃ śakravinirmitām
tava vaśyā bhaviṣyanti vanaṃ yāsyanti vā punaḥ
mayi jīvati kauravya viṣādaṃ mā kṛthāḥ kva cit
ahaṃ jeṣyāmi samare sahitān sarvapāṇḍavān
pāñcālān kekayāṃś caiva vṛṣṇīṃś cāpi samāgatān
bāṇaughaiḥ śakalīkṛtya tava dāsyāmi medinīm
saṃjaya uvāca
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ karṇaṃ tu kṛpaḥ śāradvato 'bravīt
smayann iva mahābāhuḥ sūtaputram idaṃ vacaḥ
śobhanaṃ śobhanaṃ karṇa sanāthaḥ kurupuṃgavaḥ
samāgamaḥ pāṇḍusutair dṛṣṭas te bahuśo yudhi
sarvatra nirjitaś cāsi pāṇḍavaiḥ sūtanandana
hriyamāṇe tadā karṇa gandharvair dhṛtarāṣṭraje
virāṭanagare cāpi sametāḥ sarvakauravāḥ
katham utsahase jetuṃ sakṛṣṇān sarvapāṇḍavān
garjitvā sūtaputra tvaṃ śāradābhram ivājalam
niṣphalo dṛśyase karṇa tac ca rājā na budhyate
tāvad garjasi rādheya yāvat pārthaṃ na paśyasi
purā pārthaṃ hi te dṛṣṭvā durlabhaṃ garjitaṃ bhavet
tvam anāsādya tān bāṇān phalgunasya vigarjasi
bāhubhiḥ kṣatriyāḥ śūrā vāgbhiḥ śūrā dvijātayaḥ
dhanuṣā phalgunaḥ śūraḥ karṇaḥ śūro manorathaiḥ
evaṃ paruṣitas tena tadā śāradvatena saḥ
karṇaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpaṃ vākyam athābravīt
śūrā garjanti satataṃ prāvṛṣīva balāhakāḥ
phalaṃ cāśu prayacchanti bījam uptam ṛtāv iva
doṣam atra na paśyāmi śūrāṇāṃ raṇamūrdhani
tat tad vikatthamānānāṃ bhāraṃ codvahatāṃ mṛdhe
yaṃ bhāraṃ puruṣo voḍhuṃ manasā hi vyavasyati
vṛthā śūrā na garjanti sajalā iva toyadāḥ
sāmarthyam ātmano jñātvā tato garjanti paṇḍitāḥ
so 'ham adya raṇe yattaḥ sahitau kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
hatvā pāṇḍusutān ājau sahakṛṣṇān sasātvatān
duryodhanāya dāsyāmi pṛthivīṃ hatakaṇṭakām
kṛpa uvāca
yadā kṣipasi vai kṛṣṇau dharmarājaṃ ca pāṇḍavam
devagandharvayakṣāṇāṃ manuṣyoragarakṣasām
daṃśitānām api raṇe ajeyau kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
nityaṃ dharmarataś caiva kṛtāstraś ca viśeṣataḥ
dhṛtimāṃś ca kṛtajñaś ca dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
bhrātaraś cāsya balinaḥ sarvāstreṣu kṛtaśramāḥ
guruvṛttiratāḥ prājñā dharmanityā yaśasvinaḥ
saṃbandhinaś cendravīryāḥ svanuraktāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca daurmukhir janamejayaḥ
yeṣām arthāya saṃyatto matsyarājaḥ sahānugaḥ
śatānīkaḥ sudaśanaḥ śrutānīkaḥ śrutadhvajaḥ
balānīko jayānīko jayāśvo rathavāhanaḥ
candrodayaḥ kāmaratho virāṭabhrātaraḥ śubhāḥ
yamau ca draupadeyāś ca rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
yeṣām arthāya yudhyante na teṣāṃ vidyate kṣayaḥ
sayakṣarākṣasagaṇaṃ sabhūtabhujagadvipam
niḥśeṣam astravīryeṇa kuryātāṃ bhīmaphalgunau
yudhiṣṭhiraś ca pṛthivīṃ nirdahed ghoracakṣuṣā
aprameyabalaḥ śaurir yeṣām arthe ca daṃśitaḥ
saṃjaya uvāca
abravīc ca tadā karṇo guruṃ śāradvataṃ kṛpam
satyam uktaṃ tvayā brahman pāṇḍavān prati yad vacaḥ
ete cānye ca bahavo guṇāḥ pāṇḍusuteṣu vai
ajayyāś ca raṇe pārthā devair api savāsavaiḥ
tathāpi pārthāñ jeṣyāmi śaktyā vāsavadattayā
mamāpy amoghā datteyaṃ śaktiḥ śakreṇa vai dvija
etayā nihaniṣyāmi savyasācinam āhave
hate tu pāṇḍave kṛṣṇo bhrātaraś cāsya sodarāḥ
anarjunā na śakṣyanti mahīṃ bhoktuṃ kathaṃ cana
teṣu naṣṭeṣu sarveṣu pṛthivīyaṃ sasāgarā
sunītair iha sarvārthāḥ sidhyante nātra saṃśayaḥ
tvaṃ tu vṛddhaś ca vipraś ca aśaktaś cāpi saṃyuge
kṛtasnehaś ca pārtheṣu mohān mām avamanyase
yac cāpi pāṇḍavān vipra stotum icchasi saṃyuge
atrāpi śṛṇu me vākyaṃ yathāvad gadato dvija
duḥśāsano vṛṣaseno madrarājas tvam eva ca
somadattaś ca bhūriś ca tathā drauṇir viviṃśatiḥ
tiṣṭheyur daṃśitā yatra sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
śūrāś ca hi kṛtāstrāś ca balinaḥ svargalipsavaḥ
ete sthāsyanti saṃgrāme pāṇḍavānāṃ vadhārthinaḥ
jayam ākāṅkṣamāṇā hi kauraveyasya daṃśitāḥ
yatra bhīṣmo mahābāhuḥ śete śaraśatācitaḥ
bhūriśravā jayaś caiva jalasaṃdhaḥ sudakṣiṇaḥ
śalaś ca rathināṃ śreṣṭho bhagadattaś ca vīryavān
nihatāḥ samare śūrāḥ pāṇḍavair balavattarāḥ
yāṃś ca tān stauṣi satataṃ duryodhanaripūn dvija
teṣām api hatāḥ śūrāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
kṣīyante sarvasainyāni kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
prabhāvaṃ nātra paśyāmi pāṇḍavānāṃ kathaṃ cana
yatiṣye 'haṃ yathāśakti yoddhuṃ taiḥ saha saṃyuge
saṃjaya uvāca
tathā paruṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtaputreṇa mātulam
aśvatthāmovāca
karṇa paśya sudurbuddhe tiṣṭhedānīṃ narādhama
